## Source Text: unaltered below
##

LUK 1:1 Waliha Teofiile, bantu banene bachihangaanire kuyandika emyaazi ya byooshi byagerere ahagarhi keerhu.
LUK 1:2 Abayandikaga, babibalire nk'oku rhwabalirwaga n'abalibibwene ko gurhenga oku ntangiriro, banahinduka bakozi b'eChinwa cha Nnamahanga.
LUK 1:3 Nchimala gushonda n'okubaza kw'eyi myaazi yooshi, byansimiisize naani nkubalire yo gurhenga oku ntangiriro ya yo. Bobunoola waliha Teofiile nkuyandikiire yo bwinjabwinja.
LUK 1:4 Njirire ntyo y'omenya okuli kw'enyigirizo wayankiriire.
LUK 1:5 Amango Heroode aliiri mwami w'eYudeeya, haliiri mudaahwa muguma oyirikwa Zakariya, muguma w'omu badaahwa b'echigusho cha Abiya. Mukaage aliiri muguma w'omu banyere ba Haruuni, ayirikwaga Luzabeeti.
LUK 1:6 Oku bali babiri balikwaneene embere za Nnamahanga. Babaaga bakenga bwinja amarhegeko mooshi ma Nnaweerhu n'okujira nk'oku aderhere.
LUK 1:7 Aliko, nta mwana baligwerhe, kwenge Luzabeeti aliiri ngumba na kandi eyi booshi babaaga bakola bashaaja.
LUK 1:8 Lusiku luguma, Zakariya aliiri akola akaasi kaage k'obudaahwa embere za Nnamahanga, kwenge chaali gihe ch'echigusho chaage.
LUK 1:9 Gukulikirana n'emicho y'obudaahwa, alondoolwa kuja omu Nju ya Nnaweerhu gusireeza obubaani.
LUK 1:10 Amango Zakariya aliiri gusireeza obubaani, echigusho ch'abemeezi baliiri embuga omu masaala.
LUK 1:11 Malahika wa Nnaweerhu amuhulukira, ayimanga emalyo w'entuuliro y'obubaani.
LUK 1:12 Zakariya abeere amubona, ashalama n'okuyuubaha bweneene.
LUK 1:13 Malahika amubwira ntya: «Zakariya, orhayuubahaga, kwenge Nnamahanga ayunviirhe esaala lyawe, na mukaawe Luzabeeti akuburhira omwana w'obuzaana. Nj'omuhe eziino lya Yohaana.
LUK 1:14 Nji wagwarha obusiime n'omwishingo. N'abantu banene nji bamogera okuburhwa kwage.
LUK 1:15 Kwenge nj'aba mukulu embere za Nnaweerhu. Arhakanywa divaayi changwa amaavu makalihire. Gurhengera omu nda ya nyina, nj'aba ey'ayunjwizwe Muuka-Mutagatiifu.
LUK 1:16 Nj'agalula aBaisraheeli banene emwa Nnaweerhu, Nnamahanga waabo.
LUK 1:17 Nj'agenda embere za Nnaweerhu haguma n'omurhima n'obuhashe bwa Eliya, y'agalula haguma abaana n'abazeere baabo. Nj'ahindamula abagome yi bagwarha obwenge nk'abakwaneene. Ntyo, arheganyiziza Nnaweerhu olubaga lurheganyizwe bwinja.»
LUK 1:18 Zakariya abaza malahika ntya: «Gichi nji charhuma naamenya oku ebyoola biri by'okuli? Nyoono nkola ndi mushaaja na mukaani akola mugeekulu.»
LUK 1:19 Malahika amushubiza ntya: «Nyoono nye Gabriyeeri, nyimanga embere za Nnamahanga, ntumirwe gukubwira n'ogukubalira ogu mwazi mwinja.
LUK 1:20 Aliko yunva, waaba nyamugama. Orhakaderha kugera olusiku eyi myaazi nji yaaba okwenge orhayemereere eyi myaazi yaani, nji yaaba omu mango maayo.»
LUK 1:21 Mw'ebyo bishanji olo lubaga lwaliiri kulinga Zakariya lwasoomerwa okubona alegamire omu Nju ya Nnamahanga.
LUK 1:22 Abeere ahuluka, arhachigalaga kuganiira nabo. Aliiri kubasimira n'ebishushanyo, ayoorha nyamugama. Baava bamenya oku abonekeerwe omu Nju ya Nnamahanga.
LUK 1:23 Esiku za Zakariya z'ogukola zabeere zaahwa, agaluka emwage.
LUK 1:24 Enyuma w'ezo siku, mukaage Luzabeeti aheeka obukule. Amala myeezi erhaano burhahuluka n'okuderha ntya:
LUK 1:25 «Tala oku Nnaweerhu anjiriire: asimiisizwe kunkuula ko ehyagendaga hyankoza eshoni ahagarhi k'abantu.»
LUK 1:26 Obukule bwa Luzabeeti bwabeere buli bwa myeezi ndarhu, malahika Gabriyeeri arhumwa na Nnamahanga omu gishagala ch'eGalilaaya chiyirikwa Nazareeti.
LUK 1:27 Amurhuma oku munyere orhazimenya abalume. Oyo munyere ali ashambaazizwe n'omurhabana oyirikwa Yozefu w'omu mulala gwa mwami Daawudi. Eziino ly'oyo munyere lyaliiri Mariya.
LUK 1:28 Malahika abeere aja omu mwabo oyo munyere, amubwira ntya: «Nkulamwise, obe n'omwishingo, w'eyunjwire n'omugisho, bulaala Nnaweerhu ali haguma naawe.»
LUK 1:29 Mariya abeere ayunva echo chinwa, chamushalamya. Achiibaza bichi okulamuswa ntyo kuderhere.
LUK 1:30 Malahika amubwira ntya: «Mariya, orhayuubahaga kwenge wabwene omugisho embere za Nnamahanga.
LUK 1:31 Tala, waaba bukule. Waburha omuzaana n'eziino lyaage wamuyirika Yeesu.
LUK 1:32 Nj'aba mukulu na nj'ahamagalwa Mugala wa Nnamahanga w'Elugulu Bweneene. Nnaweerhu Nnamahanga nj'amuha entebe y'obwami bw'eshekuliza Daawudi.
LUK 1:33 Nj'arhegeka enju ya Yakobo esiku n'amango n'obwime bwage burhagahwa.»
LUK 1:34 Mariya abaza malahika ntya: «Gurhe ebiila nji byagalikana na nta mulume nyinji?»
LUK 1:35 Malahika amushubiza ntya: «Muuka-Mutagatiifu nj'akuyandagalira ko n'obuhashe bwa Nnamahanga w'Elugulu Bweneene nji bwagushukulira n'egichuuchu chaabo. Chi nji charhuma n'omwana waaburhwa nj'aba mutagatiifu; nj'ahamagalwa Mugala wa Nnamahanga.
LUK 1:36 Tala oku na Luzabeeti w'omu mulala gwawe, naye ali bukule b'omwana w'obuzaana omu bugeekulu bwage. Ola wayirikwaga ngumba, mwezi gwa ndarhu guno ali bukule.
LUK 1:37 Kwenge ntaacho girhakagalika emwa Nnamahanga.»
LUK 1:38 Mariya ava aderha ntya: «Nyoono ndi muja wa Nnaweerhu, byooshi bimbeere nk'oku oderhere.» Ho n'aho malahika amuleka.
LUK 1:39 Omu siku zakulikiraga, Mariya agenda jubaajuba, aja omu gishagala chiguma ch'emisozi omu gihugo ch'eYudeeya.
LUK 1:40 Aja omu nju ya Zakariya, alamusa Luzabeeti.
LUK 1:41 Luzabeeti abeere ayunva endamuso ya Mariya, omwana ashambagarha omu nda yaage. Luzabeeti ayunjuzwa Muuka-Mutagatiifu.
LUK 1:42 Aliika omulenge munene elugulu n'okuderha ntya: «Ogishirwe omu bakazi booshi n'omwana oli omu nda yawe agishirwe.
LUK 1:43 Nyoono ndi nde okuderha mpu nyina wa Nnaweerhu andambagirire?
LUK 1:44 Tala okw'amango nayunvaga omulenge g'okulamusa kwawe omu marhwi maani, omwana oli omu nda yaani amashambagarha n'obushagaluke bunene.
LUK 1:45 Ogishirwe kwenge wayemereere oku Nnaweerhu ajira eby'akulaganyaga.»
LUK 1:46 Mariya ava aderha ntya: «Omurhima gwani gukuuze Nnaweerhu.
LUK 1:47 Na kandi gwayunjwire n'omwishingo elugulu wa Nnamahanga, Muchunguzi waani.
LUK 1:48 Kwenge alolere n'olukogo obwirhondesi b'omuja waage. Gurhengera buno abantu ba ngasi gihe bagenda bampamagala mugishwa.
LUK 1:49 Kwenge Nnamahanga Ogala Byooshi anjiriire ebintu binja binene. Eziino lyaage liri litagatiifu.
LUK 1:50 Ngasi mango ajira obubabale oku bamuyuubaha.
LUK 1:51 Kugerera emisi y'okuboko kwage, ashandeeze abantu b'omurhima gw'erumerume.
LUK 1:52 Akuulire abantu b'emisi oku ntebe zaabo z'obwami, n'okuzamuula abirhondesi.
LUK 1:53 Abaliiri nzara abayunjwize n'ebikulo n'abachire abagalwire maboko moomu.
LUK 1:54 Agwasize omukozi waage Israheeli: arhayibiriraga kuyeerekana obubabale bwage
LUK 1:55 nk'oku alaganyaga bashookuluza beerhu, Abrahaamu n'omulala gwage esiku n'amango.»
LUK 1:56 Mariya abeera haguma na Luzabeeti emyeezi yakagera kw'esharhu. Buzinda agaluka emwabo.
LUK 1:57 Egihe ch'okuburha cha Luzabeeti chagera ho, aburha omwana w'obuzaana.
LUK 1:58 Abatuuranyi na beene baabo Luzabeeti babeere bamenya oku Nnaweerhu amuyerekere obubabale bwage, basiima n'ogushagaluka haguma naye.
LUK 1:59 Hagerere siku munaane aburhire, bayinja gukembuula omwana n'ogushonda kumuyirika eziino ly'eshe Zakariya.
LUK 1:60 Aliko nyina aderha ntya: «Nanga, ayirikwe Yohaana.»
LUK 1:61 Bamubwira ntya: «Oku ntaaye omu mulala gwenyu ogwerhe eri ziino!»
LUK 1:62 Baabaza eshe bugamagama ntya: «Gurhe oshondere omwana waawe ayirikwage?»
LUK 1:63 Zakariya ahema bamuleerhere ehipaho, ayandika ko ntya: «Eziino lyaage ye Yohaana.» Booshi basoomerwa.
LUK 1:64 Ho n'aho obuunu bwage bwabumbuulwa n'olulimi lwage lwashwekuulwa, arhondera kuderha n'ogukuuza Nnamahanga.
LUK 1:65 Abatuuranyi baage booshi bagwarhwa n'obuuba. Eyoola myaazi yooshi yalambagizwa omu misozi yooshi y'egihugo ch'eYudeeya.
LUK 1:66 Booshi bayunvaga ogo mwazi baalema bakengeera n'oguchiibaza ntya omu mirhima yaabo: «Leero oyu mwana nj'aba muntu muchi?» Kwenge okuboko kwa Nnaweerhu kwaliiri haguma naye.
LUK 1:67 Eshe Zakariya ayunjuzwa Muuka-Mutagatiifu, aleeba ntya:
LUK 1:68 «Nnaweerhu agishwe, Nnamahanga w'olubaga lw'eIsraheeli, kwenge ayinjire gurhabaala n'oguchungula olubaga lwage.
LUK 1:69 Arhulerheere omuchunguzi w'obuhashe gurhengera omu mulala g'omukozi waage Daawudi,
LUK 1:70 nk'oku anabiderhaga gurhengera miira kugerera abaleebi baage batagatiifu oku
LUK 1:71 arhushwekuula oku banzi beerhu n'ogurhukuula omu maboko m'abarhushomba booshi.
LUK 1:72 Ayerekeene obubabale bwage oku ba daarha n'okuyibuka egihango chaage gitagatiifu.
LUK 1:73 Nnamahanga ajirire ntyo gukulikiza endahiro alahizizaga shookuluza weerhu Abrahaamu.
LUK 1:74 Eyo ndahiro yali y'ogurhukuula omu maboko m'bashombanyi beerhu, yi rhumukolera buzira buuba,
LUK 1:75 yi rhuba batagatiifu n'abakwaneene omu meesho maage esiku zooshi z'akalamo keerhu.
LUK 1:76 Naawe mwana waani, nji wahamagalwa muleebi wa Nnamahanga w' Elugulu Bweneene, kwenge nji wayinja nka murhumwa wa Nnaweerhu omu gurheganya enjira yaage,
LUK 1:77 yi nj'amenyesa olubaga lwage obuchunguke omu kubabalira ebyaaha byaabo,
LUK 1:78 kugerera obubabale bwa Nnamahanga weerhu. Kugerera obo bubabale, Nnamahanga arhukoleezeza ezuuba gurhengera elugulu,
LUK 1:79 y'akoleezeza abayikeere omu mwizimya n'omu gichuuchu ch'olufu, n'okuyerekeza amagulu meerhu omu njira y'omurhuula.»
LUK 1:80 Oyo mwana agendekera gukula n'okugwarha omurhima guzibuhire. Abeera omu mpinga kugera amango m'oguchiyeerekana oku lubaga lw'eIsraheeli.
LUK 2:1 Mw'amo mango omwami mukulu w'aBarooma oyirikwa Kayizaari Ogisitu aleerha erhegeko liderhere oku abantu booshi baganjwe omu bihugo byooshi by'obwami bwage.
LUK 2:2 Olu luganjo lwambere lwaba amango Kureniyo aliiri murhegesi w'egihugo ch'eSuriya.
LUK 2:3 Abantu booshi bagenda guchiyandikiisa ngasi muguma omu gishagala ch'akavukiiro kaage.
LUK 2:4 Yozefu naye arhenga omu gishagala ch'eNazareeti ch'omu Galilaaya. Achiyeerekeza omu gihugo ch'eYudeeya omu gishagala omwami Daawudi aburhwaga mo chiyirikwa Beteleheemu. Kwenge aliiri w'omu mulala gwa Daawudi.
LUK 2:5 Aja yo guchiyandikiisa haguma na Mariya mushambaaza waage. Na Mariya ey'ali bukule.
LUK 2:6 Oku bali eBeteleheemu, olusiku lwage l'okuburha lwagera ho.
LUK 2:7 Aburha omugala w'efula. Amuyambisa engobi, amulyaamiza omu hikenzi hy'okuliisiza mo ebirhungano, kwenge nta hantu haalichiri ho omu nju y'okuyankirira abahiisi.
LUK 2:8 Mw'echo gihugo mwaliiri abangere bagendaga balaala balanga obuso bwabo omu mashwa.
LUK 2:9 Malahika wa Nnaweerhu ava ababonekera. Obulangashane bwa Nnaweerhu bwabamolekera. Bayuubaha bweneene.
LUK 2:10 Aliko malahika ababwira ntya: «Murhayuubahaga, kwenge mbalerheere oMwazi Mwinja, gwashagalusa bweneene abantu booshi.
LUK 2:11 Omu budufu bwa zeene, oMuchunguzi wenyu aburhirwe omu gishagala cha Daawudi: ye Krisitu, Nnaweerhu.
LUK 2:12 N'echimenyeeso cheechi: mwashimaana enjolyaana eyambiiswe engobi, ey'elyamiizwe omu hikenzi hy'okuliisiza mo ebirhungano.»
LUK 2:13 Ho n'aho, echigusho chinene cha bamalahika gurhenga empingu chabugaana ola malahika, baliiri guharamya Nnamahanga n'okuderha ntya:
LUK 2:14 «Obukuuze bunene emwa Nnamahanga omu mpingu z'elugulu bweneene, n'oku gulu, obuholo omu bantu baage asimiiswa nabo!»
LUK 2:15 Bamalahika babeere babaleka n'okugaluka empingu, abo bangere babwirana ntya: «Boonabuno, rhuje eBeteleheemu kulola ebyabeere yo, ebi Nnaweerhu arhumenyeesize.»
LUK 2:16 Baaja yo jubaajuba. Bashigaana Mariya na Yozefu n'omwana ey'alyaamire omu hikenzi hy'okuliisiza mw'ebirhungano.
LUK 2:17 Babeere baabona enjolyaana, baabala ebi malahika abwiraga bo elugulu w'oyo mwana.
LUK 2:18 Booshi bayunvaga ebi abangere baderhaga basoomerwa bweneene.
LUK 2:19 Mariya yeewe aliiri kubiika ebyo byooshi oku murhima gwage n'ogukengeera bichi biderhere.
LUK 2:20 Abangere nabo bagaluka eyi bali bakuuza Nnamahanga n'okumuharamya oku byooshi bayunvire n'okubona ko nk'oku balibwirirwe.
LUK 2:21 Habeere hagera siku munaane omwana aburhirwe, bamukembuula, bamuyirika Yeesu, ly'eziino malahika ali amuyirikire embere nyina aheeke obukule.
LUK 2:22 Amango esiku zayeneraga z'ogucheesibwa nk'oku eRhegeko lya Muusa lyaaliderhere, Yozefu na Mariya baava bazamuukira eYerusaleema kuyeerekana omwana emwa Nnaweerhu.
LUK 2:23 Bulaala biyandikirwe ntya omu Rhegeko lya Nnaweerhu: «Ngasi mwana w'obuzaana nji waaburhwa w'olubere, arhuulwe emwa Nnaweerhu.»
LUK 2:24 Balikwaneene guhaana entuulo ehemerwe mw'elyo Rhegeko lya Nnaweerhu: «Maguuku mabiri changwa enyunyi ebiri z'entungulu.»
LUK 2:25 Haliiri muntu muguma eYerusaleema oyirikwa Simeooni. Aliiri muntu okwaneene embere za Nnamahanga n'okumukenga. Aliiri kulinga owarhulereza Israheeli, na Muuka-Mutagatiifu aliiri haguma naye.
LUK 2:26 Muuka-Mutagatiifu ali mubwirire oku arhagafiire arhaza kubona Krisitu wa Nnaweerhu.
LUK 2:27 Simeooni ava aja omu Nju ya Nnamahanga eyi ayerekeezwe na Muuka-Mutagatiifu. Amango ababusi ba Yeesu bamuleerhaga kujira eby'eRhegeko lihemere,
LUK 2:28 Simeooni amurhoola omu maboko maage, akuuza Nnamahanga n'okuderha ntya:
LUK 2:29 «Nnaweerhu wajirire nk'oku walaganyaga: okola wakaleka omuja waawe afe n'omurhuula nka okw'echinwa chaawe chiderhere.
LUK 2:30 Kwenge nachibweneere obuchunguke bwawe n'ameesho maani.
LUK 2:31 Obu buchunguke warheganyaga embere za ngasi lubaga,
LUK 2:32 b'obumoleke nji bwakumenyesa oku bapagaani. Na kandi nji bwaba bukuuze bwa Israheeli, lubaga lwawe.»
LUK 2:33 Eshe na nyina wa Yeesu basoomerwa n'ebi Simeooni aliiri kuderha elugulu w'omwana.
LUK 2:34 Simeooni abagisha n'okubwira Mariya nyina wa Yeesu ntya: «Oyu mwana ali ho yi bantu banene barhoge n'abandi bayinamuke omu Israheeli. Nj'aba chimenyeeso charhenga emwa Nnamahanga, banene nji bachilahira.
LUK 2:35 Na ntyo, nj'abishuula enkengeero zibishirwe omu mirhima ya banene. Naawe Mariya, nji wababala bweneene omu murhima gwawe nk'ogwachumirhirwe n'akeere.»
LUK 2:36 Haliiri omuleebi-kazi muguma oyirikwa Haana, mwali wa Fanuweeri, w'omu mulala gwa Haseeri. Oyo Haana abaaga akola mugeekulu wa myaaka minene. Abaaga amalama myaaka mushanvu yonyine n'eba gurhengera ogushabwa kwage, buzinda bwaho eba afa.
LUK 2:37 Alibeerere mushumbakazi, guhika amango ageraga omu myaaka makumi gali munaane n'ene. Abaaga arharhenga omu Nju ya Nnamahanga, aliko ey'anakolera Nnamahanga ezuuba n'obudufu omu guchiibuza kulya n'omu kugenda asaliira.
LUK 2:38 Naye agera ho mw'ebyo bishanji n'okuva ahwanza gusiimiriza Nnamahanga. Booshi baliiri kulingiriza oguchungulwa kwa Yerusaleema, abalira bo elugulu w'oyo mwana.
LUK 2:39 Abazeere ba Yeesu babeere bamala kujira nk'oku eRhegeko lya Nnaweerhu lihemere, bagaluka naye eGalilaaya omu gishagala chaabo ch'eNazareeti.
LUK 2:40 Oyo mwana Yeesu aliiri gukula n'okugwarha emisi. Aliyunjwire n'obwenge bunene, n'omugisho gwa Nnamahanga gwaliiri haguma naye.
LUK 2:41 Ngasi mwaka, abazeere ba Yeesu bagendaga baja eYerusaleema oku lusiku lukulu lwa Paasaka.
LUK 2:42 Yeesu abeere agwarha myaaka ekumi n'ebiri, bazamuukira yo naye gukulikirana n'emicho y'olusiku lukulu.
LUK 2:43 Olusiku lukulu lwa Paasaka lwabeere lwahwa, bafuluka. Aliko omwana Yeesu asigala eYerusaleema. Ababusi baage barhamenyaga chiro.
LUK 2:44 Baliiri gukengeera oku nkabaga Yeesu ali haguma n'abandi bantu baliiri nabo omu lugenzi. Balambagira ezuuba lyooshi. Baja barhondera kumushonda ahagarhi ka beene baabo n'abantu babayinji.
LUK 2:45 Aliko barhamubonaga. Baava bagaluka eYerusaleema eyi bali bamushonda.
LUK 2:46 Buzinda bwa siku esharhu, bamushimaana omu Nju ya Nnamahanga ayikeere ahagarhi k'abigiriza b'eRhegeko lya Nnamahanga. Aliiri kubayunviriza n'okubabaza ebibazo.
LUK 2:47 Booshi baliiri kumuyunviriza basoomererwa obwenge bwage n'ebishubizo aliiri guhaana.
LUK 2:48 Ababusi baage babeere bamubona, baashalama. Nyina amubwira ntya: «Mwana waani, charhumire warhujira ntya? Yisho haguma naani rhwaliiri kugushonda n'obuuba.»
LUK 2:49 Yeesu abashubiza ntya: «Gichi charhumaga mwanshonda? Ka murhamenyere oku nkwaneene kuba omu Nju ya Daarha?»
LUK 2:50 Aliko barhayunvaga ech'aliiri kubabwira.
LUK 2:51 Yeesu achima nabo eNazareeti. Aliiri kubakenga. Nyina aliiri kubiika ebyo binwa byooshi omu murhima gwage.
LUK 2:52 Yeesu aliiri gukula omu bwenge bunene, omu bule n'omu migisho embere za Nnamahanga n'abantu.
LUK 3:1 Omu mwaka gw'ekumi na garhaano g'oburhegesi bw'omwami mukulu w'aBarooma Kayizaari Tiberiyo, Ponsiyo Pilaato aliiri mwimangizi w'egihugo ch'eYudeeya. Na Heroode aliiri mwimangizi w'egihugo ch'eGalilaaya na mwene waabo oyirikwa Firipo omu gihugo ch'eItureya na ech'eTarakoniiti. Lisaniya naye aliiri mwimangizi w'egihugo ch'eHabileeni.
LUK 3:2 Hanaasi na Kayaafa bo baliiri bakulu b'abadaahwa. Mwamo mango, echinwa cha Nnamahanga chahikira Yohaana mugala wa Zakariya omu mpinga.
LUK 3:3 Yohaana agera omu bihugo byooshi byalitureene n'olwinji lw'eYorodaani. Aliiri kuyaamagaza ntya: «Muleke ebyaaha byenyu, mubatiizwe yi Nnamahanga ababalira.»
LUK 3:4 Na ntya byaava byaagera ho eby'omuleebi Isaya ayandikaga omu gitaabu chaage mpu: «Muntu muguma ali ahamagaza omu mpinga: ‹Murheganye enjira ya Nnaweerhu. Mumujirire enjira zilambuukire!
LUK 3:5 Ngasi lubanda nji lwayunjuzwa, ngasi musozi na ngasi hirhondo nji byalambuulwa, ngasi rukumba lw'enjira nji lwagonyoolwa. Enjira zibiihire nji zalambuulwa.
LUK 3:6 Na ngasi muntu nj'abona obuchunguke Nnamahanga ahaana.›»
LUK 3:7 Abantu banene bayinja emwa Yohaana mpu ababatiize. Alema ababwira ntya: «Mwe buuko bw'enjoka, nde wabayigiriize guchilanga oku buhane bwayinjire?
LUK 3:8 Leero, muleme mwayeerekana kugerera ebijiro binja oku mwalekere ebyaaha byenyu. Murhachibwiraga mpu: ‹Abrahaamu ali shookuluza weerhu.› Kwenge mbabwirire oku Nnamahanga agakoleesa ama mabaale n'okumajira baana ba Abrahaamu!
LUK 3:9 Embasha ekola eri hoofu guchiira emirhi oku mizi. Nkaasi murhi gurhayeezeze amalehe menja, gwachiibwa n'ogukabulwa omu muliro.»
LUK 3:10 Abantu baliiri kumubaza ntya: «Gichi rhujaage rhwajira?»
LUK 3:11 Abashubiza ntya: «Ogwerhe simiisi ebiri agwasizwe guhaana nguma okw'orhayigwerhe. Ogwerhe ech'okulya naye ajire ntyo.»
LUK 3:12 Ab'ogufurhiisa amakooli nabo bayinja kubatiizwa. Baabaza Yohaana ntya: «Mwigiriza, bichi rhukwaneene kujira?»
LUK 3:13 Ashubiza bo ntya: «Murhahoreesaga binene kulusha ebi murhegekerwe guhoreesa.»
LUK 3:14 Abasoda nabo baamubaza ntya: «Neerhu, bichi rhukwaneene kujira?» Ashubiza bo ntya: «Murhanyagaga omuntu ehyaage changwa gusidaaka omuntu oku bushaabusha. Aliko musimiiswe n'omukamarho gwenyu.»
LUK 3:15 Olubaga lwaliiri kulingiriza n'obulangaalire, ngasi muguma aliiri gukengeera omu murhima gwage oku nkabaga Yohaana ye Krisitu.
LUK 3:16 Yohaana abwira bo ntya: «Nyoono ndi nababatiiza omu menji; aliko owayinja agwerhe obuhashe kundusha. Ntakwaneene chiro gushwekuula omugozi gw'ebiraato byaage. Yeewe nj'ababatiiza na Muuka-Mutagatiifu, n'omu muliro.
LUK 3:17 Afarhire omu fune zaage engooko y'okuyeera, abiiza echibuga chaage; ahira amahemba olwage lunda n'emyaavu olwage lunda. Nj'agusha amahemba omu nguli yaage, sy'aliko nj'ayoosa emyaavu omu muliro gurhazima chiro n'ehityu.»
LUK 3:18 Yohaana ayigiriza olubaga oMwazi Mwinja omu kubaheereza ezindi nyigirizo zinene z'okubaseeza omurhima.
LUK 3:19 Aliko Yohaana akalihira Heroode, wali yimire omu gihugo ch'eGalilaaya, kwenge aliyingiire Herodiya muka mwene waabo, n'okwenge abaaga ey'akolere ebindi bijiro binene bibiihire.
LUK 3:20 Kw'ebyo byooshi, Heroode ayongeera ko echindi chijiro chibi ch'oguhiriisa Yohaana omu munyororo.
LUK 3:21 Abantu booshi babeere bamala kubatiizwa, Yeesu naye abatiizwa. Olo lusiku, oku Yeesu ali gusaliira, empingu yagichinguula,
LUK 3:22 Muuka-Mutagatiifu amuyandagalira ko omu shusho ly'eguuku. Omulenge gwayunviikana ntya gurhengera empingu: «Oli Mugala waani muzigirwa; nsimiisizwe nawe bweneene.»
LUK 3:23 Amango Yeesu arhonderaga kuyigiriza, aligwerhe emyaaka yakagera ku makumyaasharhu. Abantu baliiri kumurhoola nka mwene Yozefu. Yozefu aliiri Mugala wa Heeli,
LUK 3:24 Heeli aliiri mugala wa Mataati, Mataati aliiri mugala wa Laawi, Laawi aliiri mugala wa Meleki, Meleki aliiri mugala wa Janaayi, Janaayi aliiri mugala wa Yozefu,
LUK 3:25 Yozefu aliiri mugala wa Matatiyaasi, Matatiyaasi aliiri mugala wa Amoosi, Amoosi aliiri mugala wa Nahuumu, Nahuumu aliiri mugala wa Esuuli, Esuuli aliiri mugala wa Nagaayi,
LUK 3:26 Nagaayi aliiri Mugala wa Maati, Maati aliiri mugala wa Matatiyaasi, Matatiyaasi aliiri mugala wa Semeyini, Semeyini aliiri mugala wa Yezeechi, Yezeechi aliiri mugala wa Yooda,
LUK 3:27 Yooda aliiri Mugala wa Yohanaani, Yohanaani aliiri mugala wa Reesa, Reesa aliiri mugala wa Zorobabeeli, Zorobabeeli aliiri mugala wa Shalitiyeeri, Shalitiyeeri aliiri mugala wa Neeri,
LUK 3:28 Neeri aliiri mugala wa Meleechi, Meleechi aliiri mugala wa Aadi, Aadi aliiri mugala wa Gosaame, Gosaame aliiri mugala wa Elimadaame, Elimadaame aliiri mugala wa Ere,
LUK 3:29 Ere aliiri mugala wa Yooshuwa, Yooshuwa aliiri mugala wa Eliyezeeri, Eliyezeeri aliiri mugala wa Yoriime, Yoriime aliiri mugala wa Mataati, Mataati aliiri mugala wa Laawi,
LUK 3:30 Laawi aliiri mugala wa Simeooni, Simeooni aliiri mugala wa Yuuda, Yuuda aliiri mugala wa Yozefu, Yozefu aliiri mugala wa Yonaami, Yonaami aliiri mugala wa Eliyakiimu,
LUK 3:31 Eliyakiimu aliiri mugala wa Meleeya, Meleeya aliiri mugala wa Meena, Meena aliiri mugala wa Mattata, Mattata aliiri mugala wa Nataamu, Nataamu aliiri mugala wa Daawudi,
LUK 3:32 Daawudi aliiri mugala wa Yeese, Yeese aliiri mugala wa Yobeedi, Yobeedi aliiri mugala wa Boazi, Boazi aliiri mugala wa Saala, Saala aliiri mugala wa Nasooni,
LUK 3:33 Nasooni aliiri mugala wa Aminadaabu, Aminadaabu aliiri mugala wa Adimiini, Adimiini aliiri mugala wa Ariini, Ariini aliiri mugala wa Hesiroomi, Hesiroomi aliiri mugala wa Pereesi, Pereesi aliiri mugala wa Yuuda,
LUK 3:34 Yuuda aliiri mugala wa Yakobo, Yakobo aliiri mugala wa Isaka, Isaka aliiri mugala wa Abrahaamu, Abrahaamu aliiri mugala wa Teera, Teera aliiri mugala wa Nahoori,
LUK 3:35 Nahoori aliiri mugala wa Seruugi, Seruugi aliiri mugala wa Reehu, Reehu aliiri mugala wa Peleegi, Peleegi aliiri mugala wa Hebeeri, Hebeeri aliiri mugala wa Sheela,
LUK 3:36 Sheela aliiri mugala wa Kenaani, Kenaani aliiri mugala wa Arapakasaadi, Arapakasaadi aliiri mugala wa Seemu, Seemu aliiri mugala wa Noowa, Noowa aliiri mugala wa Lameeki,
LUK 3:37 Lameeki aliiri mugala wa Matusaleemi, Matusaleemi aliiri mugala wa Henooka, Henooka aliiri mugala wa Yereedi, Yereedi aliiri mugala wa Malaleeli, Malaleeli aliiri mugala wa Kenaani,
LUK 3:38 Kenaani aliiri mugala wa Enoosi, Enoosi aliiri mugala wa Seeti, Seeti aliiri mugala wa Adaamu, Adaamu aliiri mugala wa Nnamahanga.
LUK 4:1 Yeesu arhenga omu lwinji lw'eYorodaani ey'ayunjwizwe Muuka-Mutagatiifu. Aheekwa na Muuka-Mutagatiifu omu mpinga.
LUK 4:2 Omoola mpinga, ageregezwa na Shetaani gihe cha siku makumi mane. Arhalyaaga chintu mw'ezoola siku. Zabeere zaahwa, ayunva enzara.
LUK 4:3 Shetaani aja amubwira ntya: «Akaba oli Mugala wa Nnamahanga, bwira eli baale lihinduke mugati.»
LUK 4:4 Yeesu amushubiza ntya: «Biyandikirwe: ‹Omuntu arhakalama n'omugati gonyine.›»
LUK 4:5 Shetaani ava amuheeka elugulu bweneene, amuyeereka omu gashanji kageeke amaami mooshi m'egulu.
LUK 4:6 Shetaani amubwira ntya: «Nji naguheereza obuhashe booshi n'obukuuze bw'ama maami mooshi. Nahaabirwe ebyoola byooshi. Naani nakabiheereza eyi nshondere.
LUK 4:7 Okamparamya, byooshi byaaba byaawe.»
LUK 4:8 Yeesu amushubiza ntya: «Biyandikirwe: ‹Oharamye Nnaweerhu, Nnamahanga waawe n'okumukolera yenyine.›»
LUK 4:9 Shetaani ashuba kumuheeka eYerusaleema. Amuhira elugulu w'eNju ya Nnamahanga n'okumubwira: «Akaba oli Mugala wa Nnamahanga, chiikabula gurhenga hano kuja eshiishi.
LUK 4:10 Kwenge aMandiko Matagatiifu maderhere ntya: ‹Nnamahanga nj'arhegeka bamalahika baage bakulange.›
LUK 4:11 Na kandi: ‹Baguheeka omu maboko maabo y'okugulu kwawe nji gurhasiirhalaga oku baale.›»
LUK 4:12 Yeesu amushubiza ntya: «aMandiko Matagatiifu maderhere ntya: ‹Orhahira okageregeza Nnaweerhu, Nnamahanga waawe.›»
LUK 4:13 Abeere amala kugeregeza Yeesu omu ngasi kuntu, Shetaani aja hale naye kugera ekindi gihe.
LUK 4:14 Yeesu agaluka eGalilaaya eyi ayunjwire obuhashe bwa Muuka-Mutagatiifu. Emyaazi yaage y'amenyikana mwaho hantu hooshi.
LUK 4:15 Alema ayigiriza omu masinagoogi na ngasi muntu alema amukuuza.
LUK 4:16 Yeesu aja eNazareeti, emunda alemberwaga. Olusiku lw'eSaabato, aja omu sinagoogi nk'oku ali komeere. Ayimanga gusoma aMandiko Matagatiifu.
LUK 4:17 Bamuheereza egitaabu ch'omuleebi Isaya. Azinguula cho n'okuva abona olukere luyandikirwe ntya:
LUK 4:18 «oMuuka gwa Nnaweerhu gundi ko. Kwenge akinshogere mpu ndeme nayigiriza abakene oMwazi Mwinja. Antumire kuyaamagiza ogushwekuulwa kw'abali omu munyororo n'empumi oguhumuulwa ameesho, n'okulikuulwa kw'ababonereerwe,
LUK 4:19 n'okuyaamagaza omwaka Nnaweerhu ayeerekana olukogo lwage.»
LUK 4:20 Yeesu azinga egitaabu, achigalulira omukozi n'okuyikala. Abantu booshi baliiri omu sinagoogi baliiri kumuseeza kw'ameesho.
LUK 4:21 Ava ahwanza kubabwira ntya: «Zeene aMandiko Matagatiifu mwayuusa kuyunva mamayeenera.»
LUK 4:22 Booshi baalema bamudumiiriza n'ogusoomererwa ebinwa binja aliiri kuderha. Baalema baderha ntya: «K'arhali mugala wa Yozefu oyuula?»
LUK 4:23 Yeesu abwira bo ntya: «Okuli, mwambwira oguula mugani: ‹Mufumu, ochifumye wenyine.› Na kandi mwambwira: ‹Rhwayunviirhe ebiwajirire byooshi eGaperinaumu. Jira ebiri nk'ebyo kuno mwenyu nako.›»
LUK 4:24 Ashubi yongeera ntya: «Mbabwirire okuli: nta muleebi oyankirirwa bwinja omu gishagala chaabo
LUK 4:25 Okuli, mbabwirire okw'eIsraheeli haliiri abashumbakazi banene amango ma Eliya. Amo mango envula yamala myaaka esharhu na myeezi ndarhu buzira gurhoga. Enzara nene yabonekana omu gihugo chooshi.
LUK 4:26 Sy'aliko Eliya arharhumwaga emwa muguma wabo, aliko arhumwa emw'omushumbakazi muguma wali lamire eSarepata omu gihugo ch'Sidoona.
LUK 4:27 Haliiri kandi ababenzibenzi banene omu Israheeli amango m'omuleebi Elisha. Na ntaaye omu bo wafumire, aliko oMusuuriya Namaani yenyine.»
LUK 4:28 Booshi baliiri omu sinagoogi babeere bayunva ntyo, bakaliha.
LUK 4:29 Bayimanga, bakuula Yeesu omu gishagala, bamuheeka elugulu w'omusozi gwaliyumbakirwe ko echo gishagala mpu yi bamushunika omu lubanda.
LUK 4:30 Aliko agera ahagarhi kaabo, achigendera.
LUK 4:31 Enyuma z'ebi, Yeesu aja ayandagalira omu gishagala ch'eGaperinaumu ch'omu gihugo ch'eGalilaaya. Olusiku lw'eSaabato lwabeere lwahika, agenda kuyigiriza omu sinagoogi.
LUK 4:32 Abantu basoomererwa bweneene enyigirizo zaage, kwenge aliiri kuderha n'oburhegesi.
LUK 4:33 Omu sinagoogi haliiri omuntu walifarhirwe n'omuzimu. Akankama ntya n'omulenge munene:
LUK 4:34 «Yoo! Yeesu w'eNazareeti, gichi warhushonda ko? K'oyinjire gurhumala? Nkuyinji! Oli Mutagatiifu wa Nnamahanga.»
LUK 4:35 Yeesu akankamira bweneene oyo omuzimu n'okumubwira ntya: «Sira, rhenga m'oyu muntu!» Omuzimu akabula oyo muntu oku budaka ahagarhi k'abantu n'okumurhenga mo buzira kumujira kubi.
LUK 4:36 Abantu booshi basoomerwa n'okubwirana ntya: «Byo bich'ibi? Oyu muntu y'arhegeka n'ogukalihira n'emisi abazimu, nabo banahuluka!»
LUK 4:37 N'emyaazi eyerekeere Yeesu yayandaala mw'echo gihugo chooshi.
LUK 4:38 Yeesu ahuluka omu sinagoogi ayeerekeza emwa Simooni. Nazaala wa Simooni ali libukire n'eshuushira linene. Baahema Yeesu amufumye.
LUK 4:39 Yeesu amuyegeera, akalihira eshuushira, nalyo lyamuleka. Ho n'aho oyo mukazi ayuumuka n'ogurhondera kubakolera.
LUK 4:40 Ezuuba lyabeere lyaazika, abantu baligwerhe abalwala ba ngasi ndwala, baleerhera bo Yeesu. Ahira amaboko ku ngasi muguma n'okubafumya.
LUK 4:41 Abazimu barhenga omu balwala banene eyi bali babweja ntya: «Oli Mugala wa Nnamahanga!» Aliko Yeesu abakalihira n'okubabuza kuderha. Kwenge boowe baliyinji okw'ali Krisitu.
LUK 4:42 Bwabeere bwacha, Yeesu arhenga ahoola, achijiira ahantu harhali bantu. Abantu banene barhondera kumushonda. Babeere bamushimaana, bashonda kumubuza arhabalekaga.
LUK 4:43 Aliko Yeesu abwira bo ntya: «Ngwasize kuyigiriza oMwazi Mwinja g'obwime bwa Nnamahanga omu bindi bishagala nabyo. Kwenge echo chicharhumaga Nnamahanga antuma.»
LUK 4:44 Alema ayigiriza omu sinagoogi z'egihugo ch'eYudeeya.
LUK 5:1 Lusiku luguma, Yeesu aliyimangire ahaburhambi bw'enyanja eyirikwa Genezareeti. Abantu banene balwisa kuja ahaburhambi bwage kuyunviriza eChinwa cha Nnamahanga.
LUK 5:2 Abona maarho mabiri mali emushengo. Abashaana eyi barhengere mo bakola bali gushuka emilaga yaabo.
LUK 5:3 Yeesu ashonera omu bwarho buguma. Bwaliiri bwa Simooni. Yeesu amuhema okw'abushunike hale bugeeke n'emushengo. Yeesu ayikala m'obo bwarho n'ogurhondera guhaana enyigirizo zaage oku bantu.
LUK 5:4 Abeere amala kuderha, abwira Simooni ntya: «Shegera hale, ah'amenji maleehere. Wooyo n'abenyu, muhire emilaga yenyu omu menji, murhege.»
LUK 5:5 Simooni amushubiza ntya: «Mwigiriza, rhwalibukire obudufu booshi, rhwamanahina. Aliko obo wamambwira oku njire ntyo, nahira emilaga omu menji.»
LUK 5:6 Babeere baajira ntyo, bayirha efi zinene bweneene, oku bulyo emilaga yaabo yarhondera guchiibera.
LUK 5:7 Basimira abaabo baliiri omu bwindi bwarho mpu bayinje babagwase. Aboola bayinja. Booshi haguma bayunjuza amo maarho mabiri, oku bulyo maalema mayika omu menji.
LUK 5:8 Simooni Petero abeere abona ebyoola, afukama embere za Yeesu n'okuderha ntya: «Orhanyegeeraga, Nnaweerhu, kwenge nyoono ndi muntu w'ebyaaha!»
LUK 5:9 Simooni n'abaliiri naye, booshi baalisomeerwe ntya elugulu w'efi zinene bayirhaga.
LUK 5:10 Yakobo na Yohaana, bagala ba Zebedayo, baliiri gurhega haguma na Simooni, nabo basoomerwa. Aliko Yeesu abwira Simooni ntya: «Orhayuubahaga: gurhengera zeene waaja waloba abantu.»
LUK 5:11 Baava basiika amaarho maabo emushengo. Baaleka byooshi, bakulikira Yeesu.
LUK 5:12 Amango Yeesu aliiri omu gishagala chiguma ch'omu bishagala by'eGalilaaya, haahulukira omuntu oyunjwire ebibenzi. Abeere abona Yeesu, achikabula embere zaage, amalanga oku budaka n'okumuyinginga ntya: «Nnaweerhu, akaba bigusimiisize, wakancheesa.»
LUK 5:13 Yeesu alambuula okuboko, amuhuma ko n'okuderha ntya: «Binsimiisize, ocheeswe!» Ho n'aho, ebibenzi by'oyo muntu byaafuma.
LUK 5:14 Yeesu amurhegeka ntya: «Nta muntu obwirage ebiila. Aliko oje guchiyeerekana emw'omudaahwa, ohaane entuulo y'ogucheeswa nk'oku Muusa ayirhegekaga. K'okuyeereka abantu booshi oku wafumire.»
LUK 5:15 Aliko emyaazi eyerekeere Yeesu yayandaala hooshi. Abantu banene baalema bachiigusha mpu bamuyunvirize, anabafumye endwala zaabo.
LUK 5:16 Aliko Yeesu alema ayongoloka kuja gusaliira aharhali bantu.
LUK 5:17 Lusiku luguma, Yeesu aliiri kuyigiriza. aBafarisaayo n'abigiriza b'amarhegeko bali bayikeere ahoola, bahulukiraga omu bishagala byooshi by'eGalilaaya, by'eYudeeya n'eYerusaleema. N'obuhashe bwa Nnaweerhu bwaliiri haguma naye y'afumya abalwala.
LUK 5:18 Ho n'aho abantu baguma baagera ho baheekere omuntu ohunzize oku gipoyi. Baliiri gushonda kumuheeka omu nju n'okumurhabika embere za Yeesu.
LUK 5:19 Aliko baabula ngahe bakamugezeza elugulu w'abantu banene. Baava bashona oku nju elugulu n'ogukubuula amatebura, bamuchimiza oku gipoyi ahagarhiigarhi k'echigusho ch'abantu embere za Yeesu.
LUK 5:20 Yeesu abeere abona obwemeezi bw'abo, abwira oyo mulwala ntya: «Mwira waani, ebyaaha byaawe byababaliirwe.»
LUK 5:21 Abigiriza b'amarhegeko n'aBafarisaayo barhondera gukengeera ntya: «Oyu mulume ali nde oli kudukanga Nnamahanga? Nde wakagala kubabalira ebyaaha arhali Nnamahanga yenyine?»
LUK 5:22 Yeesu amenya enkengeero zaabo, ava ababaza ntya: «Chagarhuma mwagwarha enkengeero ziri ntya omu mirhima yenyu?
LUK 5:23 Bichi biyoolohere, akaba okuderha ntya: ‹Ebyaaha byaawe byababaliirwe›, changwa okuderha: ‹Yimanga, olambagire?›
LUK 5:24 Leero nshondere mumenye oku Mwene oMuntu agwerhe obuhashe b'okubabalira ebyaaha omu gulu.» Ava abwira oyo mulwala ohunzize ntya: «Nkubwirire, yimanga, rhoola egipoyi chaawe, ogaluke emwawe!»
LUK 5:25 Ho n'aho oyo muntu ayimanga embere z'abantu booshi, ava arhoola egipoyi chaage aliiri kulyaama ko, n'oguchijiira emwage ey'aheerhe akuuza Nnamahanga.
LUK 5:26 Booshi basoomerwa, bakuuza Nnamahanga. Bayuubaha n'okuderha ntya: «Zeene rhwabwene oku bintu bisomeezwe!»
LUK 5:27 Buzinda bwaho, Yeesu ahuluka, abona omufurhiisa w'amakooli oyirikwa Laawi, ey'ayikeere ahantu bafurhiisiza. Yeesu amubwira ntya: «Nkulikira!»
LUK 5:28 Laawi aleka byooshi, ayimanga n'okumukulikira.
LUK 5:29 Laawi amujirira esheego nene omu mwage. Abafurhiisa b'amakooli banene n'abandi bantu baliiri gusangira meeza maguma nabo.
LUK 5:30 aBafarisaayo n'abigiriza b'amarhegeko balunduma n'okubwira abigirizwa ba Yeesu ntya: «Chagarhuma mwalya n'okunywa haguma n'abafurhiisa b'amakooli n'abanyabyaaha?»
LUK 5:31 Yeesu abashubiza ntya: «Arhali abantu bagumaguma bo bakenera omufumu sy'aliko abalwala.
LUK 5:32 Ntayinjaga guhamagala abakengereere oku bakwaneene sy'aliko abayinji oku bali banyabyaaha yi babileka n'okugalukira Nnamahanga.»
LUK 5:33 aBafarisaayo bamubwira ntya: «Abigirizwa ba Yohaana kuguma n'abeerhu bazigaana guchiibuza kulya banajira n'esaala, aliko ab'emwawe boowe yi bagendeerera kulya n'okunywa.»
LUK 5:34 Yeesu ashubiza bo ntya: «Ka mwakabuza abeera b'omuhya-mulume kulya n'okunywa n'obo omuhya-mulume achiri haguma nabo? Nangwa!
LUK 5:35 Nji hayinja amango banyegwa omuhya mulume, mw'ezo siku nji bachiibuza okulya n'okunywa.»
LUK 5:36 Abwira bo kandi guno mugani: «Ntaaye okuula ehisharhe oku mwenda muhyaahya mpu ahihangire oku mwenda gushaajire. Kwenge owajira ntyo, nj'aba aberere omwenda muhyaahya, n'ehisharhe arhoolere hirhakananiira oku gushaajire.
LUK 5:37 Na ntaaye ohira edivaayi y'omuhyo omu ndaha zishaajire; okwindi, kuli kuderha oku, edivaayi y'omuhyo enabera endaha, yanabirira n'endaha zanaberekera busha.
LUK 5:38 Aliko bihemere guhira edivaayi y'omuhyo omu ndaha zihyaahya.
LUK 5:39 Na nta muntu wanywere oku divaayi y'enchulama wagasiima ey'omuhyo, kwenge baderha oku ey'enchulama y'enyinja.»
LUK 6:1 Lusiku luguma lw'eSaabato, Yeesu n'abigirizwa baage baliiri kulenga omu mashwa m'engano. Abigirizwa baage bayaagula emihuli y'engano, bayivunga omu fune n'okulya embeke.
LUK 6:2 aBafarisaayo baguma bababaza ntya: «Chagarhuma mwajira ebilahiizwe olusiku lw'eSaabato?»
LUK 6:3 Yeesu abashubiza ntya: «Ka murhasomaga ebi Daawudi ajiraga n'abaliiri haguma naye eyi bayunviirhe enzara?
LUK 6:4 Aja omu Nju ya Nnamahanga, arhoola emigati barhuuliraga Nnamahanga. Ayilya ko, ayiha oku baliiri haguma naye, n'obo eRhegeko lyeerhu liyemereere okw'abadaahwa bonyine bagwasize kulya yo.»
LUK 6:5 Kandi Yeesu ababwira ntya: «Mwene oMuntu ye nyina eSaabato.»
LUK 6:6 Olwindi lusiku lw'eSaabato, Yeesu aja omu sinagoogi kuyigiriza. Ahoola haliiri omuntu muguma w'okuboko kw'ekulyo guhunzize.
LUK 6:7 Abigiriza b'amarhegeko n'aBafarisaayo baliiri kumuloleereza bweneene yi baabona akaba agafumya olusiku lw'eSaabato, kwenge baliiri gushonda echagarhuma bamusidaaka.
LUK 6:8 Aliko Yeesu aliyinji enkengeero zaabo. Ava abwira ntya oyo muntu w'okuboko guhunzize: «Yimanga, oje ahagarhi k'abantu booshi.» Ava ayuumuka n'okuja ho.
LUK 6:9 Yeesu abwira bo ntya: «Mbabazize ntya: gichi chiyemereerwe olusiku lw'eSaabato? Okujira amenja changwa amabi? Ogufumya omuntu changwa okumuleka afe?»
LUK 6:10 Abalola booshi, abwira oyo muntu ntya: «Gonyoola okuboko kwawe.» Oyo muntu akugonyoola n'okuva kwafuma.
LUK 6:11 Aliko abigiriza b'amarhegeko n'aBafarisaayo bayunjulwa n'omujinya n'ogurhondera kubazana gurhe bajirage Yeesu.
LUK 6:12 Amo mango, Yeesu aja oku musozi kuja gusaliira. Amala k'obudufu booshi ey'ali asaliira Nnamahanga.
LUK 6:13 Bwacheere eseezi, ahamagala abigirizwa baage, achishoga mw'ekumi na babiri. Abayirika «Ntumwa.» Ezo ntumwa zeezi:
LUK 6:14 Simooni oyu Yeesu ahaaga eziino lya Petero, na Ndereya mwene waabo, Yakobo na Yohaana, Firipo na Baritolomaayo,
LUK 6:15 Matayo na Tomaasi, Yakobo mwene Lufaayo na Simooni waliiri Muzelooti,
LUK 6:16 Yuuda mwene Yakobo na Yuuda Isikariyooti, ye wahindukaga mulenzi.
LUK 6:17 Yeesu ayandagala nabo gurhenga oku musozi n'okuyimanga omu kabanda ahaliiri abigirizwa baage banene. Ahoola haliiri n'echigusho chinene ch'abantu: abantu b'eYudeeya, ab'eYerusaleema na ab'echamashinji ch'eTiiro na ech'eSidoona.
LUK 6:18 Bayinjaga mpu bamuyunviirize anabafumye endwala zaabo. Abantu baalifarhirwe n'abazimu baafuma.
LUK 6:19 Ngasi muntu aliiri gushonda amuhume ko, bulaala obuhashe bwa Nnamahanga bwaliiri kumurhenga ko n'okubafumya booshi.
LUK 6:20 Yeesu aja alola abigirizwa baage n'okuderha ntya: «Mugishirwe, mwe muli bakene, kwenge oBwami bwa Nnamahanga buli bwenyu!
LUK 6:21 Mugishirwe, mwe muli nzara buno, kwenge nji mwayuugurha! Mugishirwe, mwe muli kulira buno, kwenge nji mwasheka!
LUK 6:22 Mugishirwe, akaba abantu bakabayanga, akaba bakabalahira, bakabadukanga n'okuderha kubi elugulu w'amaziino menyu, kwenge muyemereere Mwene oMuntu.
LUK 6:23 Musiime n'ogushagaluka amango ebyoola nji byabahikira, kwenge oluhembo lwenyu luli lunene omu mpingu. Ntyo maani ku bashookuluza baabo baliiri kulibuza abaleebi ba Nnamahanga.
LUK 6:24 Aliko buhanya bwenyu mwe bachire! Kwenge mwabo mwahaabirwe olwenyu luhembo!
LUK 6:25 Buhanya bwenyu mwe muyugurhire buno! Kwenge nji mwagwarha enzara! Buhanya bwenyu mwe muli gusheka buno! Kwenge nji mwaba omu mishiibo n'omu malira!
LUK 6:26 Buhanya bwenyu akaba abantu booshi bali kubaderha bwinja, kwenge ntyo ku bashookuluza baabo baliiri kujirira abaleebi b'obubeeshi!»
LUK 6:27 «Aliko mbabwirire, mwe muli kunyunva: musiime bashombanyi benyu, mujire amenja oku babashombere;
LUK 6:28 mugishe abanabavuma n'ogusaliirira ababadukanga.
LUK 6:29 Akaba omuntu agushuurhire oku rhama liguma, omuyeerekeze n'elindi; nk'omuntu akunyagire egorhe lyaawe, omuleke arhoole n'esimiisi yaawe.
LUK 6:30 «Ohe ngasi yeeshi oguhemere echintu, na nk'omuntu agurhoolere ehyaawe, orhagishiibaga wamuhema hyo.
LUK 6:31 «Mujirire abantu nk'oku mushondere abandi babajirirage.
LUK 6:32 Nka musiimire aba basiima bonyine, mukengereere oku nji mwahaabwa oluhembo? Nanga! aBanyabyaaha nabo basiima aba basiima!
LUK 6:33 N'akonva mujira amenja oku babajirira amenja bonyine, mukengereere oku nji mwahaabwa oluhembo? Nanga! aBanyabyaaha nabo baajira ntyo.
LUK 6:34 N'akaba muyindika aba mulangaalire oku nabo nji babajuha, mukengereere oku nji mwahaabwa oluhembo? Nanga! aBanyabyaaha nabo bayindika abandi banyabyaaha yi nji babajuha!
LUK 6:35 Ahuubwe, musiime bashombanyi benyu, mubajirire amenja n'oguhoza buzira kulingiriza kugalulirwa echintu. Ntyo, nji mwahaabwa oluhembo lunene n'okuba beene Nnamahanga w'Elugulu Bweneene, kwenge ali mwinja oku barhasiima n'oku babi.
LUK 6:36 «Mube n'olukogo nk'oku Yisho ali w'olukogo.»
LUK 6:37 «Murhachiiraga muntu olushinja na Nnamahanga naye arhakabachiira lushinja. Murhaderhaga okw'abandi bahanwe na Nnamahanga arhakaderha oku muhanwe. Ahuubwe mubabalire abandi na Nnamahanga nj'abababalira.
LUK 6:38 Muhe abandi na Nnamahanga nj'abaha. Nji mwahaabwa omulengo gulengerwe bwinja, gusindagiirwe n'okuyunjuzwa bweneene kugera ogusheeshekala. Bulaala Nnamahanga nj'abalengera n'omulengo mulengera mo abandi.»
LUK 6:39 Yeesu ashuba kubabwira omugani: «Empumi erhakalambagiza eyindi mpumi, k'arhali ntyo? Akaba ntyo, oku bali babiri booshi banarhogera omu kijokole.
LUK 6:40 Omwigirizwa arhaba elugulu w'omwigiriza waage; alik'omwigirizwa oyigiriizwe bwinja anaba kuguma n'omwigiriza waage.
LUK 6:41 «Chagarhuma walola ehirhi hiri omu liisho lya mwene wenyu n'obo orhamenyere egirhi chiri omu liisho lyawe?
LUK 6:42 Gurhe wakabwira mwene wenyu ntya: ‹Mwene weerhu, leka ngukuule ehi hirhi hiri omu liisho lyawe›, werhabwene chiro egirhi chiri omu ly'emwawe? We ndyaalya we, rhang'okuule egirhi chiri omu liisho lyawe y'obona bwinja n'ogukuula ehirhi omu liisho lya mwene wenyu.»
LUK 6:43 «Omurhi mwinja gurhayeeza amalehe mabi. N'omurhi gulwere gurhayeeza amalehe menja.
LUK 6:44 Ngasi murhi gumenyikana oku malehe maago. Barhacha amalehe m'omutiini oku mirhi y'emishaaki n'emizabiibu oku marhovu.
LUK 6:45 Omuntu mwinja akuula ebintu binja biri omu murhima gwage n'omuntu mubi naye akuula ebintu bibi biri omu murhima gwage. Kwenge obuunu bwa ngasi muntu buderha ebiyunjwire oku murhima gwage.»
LUK 6:46 «Girhuma mumpamagala ‹Nnaweerhu, Nnaweerhu›, n'obo murhajira ebi mbabwirire?
LUK 6:47 «Omuntu w'okuja emunda ndi, oyunva ebinwa byaani n'okubihira omu bijiro, tala gurhe ashushire:
LUK 6:48 ali nka muntu oli kuyumbaka enju. Ajokwere bweneene omu budaka kugera oku baale, arhonderera ahoola kuyumbaka. Amango emisuuka yayinjaga, amenji m'olwinji machishenya kw'eyo nju, aliko marhagalaga kuyishaganya, kwenge eyo nju yali yumbakirwe bwinja.
LUK 6:49 Aliko, oyunviirhe ebinwa byaani buzira kubihira omu bijiro ali nka muntu oyumbakire enju oku budaka buzira kujokola y'arhonderera ahoola kuyumbaka bwinja. Amango emisuuka yagishenyaga kw'eyo nju, yahika yaagwa: yashandaakala looshi.»
LUK 7:1 Yeesu abeere amamala kubwira olubaga lwaliiri kumuyunviriza ebi binwa byooshi, aja eGaperinaumu.
LUK 7:2 Eyoola, omukulu w'abasoda w'ekirooma aligwerhe omuja waage w'akamaro. Oyo muja alilwere bweneene ey'ali bufa.
LUK 7:3 Oyo mukulu w'abasoda abeere ayunva yi baderha ebiyerekeere Yeesu, amurhumira abashamuka baguma b'aBayaahudi kumuhema ayinje amufumize oyo omuja waage.
LUK 7:4 Babeere baagera emwa Yeesu, barhondera kumuyinginga bweneene n'okuderha ntya: «Oyu mukulu w'abasoda akwaneene gurhabaalwa naawe.
LUK 7:5 Kwenge anasiima olubaga lwerhu, yeewe ye wayumbakisaga esinagoogi yeerhu.»
LUK 7:6 Nnaweerhu ava agenda nabo. Abeere akola ali hoofu n'enju, oyo mukulu w'abasoda arhuma abeera baage kubwira Yeesu ntya: «Mwigiriza, orhashiibaga wachilibuza. Nyoono ntakwaneene mp'ohike omu mwani.
LUK 7:7 Chegirhumire ntayinja nyenyine emunda oli. Aliko oderhe chinwa chiguma chonyine y'omuja waani afuma.
LUK 7:8 Kwenge naani ndi eshiishi w'abanrhegekere na kandi ngwerhe abasoda nyimangiire. Nkabwira muguma ntya: ‹Genda!›, anagenda, na nkabwira owindi ntya: ‹Yinja!›, anayinja; na nkabwira omuja waani ntya: ‹Kola echiila!›, anagikola.»
LUK 7:9 Yeesu abeere ayunva ebyo binwa, asomererwa oyo mukulu w'abasoda. Ahindamuka abwira ntya echigusho ch'abantu bali bamukulikiire: «Mbabwirire oku ntashubiraga kubona obwemeezi buli ntya, nangwa! Chiro n'omu Israheeli.»
LUK 7:10 Bala beera omukulu w'abasoda arhumaga, babeere bagaluka bashimaana omuja afumire.
LUK 7:11 Enyuma z'aho, Yeesu aja omu gishagala chiguma chiyirikwa Naiina. Abigirizwa baage n'echigusho chinene ch'abantu bamuherekeza.
LUK 7:12 Abeere agera hoofu n'omulyango g'olugo lw'echo gishagala, haahulukira abantu baliiri kuja guhamba omufu. Oyo mufu aliiri mwana w'echinege w'omushumbakazi muguma. Abantu banene b'ahoola baliiri haguma n'oyo mushumbakazi.
LUK 7:13 Nnaweerhu abeere amubona, amuyunvira obonjo bweneene n'okumubwira ntya: «Orhaliraga!»
LUK 7:14 Ayegeera n'okuva ahuma oku gipoyi. Abaali giheekere bayimanga. Yeesu aderha ntya: «Musole we, nkubwirire ntya: zuuka!»
LUK 7:15 Nyagufa azuuka, ayikala n'ogurhondera kuderha. Yeesu amugalulira nyina.
LUK 7:16 Booshi bayuubaha. Bakuuza Nnamahanga omu kuderha ntya: «Rhwabonekeerwe n'omuleebi mukulu!», na kandi: «Nnamahanga ayinjire gurhabaala olubaga lwage!»
LUK 7:17 N'omu Yudeeya yooshi na hoofu nayo hooshi, abantu bamenya ebi Yeesu ali ajirire.
LUK 7:18 Abigirizwa ba Yohaana bamubwira byooshi Yeesu aliiri kujira. Yohaana ahamagala babiri omu bo,
LUK 7:19 abarhuma emwa Nnaweerhu kumubaza ntya: «Ka wooyo we Masiiya Nnamahanga alaganyaga changwa rhukwaneene kulinga owindi?»
LUK 7:20 Abo bigirizwa babiri babeere baahika hoofu na Yeesu, bamubwira ntya: «Yohaana Mubatiiza arhurhumire gukubaza ntya: ‹Ka wooyo we Masiiya ogwasizwe kuyinja changwa rhukwaneene kulinga owindi?›»
LUK 7:21 Mw'akoola gashanji, Yeesu afumya abantu banene endwala zaabo, obulema, n'abazimu, n'okugalulira empumi okubona.
LUK 7:22 Yeesu ashubiza abigirizwa ba Yohaana ntya: «Muje kubalira Yohaana ebi mwabwene n'okuyunva: empumi yi zabona, ebirema yi byalambagira, ababenzibenzi yi baafuma, ebihuli yi byayunva, abafu yi bafuuka, n'oMwazi Mwinja yi gwashambaalirwa abakene.
LUK 7:23 Agishwe olaala orhakaleka kunyemeera!»
LUK 7:24 Abarhumwa ba Yohaana babeere bagenda, Yeesu ava arhondera kubwira ntya olubaga lwali ho elugulu wa Yohaana: «Gichi mwajaagilola omu mpinga? Ka lusheke lushaganyizwe n'omuyaga?
LUK 7:25 Kandi, gichi mwajaaga kulola? Ka muntu oyambeere emishangi minja? Aliko abayambala emishangi minja n'okulama omu muhimbo bali omu nju z'abaami.
LUK 7:26 Aliko si, gichi mwajaaga mwaja kulola? Omuleebi? Neechi, mbabwirire okw'ali muleebi, na kandi yeewe alushire omuleebi.
LUK 7:27 Kwenge Yohaana y'aMandiko Matagatiifu maderhaga ntya elugulu waage: ‹Ntumire omubala mwazi waani agurhange embere, kugurheganyiza enjira.›
LUK 7:28 Mbabwirire oku omu booshi baburhirwe n'abakazi, harhashubiraga kuba omukulu kulusha Yohaana. Aliko, omugeeke bweneene omu Bwami bwa Nnamahanga ali mukulu kumulusha.»
LUK 7:29 Olubaga looshi n'abafurhiisa b'amakooli bali bamuyunviriize, bayemeera oku Nnamahanga akwaneene, banachibatiziisa emwa Yohaana.
LUK 7:30 Aliko aBafarisaayo n'abigiriza b'amarhegeko balahiire eki Nnamahanga ashondaga oku bo n'okuva balahira kubatiizwa na Yohaana.
LUK 7:31 Yeesu ashuba kuderha ntya: «Abantu bali zeene nakabashushanya na nde? Bashushire nde?
LUK 7:32 Bashushire n'abaana bayikeere embuga, eyi baguma yi bahamagala abaabo ntya: ‹Rhwabazihiire omulizi aliko murhazinire! Rhwabayimpiire enyimpo z'emishiibo aliko murhalirire!›
LUK 7:33 Amango Yohaana Mubatiiza ayinjaga, arhaliiri kulya emigati n'okunywa edivaayi. Mwamuderha ntya: ‹Agwarhirwe n'omuzimu!›
LUK 7:34 Leero Mwene oMuntu amayinja, ali kulya n'okunywa. Kandi mwamamuderha ntya: ‹Tala oyu muntu oganiiza okulya konyine n'okunywa edivaayi. Ali mwira w'abafurhiisa b'amakooli n'abandi banyabyaaha!›
LUK 7:35 Aliko, obwenge bunene bwa Nnamahanga buyinjikeene nka b'okuli oku booshi babuyemeera.»
LUK 7:36 oMufarisaayo muguma alaalika Yeesu kulya haguma naye. Aja omu nju yaage, bayikala kulya ebiryo.
LUK 7:37 Mw'echo gishagala mwaliiri omukazi w'ebyaaha. Abeere ayunva oku Yeesu y'alya emw'oyo Mufarisaayo, aleerha omukebo gw'amarashi.
LUK 7:38 Ayimanga enyuma za Yeesu, ahaburhambi bw'amagulu maage. Arhondera kulira n'okulobya amagulu ma Yeesu n'emiziga yaage. Ashangula amagulu ma Yeesu n'enviiri zaage, amahoobera, n'okumashiiga kw'amarashi.
LUK 7:39 Oyo Mufarisaayo walaalikaga Yeesu abeere abona ntyo, achibwira ntya omu murhima gwage: «Oyu muntu nk'aliiri muleebi wa Nnamahanga, singa amenyere oyu mukazi wamuhumire ko ali nde, okw'ali munyabyaaha.»
LUK 7:40 Yeesu abwira oyo Mufarisaayo ntya: «Simooni, ngwerhe echinwa ch'ogukubwira.» Simooni ashubiza ntya: «Derha, Mwigiriza.»
LUK 7:41 Yeesu aderha ntya: «Bantu babiri baligwerhe omwinda gw'owabayindikaga. Muguma aligwerhe omwinda gw'edinaari magana marhaano n'owindi makumi marhaano.
LUK 7:42 Nka kunoola booshi ntaaye waligalire kumujuha, abababalira booshi oku bali babiri. Nde nji wamusiima bweneene mw'aba babiri?»
LUK 7:43 Simooni amushubiza ntya: «Nkengereere k'olaala ababaliraga walimugwerhe mwinda munene.» Yeesu amubwira ntya: «Waderhere okuli.»
LUK 7:44 Ashuba guhindamukira emunda oyo mukazi ali n'okubwira Simooni ntya: «K'obwene oyu mukazi? Najiire omu mwawe, chiro orhampeere amenji m'ogushuka amagulu, aliko yeewe anshukire amagulu n'emiziga yaage n'okumashangula n'enviiri zaage.
LUK 7:45 Wooyo orhanyankiriire omu kumpoobera, aliko yeewe arhalekere guhoobera amagulu maani gurhengera aha najiriire omu mwawe.
LUK 7:46 Wooyo orhashiigire amavurha omu rhwe lyaani, aliko yeewe ashiigire amarashi oku magulu maani.
LUK 7:47 Cho girhumire nkubwirire oku obuzigire bunene anyerekere, buyerekeene okw'ebyaaha byaage binene byababaliirwe. Aliko obabaliirwe bugeeke anayeerekana obuzigire bugeeke.»
LUK 7:48 Yeesu abwira oyo mukazi ntya: «Ebyaaha byaawe byababaliirwe.»
LUK 7:49 Abaliiri kulya oku meeza haguma na Yeesu barhondera guchidedeesa ntya: «Oyu ali nde w'okubabalira n'ebyaaha nabyo?»
LUK 7:50 Aliko Yeesu abwira oyo mukazi ntya: «Obwemeezi bwawe bwaguchungwire; ogende n'omurhuula.»
LUK 8:1 Buzinda bw'aho, Yeesu alenga omu bishagala bineneenene n'omu bigeekegeeke. Agenda ayaamagaza n'okubala oMwazi Mwinja gw'obwime bwa Nnamahanga. Entumwa zaage ekumi n'ebiri zaliiri haguma naye,
LUK 8:2 n'abakazi baguma Yeesu akuulaga mw' abazimu n'abandi afumyaga endwala: Mariya oyirikwa w'eMagadala, warhengwaga mo bazimu mushanvu,
LUK 8:3 Jaani muka Chuuza waliiri mwimangizi w'ebikulo bya Heroode, Suzana, n'abandi bakazi banene barhabaalaga n'ebikulo byaabo akaasi ka Yeesu n'entumwa zaage.
LUK 8:4 Abantu banene bayegeera Yeesu, barhengeraga omu ngasi gishagala. Abachiira guno mugani:
LUK 8:5 «Haliiri muhinzi muguma, agenda kubyaala emburho yaage. Okw'ali kubyaala, embeke ziguma zarhogera ahaburhambirhambi bw'enjira: zalabarhwa, n'enyunyi z'omu chaalege zalya zo.
LUK 8:6 Ezindi zarhogera oku mabaale. Zabeere zamera, zayuuma, kwenge zabulaga amenji.
LUK 8:7 Ezindi zarhogera omu mishaaki; emishaaki yamera haguma nazo n'okuzifundeeza.
LUK 8:8 Ezindi mbeke zarhogera omu budaka bwinja; zabeere zamera, zayeeza ngasi nguma amagana m'amalehe.» Yeesu abeere amala kuderha ebyoola, ayaamagaza ntya: «Ogwerhe amarhwi m'okuyunva, ayunve!»
LUK 8:9 Abigirizwa baage baamubaza ech'ogo mugani gwali guderhere.
LUK 8:10 Abashubiza ntya: «Mwabo, mwahaabirwe okumenya ebibishirwe by'obwime bwa Nnamahanga. Aliko oku bandi, bibabwirirwe omu migani, yi ‹nka baabona, ntaacho babonage, na nka bayunviriza, ntaacho bayunvage.›»
LUK 8:11 «Ogu mugani guderhere ntya: emburho zishushanyizwe n'eChinwa cha Nnamahanga.
LUK 8:12 Embeke ziri ahaburhambirhambi bw'enjira, zishushanyizwe n'abantu bayunviriza eChinwa cha Nnamahanga. Aliko Shetaani anayinja gukuula eChinwa omu mirhima yaabo yi barhabaaga n'obwemeezi n'oguchungulwa.
LUK 8:13 Ezarhogeraga oku mabaale, zishushanyizwe n'abanayunviiriza eChinwa cha Nnamahanga n'oguchiyankirira n'obushagaluke. Aliko girhagwarha emizi omu mirhima yaabo, banagwarha obwemeezi omu gashanji kageeke n'amango emirhego yayinjaga banaleka obwemeezi.
LUK 8:14 Embeke zarhogeraga omu mishaaki zishushanyizwe n'abantu bayunva eChinwa cha Nnamahanga. Aliko emilago, obuchire n'obuloke bw'akalamo byanabafundeeza, banafundwa kuyeeza amalehe makulire.
LUK 8:15 Embeke zarhogeraga omu budaka bwinja, zishushanyizwe n'abayunva eChinwa cha Nnamahanga n'oguchibiika omu murhima mwinja gunakwiriire, n'omu guchihangaana banagwarha amalehe.»
LUK 8:16 «Omuntu arhakamala guchaana etara mpu aliyuubike kw'echintu changwa alihire omu ntalule. Aliko alihanika oku gikondo, y'abaaja omu nju baabona obumoleke.
LUK 8:17 Kwenge ntaacho chibishirwe girhakabishuulwa, na ntaacho chijirirwe omu bwibisho girhakamenyikana n'okuleerhwa ahabonekeene.
LUK 8:18 Muchilange okuntu muyunviriza; kwenge nji baaha ogwerhe; aliko orhagwerhe nji bamunyega chiro n'ehyakengereere oku agwerhe.»
LUK 8:19 Nyina na beene baabo Yeesu bayinja emunda ali, aliko barhakagalire kumuyegeera elugulu w'abantu banene.
LUK 8:20 Bantu baguma babwira Yeesu ntya: «Nyoko na beene benyu bayimangire ahambuga, bali bashonda gukulola.»
LUK 8:21 Aliko abashubiza ntya: «Nyaama na beene beerhu, bali bantu bayunva eChinwa cha Nnamahanga n'okugihira omu bijiro.»
LUK 8:22 Lusiku luguma, Yeesu aja omu bwarho haguma n'abigirizwa baage. Ababwira ntya: «Rhuyambukire eshiiriza w'enyanja.» Baava bagenda.
LUK 8:23 Oku bali kugenda, Yeesu alyaama. Omulaba munene gwasuuka omu nyanja, obwarho bwalema bwarhoola amenji. Baliiri hoofu kuzika.
LUK 8:24 Baava baja kumuchula, bamubwira ntya: «Mwigiriza, Mwigiriza, rhwafa!» Azuukire, akankamira omulaba n'ebivundu. Byarhuleera. Endeera yaba.
LUK 8:25 Yeesu aja ababaza ntya: «Ngahe obwemeezi bwenyu buli?» Bayuubaha n'ogusoomerwa, baalema babwirana ntya: «Oyu ali nde? Y'arhegeka chiro omulaba n'amenji, byanamukenga.»
LUK 8:26 Bagendekera n'olugenzi lwabo guhika omu gihugo ch'aBageraasi, chiloleene n'eche Galilaaya.
LUK 8:27 Yeesu abeere ayoomoka, muntu muguma w'ahoola ayinja embere zaage. Oyo muntu alifarhirwe n'abazimu. Gurhengera miira arhayambalaga emyambalo. Arhanabeeraga omu nju aliko oku mashinda.
LUK 8:28 Abeere abona Yeesu, ashuurha olujamu, achikabula embere z'amagulu maage n'okuderha ntya n'omulenge munene: «Yeesu, Mugala wa Nnamahanga w'Elugulu Bweneene, chagarhuma wachiiheba omu byaani? Ngurhebereeze, orhandibuzaga!»
LUK 8:29 Aliikaga omulenge ntyo kwenge Yeesu alirhegekere oyo muzimu okw'arhenge m'oyo muntu. Oyo muzimu abaaga anafarha oyo muntu siku zinene. Baliiri kumulanga ey'azirikirwe amaboko n'obulegule n'ebyuuma oku magulu. Aliko agendaga acha ebyo biziriko n'oguheekwa n'oyo muzimu omu mpinga.
LUK 8:30 Yeesu amubaza ntya: «Eziino lyawe we nde?» Ashubiza ntya: «Nyoono, nye Rhuli banene»; kwenge abazimu banene balimujiire mo.
LUK 8:31 Abo bazimu bamuyinginga okw'arhabarhegekaga kuja ekuzimu.
LUK 8:32 Ahoola haliiri obuso bw'engulube zinene bwaliiri kulagirwa oku musozi. Abo bazimu barhebeereza Yeesu oku abayemereere baje mw'ezo ngulube. Abayemeerera ntyo.
LUK 8:33 Bala bazimu barhenga m'oyo muntu, baja omu ngulube, n'obo buso booshi bwachima bwalibirha oku musozi, bwachiiroha omu nyanja n'okuzika.
LUK 8:34 Abangere b'ezo ngulube babeere baabona ebyabeere, balibirha n'okuyandaaza ogo mwazi mw'echo gishagala chinene n'omu rhwango rhutureene ho.
LUK 8:35 Abantu bayinja kulola ebyabeere. Baahika emunda Yeesu ali, bashigaana oyo muntu abazimu barhengaga mo ayikeere ahaburhambi bw'amagulu ma Yeesu, ey'ayambeere, anakola agwerhe obwenge booshi. Abantu bayuubaha.
LUK 8:36 Ababonaga ebyabaaga baabalira abandi gurhe oyo muntu waliiri mw'abazimu afumyagwa.
LUK 8:37 Abantu booshi b'egihugo ch'aBageraasi baahema Yeesu arhenge emwabo, kwenge bali bafarhirwe n'obuuba bunene. Yeesu ava aja omu bwarho, achigalukira.
LUK 8:38 Omuntu warhengagwa mw'abazimu arhebeereza Yeesu okw'agende haguma naye. Aliko Yeesu amulahirira, amubwira ntya:
LUK 8:39 «Ogaluke emwawe n'okubala byooshi Nnamahanga akujiriire.» Agenda, ayaamagaza omu gishagala chinene chooshi ebi Yeesu amujiriire byooshi.
LUK 8:40 Yeesu abeere agaluka eGalilaaya, ayankiirirwa n'abantu banene, kwenge baliiri kumulinga.
LUK 8:41 Ho n'aho haahulukira omuntu muguma oyirikwa Yaiiro. Aliiri mukulu w'esinagoogi. Achikabula hoofu n'amagulu ma Yeesu ey'ali kumurhebeereza oku aje emwage,
LUK 8:42 kwenge omwali w'echinege aliiri hoofu h'ogufa. Oyo mwali aligwerhe myaaka ekumi n'ebiri. Amango Yeesu aliiri kuja yo, abantu banene baliiri kumufundeeza bweneene.
LUK 8:43 Ahoola haliiri omukazi muguma w'alilwere gurhengera myaaka ekumi n'ebiri endwala y'okuva eshagama. Abaaga amalire ebikulo byaage byooshi oku bafumu, aliko ntaaye n'omuguma wagalire kumufumya.
LUK 8:44 Ayegeera enyuma za Yeesu, n'oguhuma oku mushoojo gw'efulema yaage. Ho n'aho, okuva kwage kw'eshagama kwahwa.
LUK 8:45 Yeesu abaza ntya: «Nde wampumire ko?» Abantu booshi bahakana. Petero aja amubwira ntya: «Mwigiriza, abantu banene yi bagufundeeza n'okugushunika!»
LUK 8:46 Aliko Yeesu aderha ntya: «Hali omuntu wampumire ko. Nyoono menyere bwinja oku hali emisi yantengere ko.»
LUK 8:47 Oyo mukazi abeere abona okw'amenyikeene, ayinja adirhimana guchikabula hoofu n'amagulu ma Yeesu. Achirhondoola embere z'abantu booshi echarhumaga amuhuma ko na gurhe afumaga ho n'aho.
LUK 8:48 Yeesu amubwira ntya: «Mwali waani, obwemeezi bwawe bwagufumize; ogende n'omurhuula.»
LUK 8:49 Oku Yeesu achiri aderha, hagera omuntu warhengera emw'ola mukulu w'esinagoogi. Abwira oyoola mukulu ntya: «Mwali waawe afiire, orhagishiibaga walunza oMwigiriza.»
LUK 8:50 Aliko Yeesu abeere abiyunva, abwira Yaiiro ntya: «Orhayuubahaga, yemeera konyine, mwali waawe afuma.»
LUK 8:51 Yeesu agerere emwa Yaiiro, arhayemeeraga omuntu aja omu nju haguma naye arhali Petero, Yohaana na Yakobo, haguma n'eshe na nyina w'oyo mwana.
LUK 8:52 Abantu booshi balemaga balira n'okulumwa elugulu w'oyo munyere. Aliko Yeesu aderha ntya: «Murhaliraga, arhafiire, ahuubwe alyaamire!»
LUK 8:53 Boowe bamushekera, eyi bayinji okw'oyo munyere afiire.
LUK 8:54 Aliko amufarhira oku kuboko n'okuderha ntya n'omulenge munene: «Mwana waani, zuuka!»
LUK 8:55 Omuuka gwage gwagaluka, ho n'aho ayimanga. Yeesu arhegeka oku bamuhe ebiryo.
LUK 8:56 Abazeere b'oyo munyere basoomerwa. Aliko Yeesu abarhegeka oku ntaaye babwirage ebyabeere.
LUK 9:1 Yeesu ahamagala entumwa zaage ekumi n'ebiri aziheereza obuhashe n'oburhegesi b'ogukuula abazimu booshi n'ogufumya endwala.
LUK 9:2 Azirhuma kuyigiriza enyigirizo ziyerekeere obwime bwa Nnamahanga n'ogufumya abalwala.
LUK 9:3 Abwira ezo ntumwa ntya: «Ntaacho muchiyikirage omu lugenzi lwenyu: ebe nkoni changwa eshaho, bibe biryo changwa efuranga, na ntaaye oheekage simiisi ebiri.
LUK 9:4 Enju nji babayankirira mo, muyibeere mo kugera amango nji mwaja ahandi.
LUK 9:5 Ngasi hantu abantu nji balahira kubayankirira, murhenge omu gishagala chaabo munakunguurhe olujuchu lw'amagulu menyu. Okoola kuli kubayeereka oku Nnamahanga nj'abahana.»
LUK 9:6 Ezo ntumwa zagenda, zarhondera kulenga omu ngasi gishagala. Zaliiri kuyigiriza oMwazi Mwinja n'ogufumya abalwala ngasi hooshi.
LUK 9:7 Heroode, murhegesi w'eGalilaaya, abeere ayunva byooshi biri byaagera, abula olwimango. Kwenge baguma baliiri kuderha mpu Yohaana afuukire gurhenga omu bafu.
LUK 9:8 Abandi bantu balemaga baderha mpu Eliya yi wagalukire. Abandi balemaga baderha mpu muguma omu baleebi ba miira yi wafuukire.
LUK 9:9 Aliko Heroode aderha ntya: «Nyoono nye naderhaga bache Yohaana erhwe. Ye nde oyu naye ndi nayunva baderha ebintu biri ntya elugulu waage?» Byaarhuma Heroode naye ashonda kubona Yeesu.
LUK 9:10 Entumwa zagaluka emunda Yeesu ali zanamubwira byooshi zajiraga. Aziheeka ahantu harhali lwamo oku lunda luyerekeere egishagala ch'eBetesayida.
LUK 9:11 Abantu banene babeere bamenya okw'ajiire yo, bamukulikira. Yeesu abayankirira. Alema ababwira ebinwa biyerekeere obwime bwa Nnamahanga, anafumya abantu bali bakeneere ogufuma.
LUK 9:12 Ezuuba lyarhondeere kuzika, entumwa ekumi n'ebiri zaja zayegeera Yeesu n'okumubwira ntya: «Galula aba bantu yi baja emunda balaala, yi banabona ebiryo omu bishagala n'omu mizi ya hoofu, kwenge rhuli omu mpinga.»
LUK 9:13 Aliko Yeesu abwira entumwa zaage ntya: «Mubahe mwenyine ebi baalya!» Entumwa zaderha ntya: «Rhugwerhe migati erhaano yonyine n'efi ebiri. K'oshondere rhwenyine rhuje kugula ebiryo by'aba bantu booshi?»
LUK 9:14 N'obo haliiri hoofu nka balume bihumbi birhaano. Yeesu abwira abigirizwa baage ntya: «Mubayikaze bigusho-bigusho by'abantu makumi marhaano.»
LUK 9:15 Abigirizwa baajira ntyo, babayikaza booshi.
LUK 9:16 Yeesu arhoola ela migati erhaano na zila fi ebiri, ayerekeza ameesho empingu, abigisha. Yeesu ava abichagulanga, anarhondera abiha abigirizwa baage yi babigabira abantu.
LUK 9:17 Abantu booshi baalya banayuugurha. Abigirizwa baheeka rhurhanda ekumi na rhubiri rhw'ebichiira byasigalaga.
LUK 9:18 Lusiku luguma eyi Yeesu ali asaliira aharhali abantu, eyi n'abigirizwa baage bachigushire haguma naye, Yeesu ababaza ntya: «Abantu bali kuderha oku nye nde?»
LUK 9:19 Abigirizwa bashubiza ntya: «Baguma yi baderha oku we Yohaana Mubatiiza; n'abandi mpu we Eliya, abandi mpu oli muguma w'omu baleebi ba miira wafuukire.»
LUK 9:20 Yeesu abaza abigirizwa baage ntya: «Aliko si, nenyu muderha oku nye nde?» Petero ashubiza ntya: «Wooyo oli Krisitu wa Nnamahanga.»
LUK 9:21 Yeesu abuza abigirizwa baage oku ntaaye babwirage ebyoola.
LUK 9:22 Ashuba kuderha oku bihemere Mwene oMuntu alibuke bweneene, alahirwe n'abashamuka b'aBayaahudi, abakulu b'abadaahwa n'abigiriza b'amarhegeko, ayirhwe n'olusiku lwa gasharhu afuuke.
LUK 9:23 Yeesu aja abwira abantu booshi ntya: «Akaba hali oshondere kunkulikira, achilahire yenyine, aheeke omusalaaba gwage ngasi lusiku, anankulikire.
LUK 9:24 Bulaala, owashonda guchungula akalamo kaage, agaheza; sy'aliko owaheza akalamo kaage eyi nye ntumire, agachungula.
LUK 9:25 Gichi bimaliire omuntu okugwarha ebikulo by'egulu lyooshi, aliko aheze akalamo kaage? Ntaacho!
LUK 9:26 Nk'omuntu anyunviire eshoni, anaziyunvire emyaazi yaani, Mwene oMuntu naye nj'amuyunvira eshoni hano nj'agaluka omu bukuuze bwage, bo na bukuuze bw'Eshe na bwa bamalahika batagatiifu.
LUK 9:27 Mbabwirire okuli: Baguma omu bali hano barhaafa embere babone obwime bwa Nnamahanga.»
LUK 9:28 Enyuma w'esiku zakagera ku munaane Yeesu aderhere ntyo, arhoola Petero, Yohaana na Yakobo; azamuukira oku musozi guhema Nnamahanga.
LUK 9:29 Abeere ali ahema, eshusho ly'amalanga maage lyahindamuka, n'emyambalo yaage yaba mweru bweneene n'okubaraganya.
LUK 9:30 Ho n'aho haboneka bantu babiri bali kuganiira naye: baliiri Muusa na Eliya,
LUK 9:31 babonekana omu bukuuze gurhenga emwa Nnamahanga. Baalema baganiira haguma na Yeesu ebiyerekeere okugenda kwage kwali kwaneene kuyenerera eYerusaleema.
LUK 9:32 Mwamo mango, Petero n'abaabo baliiri ero bweneene. Basisimukire, baabona obukuuze bwa Yeesu na bala balume babiri baliyimangire haguma naye.
LUK 9:33 Muusa na Eliya babeere bali balekana na Yeesu, Petero amubwira ntya: «Mwigiriza, kuli kwinja rhubeere hano. Rhwayumbaka biraaro bisharhu: chiguma chaawe, echindi cha Muusa n'echindi cha Eliya.» Petero arhalimenyere ebyaliiri kuderha.
LUK 9:34 Petero abeere ali aderha ntyo, oluhomo lwayinja lwanabashukulira n'egichuuchu chaalo. Abigirizwa babeere baabona oluhomo lwabashukulira, bayuubaha.
LUK 9:35 Omulenge gwayunviikana m'olo luhomo: «Oyuula ye Mugala waani nachishogere. Mumuyunve!»
LUK 9:36 Enyuma w'ogo mulenge okuyunviikana, Yeesu obonekana ali yenyine. Abigirizwa baasira, na ntaaye babwirire chintu, mwamo mango, oku bibabonaga ko ahoola.
LUK 9:37 Olusiku lwakulikiraga, Yeesu na balaala bigirizwa basharhu aliiri nabo, barhenga oku musozi. Abantu banene bayinja gushigaanana na Yeesu.
LUK 9:38 Omuntu muguma ayaamira ntya ahagarhi k'abantu: «Mwigiriza, nkuyingingire, ondolere ono mugala waani, kwenge ali w'echinege.
LUK 9:39 Hali omuzimu onamufarha, ho n'aho anamuyamiisa olujamu, anamudirhimanya bweneene, anamukuliisa olufula omu buunu, n'ogurhamurhenga mo juba, n'okumuleka eyi amamuvunangula.
LUK 9:40 Nayingingire abigirizwa baawe bakuule oyo muzimu, aliko barhagalaga.»
LUK 9:41 Yeesu aderha ntya: «Mwe gisisi chibi na chizira bwemeezi, kugera mango machi nabeera haguma nenyu n'okubalembera? Leerha mugala waawe hano.»
LUK 9:42 Omwana abeere ali ayegeera Yeesu, ola muzimu amubanda ahashi n'ogurhondera kumudirhimanya. Aliko Yeesu akalihira oyo muzimu, afumya omwana n'okumugalulira eshe.
LUK 9:43 Abantu booshi basoomererwa obuhashe bunene bwa Nnamahanga. Oku booshi bali basoomererwa byooshi Yeesu ali ajira, abwira abigirizwa baage ntya:
LUK 9:44 «Muyunve bwinja ebi nashonda kubabwira: Mwene oMuntu ayinja guhanwa omu fune z'abantu.»
LUK 9:45 Aliko abigirizwa barhayunvaga echi chinwa, eby'echi chinwa chiderhere byalibishirhwe y'abigirizwa barhamenyaga echi chiderhere. Baanali bayuubahire kubaza Yeesu ebiyerekeere echi chinwa.
LUK 9:46 Haahulukira obuhaka omu bigirizwa b'ogushonda kumenya nde oli mukulu omu bo.
LUK 9:47 Yeesu walimenyere obukengeere bw'emirhima yaabo, arhoola omwana murho, amuhira eburhambi bwage.
LUK 9:48 Ababwira ntya: «Oyankiriire oyu mwana oku ziino lyaani anyankiire nyenyine. N'onyankiriire ayankiriire owantumaga. Bulaala oli mudoorho omu mweshi oyo yeeri mukulu kulusha.»
LUK 9:49 Yohaana ava aderha ntya: «Mwigiriza, rhwabonaga omuntu oli akuula abazimu oku ziino lyaawe. Rhwamubuza bulaala arhagukulikira haguma neerhu.»
LUK 9:50 Yeesu amushubiza ntya: «Murhamubuzaga, bulaala orhali mushombanyi wenyu ey'ali wenyu.»
LUK 9:51 Esiku Yeesu alikwaneene guheekwa omu mpingu zabeere zaaba hoofu, Yeesu ahiga bweneene kuja eYerusaleema.
LUK 9:52 Arhuma ab'okubala emyaazi embere zaage. Bagenda n'okuja omu gishagala chiguma ch'aBasamariya kumurheganyiza eby'obulagiirire byooshi.
LUK 9:53 Aliko aBasamariya balahira kumuyankirira bulaala aliiri ayerekera eYerusaleema.
LUK 9:54 Abigirizwa ba Yeesu, Yakobo na Yohaana babeere bamenya ntyo, baderha ntya: «Nnaweerhu, k'oshondere rhubwire omuliro guchime gurhenga empingu kubasingonyola?»
LUK 9:55 Yeesu abahindamukira n'okubakalihira.
LUK 9:56 Baava baja omu chindi gishagala.
LUK 9:57 Babeere bali omu njira, omuntu muguma abwira Yeesu ntya: «Nagukulikira ngasi hooshi waaja.»
LUK 9:58 Yeesu amubwira ntya: «Emitereri ejira enkunda n'enyunyi z'omu chaalege zijira enyogo, sy'aliko Mwene oMuntu arhajira ahagahengeka erhwe lyaage.»
LUK 9:59 Yeesu abwira owindi ntya: «Onkulikire.» Aliko oyo muntu aderha ntya: «Nnaweerhu, onyemereere ntange nje guhamba daarha.»
LUK 9:60 Yeesu amushubiza ntya: «Oleke abafu bahambe abafu baabo; wooyo ogende, oje kuyaamagaza oBwami bwa Nnamahanga.»
LUK 9:61 Owindi muntu abwira Yeesu ntya: «Nnaweerhu, handeke nagukulikira, sy'aliko onyemereere ntange nje guseezera ab'emwani.»
LUK 9:62 Yeesu amubwira ntya: «Omuntu wamarhondera guhinga akanashuba kulola enyuma, arhakwaneene omu Bwami bwa Nnamahanga.»
LUK 10:1 Enyuma w'ebyoola, Nnaweerhu achishoga bandi bigirizwa makumi gali mushanvu na babiri. Abarhuma babiri-babiri bamurhange omu gishagala chooshi na ngasi hooshi alikwaneene kuja.
LUK 10:2 Yeesu ababwira ntya: «Emyaaka y'ogushaluula elugire, sy'aliko abakozi bageehere. Leero, muheme nyina emyaaka arhume abakozi kuyishaluula.
LUK 10:3 Mugende! Mbarhumire nka byaanabuzi ahagarhi ka banyambwe.
LUK 10:4 Murhaheekaga chiro lufuranga, changwa eshaho, changwa ebindi biraato. Na ntaaye mulamusage omu njira.
LUK 10:5 Omu ngasi nju nji mwaja mo, murhange muderhe ntya: ‹Omurhuula gube kw'eyi nju!›
LUK 10:6 Akaba omoola muli omuntu oshondere omurhuula, ogo murhuula gwenyu gwanamubeera ko; n'akaba nanga, omurhuula gwenyu gwanabagalukira.
LUK 10:7 Mubeere mw'eyoola nju, mulye munanywe ebi nji baabaha, kwenge omukozi akwaneene omukamarho gwage. Murhazereeraga omu maju.
LUK 10:8 Na ngasi gishagala nji mwaja mo, bakabayankirira, mulye ebi nji baabaha.
LUK 10:9 Mufumye abalwala nji baaba mo, munababwire ntya: ‹Obwime bwa Nnamahanga bwabayegereere.›
LUK 10:10 Aliko, omu ngasi gishagala nji mwaja mo nji bakalahira kubayankirira, mugende omu njira zaacho munababwire ntya:
LUK 10:11 ‹Rhubakungurhiire olujuchu lw'egishagala chenyu lwali lunaniirire oku magulu meerhu, lo lubaage buhamiiriza bw'amabi menyu. Aliko mumenye k'obwime bwa Nnamahanga bwabayegereere.›
LUK 10:12 Mbabwirire oku m'olo lusiku nji byayoolohera Sodoomo kulusha echoola gishagala.»
LUK 10:13 «Buhanya buchi oku wooyo gishagala ch'eKoraziini! Buhanya buchi oku wooyo gishagala ch'eBetesayida! Akaba ebisomereene byajirikeene emwenyu byakajirikeene eTiiro n'eSidoona, singa hamaagera siku zinene abantu b'eyoola balekere ebyaaha byaabo, singa bayambeere ebigunira n'okuyikala omu luvu!
LUK 10:14 Cho charhuma, olusiku l'ogucha olushinja nji byayoolohera Tiiro na Sidoona kubalusha mwabo.
LUK 10:15 Nawe gishagala ch'eGaperinaumu, k'omenyere mpu nji wazamuulwa guhika echaalege? Nangwa da! Nji wayandagazwa guhika ekuzimu.
LUK 10:16 Obayunviriize eyi nyoono ny'ayunviriize, obalahiire eyi nyoono ny'alahiire, n'ondahiire eyi alahiire owantumaga.»
LUK 10:17 Abigirizwa makumi gali mushanvu na babiri bagaluka n'obushagaluke n'okuderha ntya: «Nnaweerhu, n'abazimu nabo yi barhukenga amango rhuli rhwabarhegeka oku ziino lyaawe.»
LUK 10:18 Yeesu ababwira ntya: «Nabonaga Shetaani arhoga gurhengera omu chaalege nka mubaraganyo.
LUK 10:19 Muyunve bwinja: nabaheere oburhegesi b'okulabarha enjoka n'engobe, n'ogusinyongola obuhashe booshi bw'mushombanyi, na ntaacho nji chabajira kubi.
LUK 10:20 Sy'aliko murhasiimaga kwenge abazimu bali babayunva; ahuubwe musiime okuba amaziino menyu mayandikirwe omu mpingu.»
LUK 10:21 Mw'ako gashanji, Yeesu ayunjuzwa obushagaluke kugerera Muuka-Mutagatiifu, aderha ntya: «Daarha wee, Nnaweerhu w'omu mpingu n'omu gulu, ngusimiriize kwenge ebi bintu wabibishire abanyabwenge n'abahanga, wanabibishuulira abaana badoorho. Neechi Daarha, bulaala ntyo ku walisimiisizwe.
LUK 10:22 Daarha ampeere byooshi. Ntaaye onyinji nyoono Mugala nk'arhali Daarha yenyine, na ntaaye oyinji Daarha nk'arhali oMugala na ngasi yeeshi oMugala ashondere amumenye.»
LUK 10:23 Yeesu ahindamukira abigirizwa baage, ababwirira ntya eburhambi: «Magishirwe ameesho mali maabona ebi muli mwabona!
LUK 10:24 Bulaala, mbabwirire oku, baleebi banene n'abaami banene bali bashondere kubona ebi mwabo muli mwabona, aliko barhabibonaga ko. Bashondere kuyunva ebi mwabo muli mwayunva, aliko barhabiyunvaga ko.»
LUK 10:25 Buzinda bw'ebi, mwigiriza muguma w'amarhegeko ayimanga n'okubaza Yeesu ntya omu kumurhega: «Mwigiriza, bichi nkwaneene kujira yi mbona akalamo k'esiku n'amango?»
LUK 10:26 Yeesu amushubiza ntya: «Bichi biyandikirwe omu Rhegeko? Gurhe oliyunva eyi walisoma?»
LUK 10:27 Omwigiriza w'amarhegeko ashubiza ntya: «Osiime Nnaweerhu Nnamahanga waawe n'omurhima gwawe gooshi, n'emisi yaawe yooshi n'obwenge bwawe bwooshi. Kandi: Osiime n'omutuuranyi waawe nka okw'ochisiima wenyine.»
LUK 10:28 Yeesu aja amubwira ntya: «Washubiize bwinja. Ojire ebyoola oderhere, nji waalama.»
LUK 10:29 Aliko yeewe ashonda kuyeerekana okw'akwaneene. Abaza Yeesu ntya: «Omutuuranyi waani ye nde?»
LUK 10:30 Yeesu ashuba kumubwira ntya: «Haliiri muntu muguma warhengaga eYerusaleema guchimira eYeeriko. Abeere ali omu njira, abugaanana n'ebishumuusi. Byamunyega byooshi aligwerhe, bamushuurha banagenda eyi bamulekere nka mufu.
LUK 10:31 Haahulukira omudaahwa muguma wachimaga mw'eyo njira, abeere abona oyo muntu, achigerera oku lwindi lunda lw'enjira, naye achigendera.
LUK 10:32 oMulaawi muguma naye agera ahoola, abona oyo muntu, achigerera oku lwindi lunda lw'enjira, anachigendera.
LUK 10:33 Aliko, oMusamariya muguma waliiri lugenzi, ahika hoofu naye. Amubwene, amubeera obonjo.
LUK 10:34 Ashegera aha ali, amushomoola ebibihulu omu kubisheeshera kw'amavurha n'edivaayi, abirhuba n'ebiraka. Amubarhulira oku ndogomi yaage, amuheeka omu nju y'abagenzi, anamulanga.
LUK 10:35 Eseezi ly'aho, oyo Musamariya akuula dinaari ebiri omu shaho yaage, aziheereza nyina enju y'abagenzi n'okuderha ntya: ‹Obuke bwinja oyu muntu. Hano ngaluka, nakujuha nyenyine ebindi byooshi waaba wakoleeseze k'oyu muntu.›»
LUK 10:36 Yeesu aja abaza ntya ola mwigiriza w'amarhegeko: «Nd'obwene mw'aba bantu basharhu walibeere mutuuranyi w'oyu muntu wabugaananaga n'ebishumuusi?»
LUK 10:37 Omwigiriza w'amarhegeko ashubiza ntya: «Ola muntu wamubeeraga obonjo.» Yeesu amubwira ntya: «Genda, nawe ojire ntyo.»
LUK 10:38 Oku Yeesu n'abigirizwa baage bali omu njira, Yeesu aja omu gishagala chiguma. Omukazi oyirikwa Marita amuyankirira.
LUK 10:39 Oyo Marita aligwerhe mwene waabo oyirikwa Mariya. Oyo Mariya ayikala embere za magulu ma Nnaweerhu, aliiri ayunviriza eChinwa chaage.
LUK 10:40 Aliko Marita yeewe aliiri gukola orhwasi rhunene. Ahulukira n'okuderha ntya: «Nnaweerhu, ka birhakulunzize kubona mwene weerhu andekere gukola orhwasi rhooshi nyenyine? Omubwire angwase maani.»
LUK 10:41 Nnaweerhu amushubiza ntya: «Marita, Marita, oli wachilunza n'oguchikobola na bintu binene.
LUK 10:42 Hali chintu chiguma chonyine ch'obulagiirire. Mariya yeewe achishogere echintu gikwiriire, girhakamunyagwa.»
LUK 11:1 Lusiku luguma, Yeesu aliiri hantu haguma ey'ali gusaliira. Abeere amala gusaliira, muguma omu bigirizwa baage amubwira ntya: «Nnaweerhu, orhuyigirize gusaliira nk'oku Yohaana ayigirizaga abigirizwa baage.»
LUK 11:2 Yeesu ababwira ntya: «Nka mwasaliira, mugende mwaderha ntya: ‹Daarha, eziino lyawe likuuzwe, obwime bwawe buyinje.
LUK 11:3 Orhuhe ebiryo byeerhu bya ngasi lusiku.
LUK 11:4 Orhubabalire ebyaaha byeerhu, bulaala neerhu rhubabalira abarhujirira amabi. Orhanagenda warhuleka rhwarhogera omu chigeregezo.›»
LUK 11:5 Yeesu ashuba kubwira abigirizwa baage ntya: «Nde omu mwabo wakagwarha mwira waage, akaja emwage ahagarhi k'obudufu kumubwira ntya: ‹Mwira waani, ompoze migati esharhu,
LUK 11:6 bulaala muguma omu beera baani ahikire ahamwani gurhengera omu lugenzi na ntaacho ngwerhe namusheegera.›
LUK 11:7 Akaba owabo omushubiize ntya ey'anali omu mwage: ‹Leka okumbera erhwe; olunvi lwachingirwe miira, nyoono n'abaana baani, rhwalyaamire. Ntakagala kuzuuka mpu nguhe emigati.›
LUK 11:8 Okuli mbabwirire, chiro akaba arhazuukire kumuha emigati bulaala ali mwira waage, azuuka bulaala mwira waage arhaluhire kumuyinginga, anamuha byooshi alagiriire.
LUK 11:9 «Bobunoola nyoono mbabwirire ntya: Muheme, mwanahaabwa; mushonde, mwanabona; mukongoorhe oku lunvi, mwanachinguulirwa.
LUK 11:10 Bulaala ohema ahaabwa, oshonda abona n'okongoorha oku lunvi achinguulirwa.
LUK 11:11 Nde y'eshe w'omwana omu mwabo nk'omugala amuhemere efi, akamuha enjoka ahaali h'efi?
LUK 11:12 Changwa, nk'amuhemere egi, akamuha engobe?
LUK 11:13 Akaba mwabo, mwe bantu babi, muyinji guha abaana benyu ebintu binja, gurhe Daarha w'empingu ojira olukogo lunene kulusha agafundwa guhaana Muuka-Mutagatiifu oku bamuhemere ye?»
LUK 11:14 Lusiku luguma, Yeesu aliiri gukuula omuzimu wajiraga omuntu muguma kuba nyamugama. Omuzimu abeere ahuluka, nyamugama arhondera kuderha. Abantu banene baliiri ahoola basoomerwa bweneene.
LUK 11:15 Aliko bantu baguma baderha ntya: «Yeesu ali akoleesa Belizebuuli, mukulu w'abazimu, omu guhulusa abazimu.»
LUK 11:16 Abandi bantu nabo baarhega Yeesu omu kumuhema echimenyeeso ch'ogurhengera empingu.
LUK 11:17 Aliko, Yeesu alimenyere enkengeero zaabo, ababwira ntya: «Obwami buchishandeeze bonyine, bujiire ebw'olufu lwabo; enju zaabo zanahenera mo ziguma oku zindi.
LUK 11:18 Akaba leero Shetaani ali achilwisa yenyine, gurhe obwami bwage bwakalama, kwenge muli mwaderha mpu nyoono ndi nakoleesa Belizebuuli omu guhulusa abazimu?
LUK 11:19 N'akaba ndi nahulusa abazimu kugerera Belizebuuli, abaana benyu babahulusa kugerera nde? Chi nji charhuma bonyine nji baaba bazuuzi benyu.
LUK 11:20 Aliko, akaba ndi nahulusa abazimu kulengera obuhashe bwa Nnamahanga, k'okuderha k'obwime bwage bwabahikiire.
LUK 11:21 Omuntu w'emisi ohagarhiire emitwaro yaage, amango ali alanga enju yaage, ebikulo byaage eyi bilangirwe bwinja.
LUK 11:22 Aliko, akaba omulushire emisi agahulukira n'okumuhima, akamunyega emitwaro yaage yooshi alilangaliire; na ntyo anagabira abandi bantu ebintu amunyegaga.
LUK 11:23 Omuntu orhali haguma naani eyi ali andwisa; n'omuntu orhangwasa kugusha eyi ali ashandaaza.»
LUK 11:24 «Amango omuzimu arhengere omu muntu, anaja omu mpinga gushonda amahumuukiro. Na nk'amabulire, anaderha ntya: ‹Nkola kugaluka omu nju yaani, mula narhengeraga.›
LUK 11:25 Ey'ayigera mo, anayibugaana ehyagiirwe enarheganyizwe bwinja.
LUK 11:26 Leero, anaja agenda gushonda bandi bazimu mushanvu babi kumulusha. Baanaja mo n'okubeera mo. Oboorhere b'oyo muntu bwanaba bubi kulusha obwambere.»
LUK 11:27 Yeesu abeere ali aderha ntyo, omukazi muguma mw'abo bantu banene aderha n'omulenge munene n'okumubwira ntya: «Enda yaguheekaga egishwe n'amabeere makuyonsaga!»
LUK 11:28 Aliko Yeesu ashubiza ntya: «Ahuubwe, bagishirwe abali bayunva eChinwa cha Nnamahanga n'ogukulikira cho.»
LUK 11:29 Abantu banene babeere bali bachiigusha, Yeesu arhondera kuderha ntya: «Echi gisisi chiri gisisi chibi: chiri chashonda echimenyeeso. Girhagahaabwa echindi chimenyeeso kuleka echa Yoona.
LUK 11:30 Kwenge nka kulaala Yoona abaaga chimenyeeso oku bantu b'eNinaawi, ko n'oko Mwene oMuntu aba chimenyeeso kw'echiila gisisi.
LUK 11:31 Olusiku l'ogucha olushinja, omugoli w'egarhongo nj'ahulukira haguma n'abantu b'echi gisisi. Nj'abahaniisa, bulaala alirhengere omu mahanga ma hale kuja kuyunva ebinwa by'obwenge bunene bwa Solomoono. N'obo hanoola hali olushire Solomoono!
LUK 11:32 Amango m'ogucha olushinja, abantu b'eNinaawi nabo nji bayimanga haguma n'abantu b'echi gisisi, n'okugihaniisa. Kwenge balekere ebyaaha byaabo amango Yoona ayamagazaga omwazi. Leero hanoola hali olushire Yoona.»
LUK 11:33 «Ntaaye ochaana etara mpu alihire ahabishirwe changwa omu garhanda; ahuubwe analihanika oku gikondo, y'abaaja omu nju baabona obumoleke.
LUK 11:34 Eliisho lyawe ly'etara ly'omubiri gwawe. Nk'eliisho lyawe likwiriire, omubiri gwawe gooshi nago gukolezeezwe. Aliko nk'alibiihire, omubiri gwawe nago eyi guli omu mwizimya.
LUK 11:35 Ochilange obumoleke bukuli mo burhaba mwizimya.
LUK 11:36 Akaba leero omubiri gwawe gooshi gukolezeezwe, buzira kugwarha olunda n'oluguma omu mwizimya, omubiri gwawe gooshi nji gwaba gukolezeezwe kuguma n'amango etara likukoleezeza n'obumoleke bwalyo.»
LUK 11:37 Oku Yeesu ali aderha, oMufarisaayo muguma amulaalika emwage mpu aje kulya. Yeesu aja omu nju, ayikala n'okulya.
LUK 11:38 Oyo Mufarisaayo asoomerwa okubona Yeesu alya buzira gukalaba.
LUK 11:39 Aliko Nnaweerhu amubwira ntya: «Mwabo mwe Bafarisaayo muzigaana gucheesa emugongo w'engumbu n'embale, n'obo omu mirhima yenyu muyunjwire obushumuusi n'obubi.
LUK 11:40 Mwe binganyi! Owalemaga omubiri g'omuntu k'arhanali ye walemaga omurhima?
LUK 11:41 Aliko mwabo, muhaane n'omurhima g'obonjo ebiri omu mirhima yenyu, n'ebindi byooshi byacheeswa emwenyu.
LUK 11:42 «Aliko buhanya buchi emwenyu, mwe Bafarisaayo! Munahaana entuulo y'echigabi chiguma ch'ekumi ch'ebirhi by'obulunge n'echa ngasi buuko bw'eshogo, aliko mwanagenda mwakeneereza kujira ebijiro bikwaneene n'obuzigire bwa Nnamahanga! Ebyoola bimwali mukwaneene kujira, buzira kuleka ebindi.
LUK 11:43 «Buhanya buchi emwenyu, mwe Bafarisaayo! Musiima kuyikala oku bichumbi by'embere omu masinagoogi, munasiima abantu babalamuse n'obukenge omu soko!
LUK 11:44 «Buhanya buchi oku mwabo! Muli nka shinda zirhagwerhe chimenyeeso, abantu banazilambagira ko buzira kumenya!»
LUK 11:45 Muguma omu bayigiriza amarhegeko ava aderha ntya: «Mwigiriza, omu kuderha ntyo, orhudukangire neerhu!»
LUK 11:46 Yeesu amushubiza ntya: «Buhanya buchi oku mwabo nenyu bigiriza b'amarhegeko! Muheesa abantu emizigo ekomeere guheeka, nenyu mwenyine murhakanayihuma ko n'omudoke!
LUK 11:47 «Buhanya buchi oku mwabo! Muyumbaka bwinja eshinda z'abaleebi n'obo bashookuluza benyu bababayirhaga!
LUK 11:48 Omu kujira ntyo, muyerekeene oku muyemereere ebijiro bya bashookuluza benyu, bulaala boowe bo bayirhaga abaleebi, nenyu yi mwayumbaka eshinda zaabo!
LUK 11:49 Cho girhumire Nnamahanga omu bwenge bwage bunene aderhere ntya: ‹Nabarhumira abaleebi n'entumwa. Bayirha baguma n'okulibuza abandi.›
LUK 11:50 Cho girhumire echi gisisi nji chaabazwa eshagama yasheeshwaga y'abaleebi booshi gurhengera okulemwa kw'egulu,
LUK 11:51 gurhengera oku shagama ya Abeeli kugera oku shagama ya Zakariya, wayirhwaga ahagarhi k'entuuliro n'ahantu hatagatiifu. Neechi, mbabwirire byo, echi gisisi nji chabazibwa byooshi.
LUK 11:52 «Buhanya buchi oku mwabo bigiriza b'amarhegeko! Mwakuulire olufunguulo loguchingula omulyango g'okuja omu nju y'okuyigira m'okumenya Nnamahanga. Nenyu mwenyine murhajaaga mo, n'abashondaga kuja mo, mwababuza.»
LUK 11:53 Yeesu ayuusize gurhenga ahoola, abigiriza b'amarhegeko n'aBafarisaayo barhondera kumulunza bweneene n'okumubaza oku biyerekeere bintu binene,
LUK 11:54 bashonda kumurhega, yi baabona echinwa chagarhuma bamusidaaka.
LUK 12:1 Amo mango, abantu banene bachigusha bihumbi n'ebihumbi, oku bulyo baalema baalabarhana. Yeesu arhanga kubwira abigirizwa baage ntya: «Muchilange n'echachu y'aBafarisaayo, k'okuderha obulyaalya.
LUK 12:2 «Ntaacho gishukuliirwe girhagashukuulwa, na ntaacho chibishirwe girhakamenyekana.
LUK 12:3 Cho girhumire ngasi byooshi mwaderhere omu mwizimya nji byayunviikana ezuuba lyakola. Echi mwabohereeze omu gurhwi ebusiika, nji chayaamagazizwa oku nju elugulu.
LUK 12:4 «Mwe beera baani, mbabwirire byo: murhayuubahaga abantu bayirha omubiri, na nta chindi bakanachigala kujira enyuma z'aho.
LUK 12:5 Nkola nabayeereka nde mukwaneene kuyuubaha. Muyuubahe Nnamahanga, yegwerhe obuhashe b'okuyirha n'ogukabula omu hantu h'amalibuko manene. Neechi, mbabwirire byo, oyoola yi muhemerwe kuyuubaha.
LUK 12:6 Ka barhaguza nyunyi erhaano z'ebishwa oku bicheri bibiri? Aliko, chiro nta nguma omu zo eyibiriirwe na Nnamahanga.
LUK 12:7 N'enviiri z'amarhwe menyu zooshi ziganjirwe. Leero, murhayuubahaga chiro; mugwerhe akamaro kanene kulusha ebishwa binene.»
LUK 12:8 «Mbabwirire byo: ngasi yeeshi nji wanyemeera embere z'abantu, Mwene oMuntu naye nj'amuyemeera embere za bamalahika ba Nnamahanga.
LUK 12:9 Aliko, ola nji wandahira embere z'abantu, naye nj'alahirwa embere za bamalahika ba Nnamahanga.
LUK 12:10 «Na ngasi yeeshi nji waderhera kubi Mwene oMuntu nj'ababalirwa, aliko ola nji wadukanga Muuka-Mutagatiifu arhakababalirwa.
LUK 12:11 «Hano nji babakululira omu masinagoogi, abarhwali n'abarhegesi, murhayuubahiraga obulyo nji mwabuurana, changwa bichi nji mwaderha.
LUK 12:12 Bulaala Muuka-Mutagatiifu nj'abayigiriza ho n'aho bichi mukwaneene kuderha.»
LUK 12:13 Muntu muguma mw'abo bantu banene abwira Yeesu ntya: «Mwigiriza, bwira mwene weerhu ampe echaani chigabi ch'omwandu gwerhu.»
