LUK 12:14 Yeesu amushubiza ntya: «Muza wee, nde wanjiraga muzuuzi changwa muntu w'okubagabira omwandu gwenyu?»
LUK 12:15 Ashuba kubabwira ntya: «Muchilange n'okugwarha amahugu ma ngasi buuko, kwenge akalamo k'omuntu garharhengeere omu kanji k'ebikulo byaage.»
LUK 12:16 Yeesu ababwira ogu mugani: «Eshwa ly'omugale muguma lyayeeza bweneene.
LUK 12:17 Alema akengeera n'oguchiibaza ntya: ‹Bichi njirage? Bulaala ntagwerhe hantu hanene h'ogushaluulira emyaaka yaani.›
LUK 12:18 Aderha ntya: ‹Tala oku naajira: nashanda enguli zaani, nayumbaka ezigalihire; nji nalundira mo amahemba maani n'ebindi bikulo.›
LUK 12:19 N'enyuma z'aho, nji nachibwira ntya omu murhima: ‹Ngwerhe ebintu binene bweneene bibiikirwe, bya myaaka minene; nahumuuka, naalya, nanywa, naashagaluka.›
LUK 12:20 Aliko Nnamahanga amubwira ntya: ‹Oli muhwinja! M'obu budufu waafa! Ka warheganyize nde nji waaba nyina ebi bintu byooshi wachibikiire?›»
LUK 12:21 Yeesu ashuba kuderha ntya: «Ntyo ku bibeera omuntu ochihakira ebikulo byaage yenyine, aliko eyi arhali mugale embere za Nnamahanga.»
LUK 12:22 Yeesu ashubi bwira abigirizwa baage ntya: «Mulolage egirhumire mbabwira oku murhachiganyaga elugulu w'akalamo kenyu, akaba bichi mwalya; changwa elugulu w'omubiri gwenyu, akaba bichi mwayambala.
LUK 12:23 Bulaala akalamo kali ka bulagiirire kulusha ebiryo, n'omubiri guli gwabulagiirire kulusha emyambalo.
LUK 12:24 Mulole ebihungwe: birhahinga birhanashaluula, birhajira aha bibiikira changwa enguli. Aliko Nnamahanga yebiliisa! Mwabo muli b'akamaro kanene kulusha enyunyi!
LUK 12:25 Nde omu mwabo omu guchiiganya, wakagala kuleehya chiro bugeeke akalamo kaage?
LUK 12:26 Akaba ntaacho mwagachigalira mw'ebi bintu bigeeke, gichi chagarhuma mwachilunza oku bisigeere?
LUK 12:27 Mulole guurhe ebirhi biyaasa: birhakola, birhaluka fulema; aliko, mbabwire oku chiro mwami Solomoono omu bukuuze bwage arhayambalaga nka chiguma omu byo.
LUK 12:28 Akaba Nnamahanga ayambisa ntya egirhi chiri omu shwa zeene n'omuseezi banagiheba omu chibeeye, bichi byaagarhuma arhabayambisa nenyu kulusha, mwe bantu b'obwemeezi bugeeke!
LUK 12:29 Nenyu, murhagendaga mwashonda gichi mwalya changwa gichi mwanywa, murhanachibuliisaga omurhuula.
LUK 12:30 Ebyo byooshi by'abapagaani ba lino gulu bashonda buzira kuluha. Yisho wenyu ayinji oku mubikeneere.
LUK 12:31 Ahuubwe, murhange mushonde obwime bwa Nnamahanga, n'ebyoola bindi naye nj'abaheereza byo.
LUK 12:32 Murhayuubahaga, mwe buso bugeeke; kwenge byasimiisize Yisho okubaha oBwami bwage.»
LUK 12:33 Yeesu ashuba kuderha ntya: «Muguze ebintu byenyu, muhe abakene efuranga. Muchijirire orhushaho rhw'efuranga rhurhagashaaja, muchibiikire ebikulo birhaagahwa omu mpingu. Eyoola nta mwizi wakayegeera yo na nta mushwa gwakabibiihya.
LUK 12:34 Bulaala emunda ebikulo byaawe biri, yi n'omurhima gwawe gwaba guli.»
LUK 12:35 Yeesu ashuba kuderha ntya: «Muchirheganye, mube muyambeere emyambalo y'akaasi n'amatara machaanirwe.
LUK 12:36 Nenyu mube kuguma n'aba bantu bali balinga nnahamwabo agaluke gurhenga oku buhya, hano akongoorha oku lunvi bagale kumuchinguulira jubaajuba.
LUK 12:37 Bagishirwe aba bagaragu nnahamwabo ashimaana bataramire ey'agaluka! Okuli, mbabwirire, naye nj'ayambala emyambalo y'akaasi, nj'abayikaza n'okuyinja kubaha ebiryo.
LUK 12:38 Nk'ayinjire omu budufu ahagarhi changwa buyerekeera gucha, akanababugaana bagitaramire, bagishirwe!»
LUK 12:39 «Mumenye bwinja: nyina enju nk'amenyaga aha saa zinga egishambo chigwasize kuyinja, arhakalekere enju yaage eshandwe.
LUK 12:40 Nenyu leero muchirheganye, bulaala Mwene oMuntu nj'ayinja omu saa murhaganiizize.»
LUK 12:41 Petero abaza Yeesu ntya: «Nnaweerhu, ka rhwewe rh'obwirire ogu mugani changwa abantu booshi?»
LUK 12:42 Nnaweerhu ashubiza ntya: «Nde ye mukozi orhahemuka, na munya bwenge, eyi nnahamwabo akajira mwimangizi w'abandi bakozi baage, y'abaheereza ebiryo omu gashanji gahemerwe?
LUK 12:43 Agishirwe oyu muja, akaba nnahamwabo hano agaluka, amushimaana ali akola ntyo!
LUK 12:44 Okuli mbabwirire: nnahamwabo nj'amujira mwimangizi w'ebikulo byaage byooshi.
LUK 12:45 Aliko, nk'oyo muja achibwirire ntya omu murhima gwage: ‹Nnahamwerhu alegamire kuyinja›, agarhondera gukubirha abaabo baja b'abalume n'aba bakazi, agarhondera kulya, kunywa n'okulaluka,
LUK 12:46 nnahamwabo nj'agaluka olusiku oyo muja arhalikengereere, n'esa arhamenyere. Nj'amuhana bweneene n'okumuyikaza haguma n'abahemusi.
LUK 12:47 «Omuja nji waaba amenyere ogushonda kwa nnahamwabo, aliko arharheganyaga n'okujira echintu chiyerekeere oko gushonda, nj'ashuurhwa enkoni zirhankaganjwa.
LUK 12:48 Sy'aliko, ola orhamenyaga ogushonda kwa nnahamwabo, n'okuba ajirire ebintu bikwaneene obuhane nj'ashuurhwa nkoni zigeeke. Eyi baheere bintu binene, nji baamubaza binene; eyi babikiisize binene, nji bamuhema binene kulusha.»
LUK 12:49 «Nayinjaga guhira omuliro oku gulu; nagashondere gube gwachaanirwe!
LUK 12:50 Nkwaneene kubatiizwa omu malibuko; n'omurhima gwani gurhaviire gwarhuleera kugera birhaza kujirika.»
LUK 12:51 «Ka muganiizize oku nayinjaga kuleerha omurhuula oku gulu? Nangwa, mbabwire okuli, sy'aliko obuhaka.
LUK 12:52 Gurhenga bunoola, bantu barhaano balamire omu nju nguma barhakayunviikana, basharhu nji balwisa babiri, na babiri nji balwisa basharhu.
LUK 12:53 Omwana n'eshe barhakayunviikana, omunyere na nyina barhakayunviikana, omwazaana na nazaala barhakayunviikana.»
LUK 12:54 Yeesu ashuba kubwira olubaga lw'abantu ntya: «Eyi mwabona ebichu byahulukira ebuzikiro bw'ezuuba, ho n'aho mwanaderha: ‹Envula yayinjire›, ebyoola byanahika.
LUK 12:55 Na nk'omuyaga gw'egarhongo guli kugera, mwanaderha: ‹Echuuka chaaba.› Ebyoola byanahika.
LUK 12:56 Mwe ndyaalya! Muyinji kumenya oboorhere bw'egulu n'echaalege. Gurhe mwagafundwa kumenya amango mali bunoola?»
LUK 12:57 «Na girhuma mwenyine murhagala kumenya ebikwaneene?
LUK 12:58 Nka waaja kubuurana n'ogusidaakire embere z'omurhegesi, ochihangaane oyunviikane naye omu njira; y'arhaguheeka embere z'omuzuuzi. Omuzuuzi naye akaguhaana omu maboko m'omupoolisi, n'oyo mupoolisi anaguhira omu munyororo.
LUK 12:59 Okuli nkubwirire, orhagarhenga omu munyororo orhanahongere olufuranga lw'obuzinda omu zibaguchiire.»
LUK 13:1 Amo mango, abantu baguma bayinja kubalira Yeesu gurhe Pilaato ayirhaga aBagalilaaya baguma eyi bali gurhuula entuulo emwa Nnamahanga.
LUK 13:2 Yeesu ababwira ntya: «Mwabo muganiizize kw'abo Bagalilaaya bayirhwaga ntyo, k'okuderha oku bo baligwerhe ebyaaha binene kulusha abandi Bagalilaaya booshi?
LUK 13:3 Mbabwirire oku nangwa. Aliko nka murhalekere ebyaaha byenyu, mweshi nji mwafa kuguma nabo.
LUK 13:4 Changwa, aboola bantu ekumi na munaane omunaara gw'eSilowaamu gwarhogeraga ko, gwanabayirha, muganiizize oku boowe bo baliiri babi bweneene kulusha abandi Banyayerusaleema booshi?
LUK 13:5 Mbabwirire oku nanga. Nenyu nka murhalekere ebyaaha byenyu, mweshi nji mwafa kuguma nabo.»
LUK 13:6 Yeesu ashuba kubabwira guno mugani: «Haliiri muntu muguma waligwerhe omurhi guyirikwa tiini omu shwa lyaage ly'emizabiibu. Aja oku go gushonda amalehe, aliko ntaamo abwene.
LUK 13:7 Ava abwira omuhinzi w'elyo shwa ntya: ‹Lola! Myaaka esharhu eyi ndi nayinja gushonda amalehe k'oguula murhi eyi ntanamabona. Oguche! Chagarhuma gwabeera bushaabusha omu budaka?›
LUK 13:8 Aliko oyo muhinzi anamushubiza ntya: ‹Nnaweerhu, oguleke kandi guno mwaka, mpingire go n'okuguhira kw'emyaavu.
LUK 13:9 Ntyo, nkabaga nji gwaleerha amalehe omu mwaka gwayinjire, akaba birhabeere ntyo, wanagucha!›»
LUK 13:10 Lusiku luguma lw'eSaabato, Yeesu aliiri kuyigiriza omu sinagoogi.
LUK 13:11 Ahoola haliiri omukazi olwere. Gurhengera myaaka ekumi na munaane, omuzimu alimuyinamize. Arhakagalire chiro kuyinamuka.
LUK 13:12 Yeesu abeere amubona, amuhamagala n'okumubwira ntya: «Nyaama wee, endwala yawe yafumire!»
LUK 13:13 Amuhira ko amaboko, ho n'aho ayinamuka n'okuva arhondera gukuuza Nnamahanga.
LUK 13:14 Aliko omukulu w'esinagoogi agaya oku Yeesu afumyize omuntu olusiku lw'eSaabato. Ava abwira echigusho ch'abantu ntya: «Hali siku ndarhu z'ogukola mo akaasi; mw'ezoola siku zimulemage mwayinja mo guchifumiisa, sy'aliko nangwa olusiku lw'eSaabato!»
LUK 13:15 Nnaweerhu amushubiza ntya: «Mwe ndyaalya mwe! Nkaasi muguma wenyu ashwekuula enka yaage changwa epunda yaage n'okuyiheeka gushooka olusiku lw'eSaabato, k'arhali ntyo?
LUK 13:16 N'oyuula mukazi w'obuuko bwa Abrahaamu owalizirikirwe na Shetaani myaaka ekumi na munaane, ka birhahemere ashwekuulwe mw'ebyo biziriko byaage olusiku lw'eSaabato?»
LUK 13:17 Yeesu abeere ali kuderha ntyo, booshi baliiri kumulwisa bayunva eshonyi; aliko echigusho chooshi ch'abantu chamogera ebijiro binja byooshi aliiri kujira.
LUK 13:18 Yeesu ashuba kuderha ntya: «oBwami bwa Nnamahanga bwagashusha na gichi? Nankabushushanya na gichi?
LUK 13:19 Bushusheene n'ehiburho hy'eharadaali muntu muguma arhoolaga anahibyaala omu shwa lyaage. Hyaamera n'ogukula, hyaaba murhi, n'enyunyi z'omu chaalege zayumbaka ebyoogo byaazo omu marhabi maago.»
LUK 13:20 Yeesu ashuba kuderha ntya: «Gichi nankalinganya n'oBwami bwa Nnamahanga?
LUK 13:21 Bulinganeene n'echachu omukazi arhoolaga n'okuyihira omu milengo esharhu y'eshaano y'ogukola emigati, kugera egihe yooshi yarhunda.»
LUK 13:22 Yeesu aliiri omu njira aja eYerusaleema, alenga omu bishagala bineneenene n'ebigeekegeeke ayigiriza.
LUK 13:23 Muntu muguma amubaza ntya: «Nnaweerhu, k'arhali bantu bageeke bonyine nji bachungulwa?» Yeesu ashubiza ntya:
LUK 13:24 «Muchihangaane kuja omu Bwami bwa Nnamahanga kugerera omu mulyango gufundereere. Bulaala, yi nababwira, bantu banene nji bashonda kuja mo aliko barhakagala.
LUK 13:25 Amango nyina enju nj'aba ayimangire ey'amanachinga omulyango, nji mwaba mwamasigala embuga. Nji mwarhondera gukongoorha oku mulyango n'okuderha ntya: ‹Nnaweerhu, orhuchinguulire.› Nj'abashubiza ntya: ‹Mwabo, ntenji muli ba ngahe.›
LUK 13:26 Ho n'aho, nji mwamubwira ntya: ‹Rhwaliire rhwananywa haguma naawe, wanagendaga wayigiriza emwerhu!›
LUK 13:27 Naye nj'ababwira ntya: ‹Ntenji muli ba ngahe. Muje hale naani, mweshi mwe mukola amabi!›
LUK 13:28 Eyoola nji yaaba amalira n'oguhekenya amenyo, amo mango nji mwabona Abrahaamu, Isaka na Yakobo, n'abaleebi booshi omu Bwami bwa Nnamahanga, aliko mwabo nji mwaba mwakabwirwe embuga!
LUK 13:29 Abantu nji barhengera ebuhulukiro bw'ezuuba n'ebuzikiro bwalyo, n'abandi gurhengera emalambo n'egarhongo n'okuyikala balye haguma omu Bwami bwa Nnamahanga.
LUK 13:30 Mumenye oku hali abazinda nji baaba barhanzi, hali n'abarhanzi nji baaba bazinda.»
LUK 13:31 Mw'ebyoola bishanji, aBafarisaayo baguma bayegeera Yeesu n'okumubwira ntya: «Rhenga hano, ochigendere ahandi, bulaala Heroode yashonda gukuyirha.»
LUK 13:32 Yeesu abashubiza ntya: «Mugende mujibwira ogoola mutereri ntya: ‹Yi nalibisya abazimu n'ogufumya abalwala zeene n'omuseezi. Na lishinjo naamala akaasi kaani.›
LUK 13:33 Aliko bihemere ngendekere olugenzi lwani zeene, omuseezi na lishinjo, bulaala birhakwaneene kuyirhira omuleebi ahandi aharhali eYerusaleema.»
LUK 13:34 «Yerusaleema, Yerusaleema, wooyo weyirha abaleebi n'okubanda amabaale abantu Nnamahanga agurhumiraga! Kanga nashondaga guhira haguma abaana baawe nk'oku engoko ehira haguma ebyaanagoko byaayo omu byuubi byaayo! Aliko murhabilonzaga.
LUK 13:35 Mumenye okw'enju yenyu yaaba mushaka. Mbabwirire byo: murhagachimbona kugera amango hayinja egihe nji mwaderha ntya: ‹Nnamahanga agishe owayinja oku ziino lya Nnaweerhu!›»
LUK 14:1 Lusiku luguma lw'eSaabato, Yeesu aja kulya emwa muguma w'abakulu b'aBafarisaayo. Abaliiri ho booshi baliiri bamuloleereza.
LUK 14:2 Omuntu olwere endwala y'ogurhundiisa omubiri aliiri embere za Yeesu.
LUK 14:3 Yeesu abaza abigiriza b'amarhegeko n'aBafarisaayo ntya: «K'amarhegeko meerhu mayemereere changwa nangwa omuntu ogufumya omulwala olusiku lw'eSaabato?»
LUK 14:4 Aliko baasira. Yeesu ava arhoola oyo mulwala, amufumya n'okumuleka agende.
LUK 14:5 Ashuba kubabaza ntya: «Nde omu mwabo nk'omugala changwa enka yaage egarhogera omu gishimu, ka ho n'aho arhakayikuula mo nachiro luli lusiku lw'eSaabato?»
LUK 14:6 Baabula echi bamushubiza.
LUK 14:7 Yeesu abeere abona gurhe abalaalikirwe yi bachiishoga ebichumbi by'embere, abachiira ogu mugani:
LUK 14:8 «Nk'omuntu aguhamageere kuja kulya amango m'obuhya, orhajaaga kuyikala oku gichumbi ch'embere. Bulaala hali amango omuntu okengerwe gukulusha alaalikirwe,
LUK 14:9 owabalaalikaga wooyo n'owenyu akayinja gukubwira ntya: ‹Olekere oyuula muntu egichumbi.› Wanaja wagwarhwa n'eshoni z'okuja kuyikala oku gichumbi ch'enyuma.
LUK 14:10 Aliko, amango olaalikirwe, wanaja kuyikala oku gichumbi ch'enyuma, y'amango hano owakulaalikaga ayinja, akubwire ntya: ‹Mwira waani, oje kuyikala oku gichumbi ch'embere!› Ntyo, nji bwakubeera bukenge embere z'abantu booshi nji baaba bayikeere haguma naawe oku meeza.
LUK 14:11 Bulaala ngasi yeeshi ochizamwire nj'ayandagazwa, n'ochiyandageeze nj'azamuulwa.»
LUK 14:12 Yeesu ashuba kubwira ola wamulaalikaga ntya: «Amango warheganyiza abantu ebiryo by'ezuuba changwa by'egolo, orhalaalikaga abeera baawe, changwa beene benyu, changwa abantu b'omulala gwawe, changwa abatuuranyi baawe b'abachire. Bulaala nabo nji bakayinja gukulaalika, na ntyo wanaba wamajuhwa.
LUK 14:13 Aliko amango wahamagala abantu kulya oku lusiku lukulu, olaalike abakeene, ebirema, abahunzize n'empumi.
LUK 14:14 Ntyo, nji waaba mugishwa, kwenge boowe barhagwerhe echi bagakujuha omu gukugalulira! Aliko, nji waajuhwa amango m'ogufuuka kw'abakwaneene.»
LUK 14:15 Muntu muguma omu baliiri baalya haguma na Yeesu abeere ayunva ebyo binwa, aderha ntya: «Agishirwe ola nji waalya omu Bwami bwa Nnamahanga!»
LUK 14:16 Yeesu amushubiza ntya: «Haliiri muntu muguma warheganyaga biryo binene, analaalika bantu banene.
LUK 14:17 Egihe ch'okulya chagerere ho, arhuma omuja waage kubwira abalaalikirwe: ‹Muyinje, byooshi byarheganyizwe.›
LUK 14:18 Aliko booshi barhondera kuderha ngasi muguma echaarhuma arhabonekana. Omwambere amubwira ntya: ‹Nagulaga eshwa, bimpemere nje kulirhangula; nguhemere ombabalire.›
LUK 14:19 Owindi aderha ntya: ‹Nagulaga enka ekumi z'oguhingiisa, nguhemere ombabalire, naaja kulola akaba zaakola.›
LUK 14:20 Owindi aderha ntya: ‹Namayuusa gushaba, chocharhuma ntayinja!›
LUK 14:21 Oyo muja agaluka emwa nnahamwabo, amubalira ebyo byooshi. Nnahamwabo akaliha, abwira oyo omuja waage ntya: ‹Genda juba omu njira zineneenene n'omu zigekegeeke z'egishagala, oleerhe hano abakene, ebirema, empumi n'abahunzize.›
LUK 14:22 Omuja abeere amala kujira ntyo, aderha ntya: ‹Nnaweerhu, ebi wahemaga byajirirwe, aliko hanachiri ahakayikalwa!›
LUK 14:23 Nnahamwabo ava amubwira ntya: ‹Oje omu njira n'omu migenderano y'egishagala, oseeze abantu bayinje kuja omu nju, y'omu mwani muyunjula abantu.
LUK 14:24 Kwenge, mbabwirire byo, ntaaye mw'aba bantu bali balaalikirwe nji waalya oku biryo byaani.›»
LUK 14:25 Lusiku luguma abantu banene baliiri kulambagira haguma na Yeesu omu njira. Ahindamuka n'okubabwira ntya:
LUK 14:26 «Nk'omuntu ankulikiire arhanansiimire kulusha eshe, nyina, mukaage, abaana baage, beene baabo, bali baabo, chiro n'akalamo kaage, arhaakaba mwigirizwa waani.
LUK 14:27 N'omuntu orhaheekere omusalaaba gwage n'okunkulikira, arhaakaba mwigirizwa waani.
LUK 14:28 «Nde omu mwabo, nk'ashondere kuyumbaka enju nene, arharhanga kuyikala aganje engulo y'ebyakoleesa n'okulola akaba agwerhe ebikulo by'okuyiyunjuza?
LUK 14:29 Kwenge, nk'arhondeere kuyumbaka n'akaba arhagalire kumala, aba nji baabona ntyo, nji bamushekera.
LUK 14:30 Baderha ntya: ‹Oyu muntu arhondeere kuyumbaka, aliko agambirwe kuyunjuza.›
LUK 14:31 Changwa mwami ohe, nk'ashondere kulwisa owindi mwami, orharhanga kuyikala n'oguchiibaza akaba oku misi y'abasoda baage bihumbi ekumi, akagala guhima oyo waabo oyinjire na basoda bihumbi makumyaabiri?
LUK 14:32 Akaba arhakagala, agarhumira oyo waabo abantu achiri hale b'okumubaza gurhe bakayunviikana n'omurhuula gube ho.
LUK 14:33 Nenyu ntyo kubinali! Ngasi yeeshi omu mwabo nk'arhalekere ebikulo byaage byooshi arhaakaba mwigirizwa waani.»
LUK 14:34 «Omunyu chiri chintu gikwiriire. Sy'aliko gugaheza obuloke, gurhe bakagugalulira bo?
LUK 14:35 Gurhachiri gwinja oku budaka changwa oku myaavu; banagukabula embuga. Ogwerhe amarhwi m'okuyunva, ayunve!»
LUK 15:1 Abafurhiisa b'amakooli n'abanyabyaaha baliiri kuyegeera Yeesu yi bamuyunviriza.
LUK 15:2 aBafarisaayo n'abigiriza b'amarhegeko babeere baabona ntyo, bamuveeba ntya: «Oyu muntu y'ayankirira abanyabyaaha n'okulya nabo!»
LUK 15:3 Aliko Yeesu abachiira ogu mugani:
LUK 15:4 «Nde omu mwabo, nk'agwerhe ntaama egana, agaheza nguma omu zo, k'arhakaleka zila zindi makumi gali mwenda na mwenda omu mpinga y'aja gushonda ela eherere kugera amango ayibona?
LUK 15:5 N'akayibona, anayihira oku birhugo byaage n'obushagaluke bunene,
LUK 15:6 anagaluka emwage, anahamagala beera baage n'abatuuranyi baage n'okubabwira ntya: ‹Mushagaluke haguma naani, bulaala nabwene entaama yaani yali herere.›
LUK 15:7 Na ntyo mbabwirire byo, nji haaba obushagaluke bunene omu mpingu oku munyabyaaha muguma olekere ebyaaha byaage, ahaali h'abantu makumi gali mwenda na mwenda bakwaneene barhakeneere okuleka ebyaaha byaabo.»
LUK 15:8 Yeesu ashuba kuderha ntya: «Mukazi muchi, nk'agwerhe bicheri ekumi by'efuranga n'agaheza gicheri kiguma, k'arhagachaana etara, agahyaagira enju n'agashonda bwinjabwinja kugera amango achibona?
LUK 15:9 Na hano abona echo gicheri, anahamagala abeerakazi n'abatuuranyi baage n'okuderha ntya: ‹Mushagaluke haguma naani, bulaala nabwene egicheri chaani ch'efuranga nalihezeze!›
LUK 15:10 Mbabwirire byo oku ntyo ku bamalahika ba Nnamahanga banashagaluka nk'omunyabyaaha muguma alekere ebyaaha byaage.»
LUK 15:11 Yeesu ashuba kuderha ntya: «Haliiri muntu muguma waligwerhe bagala babiri.
LUK 15:12 Omudoorho abwira eshe ntya: ‹Daarha, ompe echaani chigabi ch'agashambala chikwaneene kuba chaani.› Eshe abagabira bombi.
LUK 15:13 Enyuma wa siku zigeeke, omugala mudoorho aguza omwandu gwage n'okugenda omu gihugo cha hale. Mw'echo gihugo ashandaguza ebikulo byaage omu boorhere bubi.
LUK 15:14 Amalire kubishandaguza byooshi, enzara nene yaba mw'echo gihugo, arhondera kubula ngasi chintu.
LUK 15:15 Aja agenda gukolera omuntu muguma w'echo gihugo. Oyo muntu amurhuma omu mashwa maage kulagira engulube.
LUK 15:16 Oyo murhabana alema agifiija kulya oku biryo by'engulube sy'aliko ntaaye wamuheere byo.
LUK 15:17 Buzinda agishuba ko, aderha ntya: ‹Abakozi booshi ba daarha bali omu muhimbo, n'obo nyoono hano ndi naafa n'enzara!
LUK 15:18 Nagaluka emwa daarha, nanamubwira ntya: “Daarha, najirire echaaha embere za Nnamahanga n'embere zaawe.
LUK 15:19 Ntachikwaneene kuyirikwa mugala waawe. Oje wantoola nka muguma w'omu bakozi baawe.”›
LUK 15:20 Ava agaluka, aja emw'eshe. «Abeere achiri hale n'aha mwabo, eshe amulangiira, amuyunvira obonjo bunene. Alibirha kumulinga, amuhoobera.
LUK 15:21 Omugala aj'amubwira ntya: ‹Daarha, najirire echaaha emwa Nnamahanga n'emwawe, ntachikwaneene guhamagalwa mugala waawe.›
LUK 15:22 Aliko eshe abwira abaja baage ntya: ‹Muyanguhe, muleerhe omwambalo gukwiriire bweneene mumuyambise go, mumuyambise olupeta oku mudoke munamuyambise ebiraato.
LUK 15:23 Muleerhe enyana eshishire muyibaage; rhujire edinye rhunasiime,
LUK 15:24 bulaala oyu mugala waani abaaga afiire leero afuukire, abaaga aherere leero abonekere.› Banarhondera edinye.
LUK 15:25 «Mw'ako gashanji, omugala w'efula aliiri omu shwa. Abeere agaluka, n'okuyegeera aha mwabo, ayunva abantu bali kuyimpa n'okuzina.
LUK 15:26 Ahamagala muguma omu bakozi b'eshe, amubaza bichi byabeere.
LUK 15:27 Omukozi amubwira ntya: ‹Mudoorho waawe agalukire bobunoola yisho ayirhire enyana eshishire, bulaala amubwene mugumaguma.›
LUK 15:28 Oyo mugala w'efula ayunva oburhe, alahira kuja omu nju. Eshe ahuluka kumurhebeereza aje mo.
LUK 15:29 Aliko abwira eshe ntya: ‹Tala! Hamaagera myaaka minene bweneene eyi ndi nagukolera. Ntashubiraga kuvuna erhegeko lyaawe chiro n'eliguma. N'obo orhashubiraga kumpa chiro omwana gw'empene yi nshagaluka haguma na beera baani.
LUK 15:30 Aliko oyu mugala waawe wahezeze ebikulo byaawe omu bubaraga, abeere agaluka, wamubagiire enyana eshishire!›
LUK 15:31 Eshe amubwira ntya: ‹Mwana waani, oli haguma naani esiku zooshi, na byooshi ngwerhe biri byaawe.
LUK 15:32 Sy'aliko byaalihemere rhujire edinye n'ogushagaluka, bulaala oyu mwene wenyu abaaga afiire, aliko afuukire; abaaga aherere, aliko abonekere!›»
LUK 16:1 Yeesu ashuba kubwira abigirizwa baage ntya: «Haliiri omuchire muguma waligwerhe omwimangizi w'ebikulo byaage. Abantu bayinja gusidaaka oyo mwimangizi emwa nnahamwabo oku agwerhe ashandaguza ebikulo byaage.
LUK 16:2 Nnahamwabo amuhamagala n'okumubwira ntya: ‹Bichi ndi nayunva baderha elugulu waawe? Nyeerekaga oluganjo lw'ebikulo byaani, bulaala orhagachiba mwimangizi wabyo.›
LUK 16:3 Oyo mwimangizi aderha ntya omu murhima gwage: ‹Nnahamwerhu akola kunyaga akaasi kaani. Bichi njirage? Ntaviire nakoomera oguhinga amashwa na kandi nji nagwarha eshoni z'oguhemuuza.
LUK 16:4 Ahaa! Namaamenya echi naajira, yi haboneka abanyankiirira emwa baabo hano nkuulwa oku kaasi kaani.›
LUK 16:5 Aja ahamagala ngasi muguma waligwerhe omwinda gwa nnahamwabo. Abaza omwambere ntya: ‹Mwinda munganachi gwa nnahamwerhu ogwerhe?›
LUK 16:6 Amushubiza ntya: ‹Nkunguru egana z'amavurha.› Oyo mwimangizi w'ebikulo amubwira ntya: ‹Rhoola aka karataasi kayandikirwe k'omwinda gwawe; yikala juba oyandike nkunguru makumi marhaano.›
LUK 16:7 Ashuba kubwira owindi ogwerhe omwinda: ‹Naawe mwinda munganachi gwa nnahamwerhu ogwerhe?› Amushubiza ntya: ‹Bigunira egana by'amahemba.› Omwimangizi w'ebikulo amubwira ntya: ‹Rhoola aka karataasi kayandikirwe k'omwinda gwawe; yikala juba onayandike makumi gali munaane.›
LUK 16:8 Nyina ebikulo asiima omwimangizi muhemusi, bulaala akolere n'obwenge. Bulaala, abantu b'eri gulu bayanguha omu bijiro byaabo kulusha abantu b'obumoleke.»
LUK 16:9 Yeesu ashuba kuderha ntya: «Nyoono mbabwirire ntya: Muchijirire abeera haguma n'obuchire bubi bw'eri gulu, yi hano muba murhachigwerhe obuchire, abantu babayankiirire omu biikalo by'esiku n'amango.
LUK 16:10 «Omuntu orhali muhemusi omu bintu bigeeke eyi arhanali muhemusi omu bintu binene; n'omuntu muhemusi omu bintu bigeeke eyi anali muhemusi omu bintu binene.
LUK 16:11 Akaba leero mwabeere bantu bahemusi omu buchire bw'eri gulu, nde nji wabajira bimangizi b'obuchire bw'okuli?
LUK 16:12 N'akaba mwabeere bantu bahemusi omu bintu byabeene, nde nji wabaheereza ebintu bababikiire?
LUK 16:13 «Nta muja wakagala gukolera ba shoobuja babiri: changwa anagaya muguma n'ogusiima owindi, changwa anagishwekera oku muguma n'okuboneerera owindi. Murhakagala gukolera Nnamahanga, munakolere ebikulo.»
LUK 16:14 aBafarisaayo babeere bayunva ebi binwa byooshi, barhondera gushekera Yeesu, bulaala basiimaga efuranga.
LUK 16:15 Yeesu ababwira ntya: «Muli bantu bachiyeerekana nka ab'okuli embere z'abantu, aliko Nnamahanga ayinji emirhima yenyu. Bulaala, ech'abantu barhoolere nka gikwaneene, chiba chigayisize Nnamahanga.
LUK 16:16 «Egihe ch'eRhegeko lya Muusa n'ebitaabu by'abaleebi chagendekeere kugera amango ma Yohaana Mubatiiza. Gurhengera amo mango, oMwazi Mwinja g'oBwami bwa Nnamahanga gwayamageezwe na ngasi muntu y'alwisa kuja mo.
LUK 16:17 Aliko byakayolohera empingu n'egulu guhirima, ahaali h'ehinwa hityuuli hy'eRhegeko lya Nnamahanga hirhenge.
LUK 16:18 «Ngasi mulume wayegwire mukaage n'agashaba owindi, eyi ajirire obuhushi, n'oshabire omukazi bayegwire, eyi naye ajirire obuhushi.»
LUK 16:19 «Haliiri mulume muguma w'omugale wagendaga ayambala emyambalo edukwire y'engulo nene. Oyo mugale agendaga ajira edinye ngasi lusiku.
LUK 16:20 Haliiri n'omukene muguma oyirikwa Lazaaro wabaaga alyaama embere w'omulyango gw'enju yaage. Omubiri gwa Lazaaro gwali guyunjwire ebihulu.
LUK 16:21 Lazaaro aliiri guchifiija kulya orhuboole rhw'ebiryo rhwagendaga rhwarhoga oku meeza m'oyo mugale. Na kandi embwa zagenda zayinja kumiima ebihulu byaage.
LUK 16:22 Hagera olusiku oyo mukene afa. Bamalahika bamuheeka ahaburhambi bw'Abrahaamu. Ola mugale naye afa, bamuhamba.
LUK 16:23 Agerere ekuzimu, alibuka bweneene. Ayinamula ameesho, alangiira Abrahaamu na Lazaaro ali eburhambi bwage.
LUK 16:24 Ava ayaama ntya: ‹Daarha Abrahaamu, ombeere obonjo; obwire Lazaaro ahire esongi ly'omudoke gwage omu menji, ambobeeze olulimi, bulaala ndi nalibuka bweneene m'ogu muliro.›
LUK 16:25 Aliko Abrahaamu amushubiza ntya: ‹Mwana waani, yibuka oku waliyankiriire bintu binja binene omu kalamo kaawe, aliko Lazaaro yeewe aligwerhe malibuko manene. Bunoola, yeewe y'arhuleerezwa, aliko wooyo yi walibuka.
LUK 16:26 Na kandi, hali omuhonga guleehere bweneene ahagarhi kenyu neerhu. Cho girhumire, abashondere gurhenga eno kuja emunda muli barhakabigala. Na kandi ntaaye wakagala kugera eno munda rhuli gurhengera eyo munda muli.›
LUK 16:27 Omugale aderha ntya: ‹Daarha wee, nguhemere n'obonjo, orhume Lazaaro omu mwerhu;
LUK 16:28 bulaala ngwerhe beene beerhu barhaano, aje kubahanuula yi nji barhayinja nabo hano hantu h'amalibuko.›
LUK 16:29 Abrahaamu amushubiza ntya: ‹Beene benyu bagwerhe ebitaabu bya Muusa na eby'abaleebi, babiyunve.›
LUK 16:30 Omugale aderha ntya: ‹Nangwa, daarha Abrahaamu, aliko nk'omuntu muguma afuukire akaja emunda bali, bakaleka ebyaaha byaabo.›
LUK 16:31 Aliko Abrahaamu abwira omugale ntya: ‹Akaba barhashondere kuyunva Muusa n'abaleebi, barhakayemeera chiro omuntu wafuukire gurhenga omu bafu.›»
LUK 17:1 Yeesu abwira abigirizwa baage ntya: «Ntaako byankaba yi habula ebyaarhuma abantu baajira ebyaaha, aliko buhanya buchi oku omuntu nji waaba mpanvu y'okujira echaaha!
LUK 17:2 Kwakabeere kwinja oku yeewe, ashwekerwe olushyo omu gosi, anakabulwe omu nyanja, ahaali h'ogurhuma muguma mw'aba badoorho ajira echaaha.
LUK 17:3 Muchilange bwinja mwenyine! «Akaba mwene wenyu akujiriire echaaha, omuhanuule. Akaleka ebyaaha byaage, omubabalire.
LUK 17:4 N'akaba akujiriire echaaha kali mushanvu omu lusiku, n'akayinja emunda oli kali mushanvu gukubwira ntya: ‹Nalekere ebyaaha byaani›, omubabalire.»
LUK 17:5 Entumwa zabwira Nnaweerhu ntya: «Orhuyushuulire obwemeezi.»
LUK 17:6 Nnaweerhu ashubiza ntya: «Nka mwaligwerhe chiro obwemeezi bugeeke kuguma n'ehiburho hye haradaali, mwakabwirire ogu murhi gw'agafuleesi ntya: ‹Chikundula onaje guchibyaala omu nyanja›, gwakanabakengere.»
LUK 17:7 Yeesu ashuba kuderha ntya: «Nka muntu muguma omu mwabo agwerhe omuja ohinga eshwa changwa olagira ebirhungano byaage, hano amubona agaluka gurhenga omu shwa, k'akamubwira ayinje juba alye?
LUK 17:8 Nangwa, ahuubwe akamubwira ntya: ‹Nvuyira ebyaani biryo, onayambale bwinja, ompe ndye nanywe; naawe handeke walya onanywe buzinda.›
LUK 17:9 Arhagasiimiriza omuja waage okw'ajirire eby'alirhegekerwe kujira, k'arhali ntyo?
LUK 17:10 Nenyu ntyo kubinali: hano nji muba mwamakola byooshi bibarhegekerwe, muderhe ntya: ‹Rhuli baja barhagwerhe kamaro, hoshaaho rhwajirire ebi rhwalihemerwe kujira.›»
LUK 17:11 Yeesu abeere ali omu njira aja eYerusaleema, agera eburhambirhambi b'olubibi lugabire eSamariya n'eGalilaaya.
LUK 17:12 Abeere aja omu gishagala chiguma, ababenzibenzi ekumi bayinja kumushimaana. Bayimanga hale naye.
LUK 17:13 Barhondera kuyaama ntya: «Yeesu, Mwigiriza, orhubeere obonjo!»
LUK 17:14 Yeesu abeere ababona, ababwira ntya: «Muje guchiyeerekana emw'abadaahwa.» Babeere bali baaja yo, baava baafuma.
LUK 17:15 Muguma omu bo, abeere abona afumire, agaluka akuuza Nnamahanga n'omulenge munene.
LUK 17:16 Achikabula embere z'amagulu ma Yeesu, amalanga oku budaka, amubwira kooko. Oyu muntu aliiri Musamariya.
LUK 17:17 Yeesu ava aderha ntya: «K'arhali booshi ekumi baafumaga? Ngahe bandi mwenda bali?
LUK 17:18 Ka ntaaye wakengereere kugaluka gukuuza Nnamahanga, kuleka oyu orhali Muyaahudi?»
LUK 17:19 Yeesu aja amubwira ntya: «Yimanga ogende, obwemeezi bwawe bwaguchungwire.»
LUK 17:20 aBafarisaayo baabaza Yeesu ntya: «Mango machi oBwami bwa Nnamahanga nji bwayinja?» Yeesu abashubiza ntya: «oBwami bwa Nnamahanga burhayinja bwachitaragaza.
LUK 17:21 Abantu barhakaderha ntya: ‹Mulolage! oBwami bwa Nnamahanga buli hano!›, changwa: ‹Buli halira!› Bulaala, mumenyage bwinja, oBwami bwa Nnamahanga buli ahagarhi kenyu.»
LUK 17:22 Yeesu ashuba kubwira abigirizwa baage ntya: «Agashanji kayinja nji mwachifiija kubona Mwene oMuntu chiro lusiku luguma, aliko nji murhamubona.
LUK 17:23 «Abantu nji bababwira ntya: ‹Ali haliira!›, changwa: ‹Ali hano!› Murhalibirhiraga yo.
LUK 17:24 Nka kula omubaraganyo gubaraganya omu nkuba gurhengera omu luhande luguma guhika omu lwindi, ntyo ku Mwene oMuntu nj'aba omu olusiku lwage.
LUK 17:25 Aliko embere Mwene oMuntu agaluke, bihemere alibuke bweneene analahirwe n'echi gisisi.
LUK 17:26 «Nk'oku byabaaga omu siku za Noowa, ku nji byaaba amango Mwene oMuntu nj'agaluka.
LUK 17:27 Abantu bagendaga baalya n'okunywa, bagendaga baashaba n'ogushabwa, kugera oku lusiku Noowa ajaaga omu nkuge. Leero emisuuka minene yahulula, yabazisya booshi.
LUK 17:28 «Kandi nji byaaba kuguma n'esiku za Looti: abantu bagendaga baalya n'okunywa, bagendaga baagula n'okuguza, bagendaga bahinga n'okuyumbaka.
LUK 17:29 Sy'aliko olusiku Looti arhengaga eSodoomo, omuliro n'ebiseese byarhoga gurengera oku nkuba nka nvula, byayirha abantu booshi.
LUK 17:30 Kandi ntyo ku nji byaaba olusiku Mwene oMuntu nj'agaluka.
LUK 17:31 «Olo lusiku, omuntu nji waaba ali oku nju elugulu, arhajaaga omu nju gurhoola ebintu byaage. N'ola muntu nji waaba ali omu shwa lyaage arhachigalukaga emwage.
LUK 17:32 Muyibuke ebyahikiraga muka Looti!
LUK 17:33 Omuntu nji washonda kulanga akalamo kaage nj'agaheza; aliko omuntu nji washonda kugaheza nj'akalanga.
LUK 17:34 «Mbabwirire, m'obo budufu, bantu babiri nji baaba balyaamire oku buliri buguma: muguma nj'aheekwa, owindi nj'alekwa.
LUK 17:35 Bakazi babiri nji baaba bali basyera haguma: muguma nj'aheekwa, owindi nj'alekwa. [
LUK 17:36 Bantu babiri nji baaba bali omu shwa: muguma nj'aheekwa, owindi nj'alekwa.»]
LUK 17:37 Abigirizwa baabaza Yeesu ntya: «Nnaweerhu, ngahe ebyo nji byabeera?» Naye abashubiza ntya: «Ahali omurhumba, ho hagwirira banyunda.»
LUK 18:1 Yeesu ashuba guchiira abigirizwa baage ogu mugani y'abayeereka oku bakwaneene gusaliira buzira kuluha.
LUK 18:2 Aderha ntya: «Omu gishagala chiguma haliiri omuzuuzi muguma orhayuubahaga Nnamahanga na nta muntu akengaga.
LUK 18:3 Kandi mw'echo gishagala haliiri omushumbakazi muguma wagendaga aja kubwira oyo muzuuzi ntya: ‹Onchiire bwinja olushinja n'omushombanyi waani!›
LUK 18:4 Halenga siku zinene alahiire kumuchiira lo. Aliko buzinda achibwira ntya: ‹Nachiro mpu ntayuubaha Nnamahanga na nta muntu nkenga,
LUK 18:5 aliko bunoola oyu mushumbakazi ali andunza, namuchiira bwinja olushinja lwage, arhayinja kumbera erhwe.›»
LUK 18:6 Nnaweerhu aja aderha ntya: «Muyunve bwinja eby'oyu muzuuzi muhemusi aderhere!
LUK 18:7 Ka Nnamahanga yeewe arhagachiira bwinja olushinja abantu baage achishogere, n'obo bali bamulilira ezuuba n'obudufu? Ka nj'alegama kubarhabaala?
LUK 18:8 Mbabwirire oku Nnamahanga nj'abachiira bwinja olushinja jubaajuba. Sy'aliko amango Mwene oMuntu nj'agaluka, ka nj'abugaana obwemeezi omu gulu?»
LUK 18:9 Yeesu ashuba gucha ogu mugani oku bantu baliiri guchiibona oku bakwaneene n'ogukena abandi bantu:
LUK 18:10 «Lusiku luguma, bantu babiri baja gusaliira omu Nju ya Nnamahanga. Muguma aliiri Mufarisaayo n'owindi aliiri mufurhiisa w'amakooli.
LUK 18:11 oMufarisaayo ayimanga, asaliira ntya omu murhima gwage: ‹Nnamahanga wee, nguheere obukuuze bulaala ntali kuguma n'abandi bantu. Boowe bali bishumuusi, barhakwaneene, bali bahushi. Kandi ntali kuguma n'oyu mufurhiisa w'amakooli.
LUK 18:12 Nanchiibuza kulya kabiri omu boso, nampaana chigabi chiguma ch'ekumi ch'ebintu mbona.›
LUK 18:13 Aliko omufurhiisa w'amakooli yeewe, aliyimangire hale. Chiro arhanagalaga kuyinamula ameesho elugulu, sy'aliko achishuurha egifuba omu kuyeerekana oku arhakwaneene. Aderha ntya: ‹Yoo! Nnamahanga, ombeere obonjo, nye munyabyaaha!›
LUK 18:14 Yeesu aja aderha ntya: ‹Mbabwirire, oyu mufurhiisa w'amakooli yi wagalukire emwage ey'akwaneene, si arhali ola Mufarisaayo. Kwenge ngasi muntu yeeshi wachizamuula nj'ayandagazwa, aliko ola wachiyandagaza nj'azamuulwa.›»
LUK 18:15 Bantu baguma baleerhera Yeesu enjolyaana nazo mpu azigishe omu kuzihira kw'amaboko. Abigirizwa baage babeere baabona ntyo, bakalihira abo bantu.
LUK 18:16 Aliko Yeesu arhegeka oku bamuleerhere abo baana n'okuderha ntya: «Muleke abaana bayinje emunda ndi! Murhababuzaga, bulaala oBwami bwa Nnamahanga buli bw'abantu bali kuguma nabo.
LUK 18:17 Mbabwirire okuli: omuntu orhayankiriire oBwami bwa Nnamahanga nka mwana mudoorho arhakabuja mo chiro n'ehityu.»
LUK 18:18 Omukulu muguma w'aBayaahudi abaza Yeesu ntya: «Mwigiriza mwinja, bichi ngwasize kujira yi mbona akalamo k'esiku n'amango?»
LUK 18:19 Yeesu amushubiza ntya: «Gurhe wankanyirika mwinja? Nta muntu mwinja, arhali Nnamahanga yenyine.
LUK 18:20 Sy'omenyere amarhegeko: ‹Orhahushaga, orhayirhaga, orhazimbaga, orhahamiirizaga obubeeshi, okenge yisho na nyoko.›»
LUK 18:21 Oyo mukulu ashubiza ntya: «Ama marhegeko mooshi namakengere gurhenga ndi musole.»
LUK 18:22 Yeesu abeere ayunva ntyo, amubwira ntya: «Hachikubuliire kandi chintu chiguma: oguze ebintu byooshi ogwerhe, efuranga zarhenga mo ozigabire abakene, nji wanaja wagwarha obuchire omu mpingu. Wanaja wayinja n'okunkulikira.»
LUK 18:23 Aliko oyo muntu abeere ayunva ntyo, agaya bweneene, bulaala aliiri muchire bweneene.
LUK 18:24 Yeesu abwene oku agayire, aderha ntya: «Okuli, bikomereere abachire kuja omu Bwami bwa Nnamahanga!
LUK 18:25 Bulaala kuyoloheere bweneene engamiya kugera omu hirhule hy'esindani ahaali h'omugale kuja omu Bwami bwa Nnamahanga.»
LUK 18:26 Abantu baliiri bamuyunviriza baderha ntya: «Nde leero wagachungulwa?»
LUK 18:27 Yeesu ashubiza ntya: «Ebirhakagalika oku bantu byakagalika emwa Nnamahanga.»
LUK 18:28 Petero aja aderha ntya: «Tala oku rhwewe rhwalekere ebintu rhwali rhugwerhe yi rhugukulikira.»
LUK 18:29 Yeesu ababwira ntya: «Mbabwire okuli, nta muntu walekere enju, mukaage, beene baabo, abazeere baage changwa abaana baage elugulu w'obwime bwa Nnamahanga,
LUK 18:30 orhakayankirira ebintu binene mu mano mango, n'omu siku zayinja nj'abona akalamo k'esiku n'amango.»
LUK 18:31 Buzinda bw'aho, Yeesu arhoola zila ntumwa zaage ekumi n'ebiri n'okuzibwira ntya: «Tala oku rhwazamuukira eYerusaleema; byooshi byayandikwaga n'abaleebi bilolere Mwene oMuntu byajirika.
LUK 18:32 Bulaala nj'ahaanwa oku barhali Bayaahudi. Nji bamushinyagulira, nji bamulibuza, nji bamuchiira ko,
LUK 18:33 nji bamushuurha, nji banamuyirha. N'olusiku lwa gasharhu nj'afuuka.»
LUK 18:34 Aliko barhayunvaga eby'echi chinwa chiderhere, bulaala byaali bishirwe. Barhaalimenyere bichi Yeesu ashondaga kuderha.
LUK 18:35 Amango Yeesu ayegeeraga egishagala ch'eYeeriko, haliiri empumi nguma yali yikeere eburhambi bw'enjira ey'eri yahemuuza.
LUK 18:36 Eyo mpumi yayunva abantu banene yi baagera, yanabaza bichi byabeere.
LUK 18:37 Bayishubiza ntya: «Yeesu w'eNazareeti yeeri kulenga.»
LUK 18:38 Empumi yaliika omulenge: «Yeesu, Mwene Daawudi, ombeere obonjo!»
LUK 18:39 Abaliiri balambagira embere bayikalihira yi bayisizya, aliko yayaama bweneene: «Mwene Daawudi, ombeere obonjo!»
LUK 18:40 Yeesu ayimanga n'ogurhegeka oku bayileerhere ye. Empumi yabeere yaagera hoofu naye, Yeesu ayibaza ntya:
LUK 18:41 «Gichi oshondere nkujirirage?» Yashubiza ntya: «Nnaweerhu, nshube mbone.»
LUK 18:42 Yeesu ayishubiza ntya: «Shuba kubona; obwemeezi bwawe bwagufumize.»
LUK 18:43 Ho n'aho yabona n'okumukulikira ey'eri yakuuza Nnamahanga. Olubaga looshi lwabeere lwabona ebyoola, lwarhondera gukuuza Nnamahanga.
LUK 19:1 Yeesu aliiri abalama kugerera omu gishagala ch'eYeeriko.
LUK 19:2 Mw'echo gishagala mwaliiri omuntu muguma oyirikwa Zaakayo. Oyo Zaakayo aliiri mukulu w'abafurhiisa b'amakooli. Aliiri muchire.
LUK 19:3 Agendaga ashonda kubona Yeesu ali nde. Aliko, elugulu w'abantu banene arhakamubwene bulaala aliiri muufu.
LUK 19:4 Alibirhira embere, anashona oku murhi g'omukuyu y'abona Yeesu, kwenge alikwaneene kulenga ahoola.
LUK 19:5 Yeesu abeere agera ahoola, ayinamula ameesho anamubwira ntya: «Zaakayo, shonooka juba; bulaala bimpemere ndyaame emwawe zeene.»
LUK 19:6 Zaakayo ashonooka juba, ayankirira Yeesu n'obushagaluke bunene.
LUK 19:7 Abantu booshi baabonaga ebyoola, balunduma n'okuderha ntya: «Mulolage! Oyu muntu ajiire kulyaama emw'omunyabyaaha!»
LUK 19:8 Aliko Zaakayo ayimanga, abwira Nnaweerhu ntya: «Nnaweerhu! Naaha abakene oluhande lw'ebintu byaani, n'akaba hali eyi nalengenye echintu chaage, namugalulira cho eyi nkubire cho kane.»
LUK 19:9 Yeesu amubwira ntya: «Zeene obuchunguke bwahikire mw'eyila nju, bulaala oyu naye ali mugala w'Abrahaamu.
LUK 19:10 Kwenge Mwene oMuntu ayinjire gushonda n'oguchungula abaherere.»
LUK 19:11 Abantu babeere bayunva ebyoola, bakengeera okw'obwime bwa Nnamahanga bukola kubonekana ho n'aho, bulaala Yeesu aliiri hoofu n'eYerusaleema. Aja ashuba kubachiira ogu mugani.
LUK 19:12 Aderha ntya: «Haliiri murhwali muguma wajaaga omu gihugo cha hale mpu aje kuyimikirwa yo, buzinda agaluke kuyima omu gihugo chaage.
LUK 19:13 Ahamagala bantu ekumi omu baja baage, abaha bicheri ekumi n'okubabwira ntya: ‹Murhimbuule n'ezi furanga kugera amango nagaluka.›
LUK 19:14 Aliko abantu b'egihugo chaage babaaga bamugayire. Baarhuma abantu enyuma zaage kuderha ntya: ‹Rhurhashonda oyu muntu abe mwami weerhu.›
LUK 19:15 «Abeere ayimikirwe, agaluka, ahamagaza bala baja ahaaga efuranga, mpu amenye enyungu nchi babwene omu burhimbuuzi.
LUK 19:16 Omuja mwambere achimoleka n'okuderha ntya: ‹Waliha, egicheri chaawe chayungukire bindi ekumi.›
LUK 19:17 Mwami amubwira ntya: ‹Kooko, oli muja mwinja; bulaala orhabeere muhemusi omu bintu bigeeke, wagwarha oburhegesi oku bishagala ekumi.›
LUK 19:18 Omuja wakabiri ayinja n'okuderha ntya: ‹Waliha, egicheri chaawe chayungukire bindi birhaano.›
LUK 19:19 Mwami amubwira ntya: ‹Naawe waaba murhegesi wa bishagala birhaano.›
LUK 19:20 Owindi muja ayinja n'okuderha ntya: ‹Waliha, tala egicheri chaawe, nalichibiikire omu gitambara,
LUK 19:21 kwenge nali nkuyuubahire, bulaala oba muntu mudaarhi bweneene. Wooyo onarhoola eby'orhabiikaga, n'ogushaluula eby'orhahingaga.›
LUK 19:22 Mwami amubwira ntya: ‹Wooyo oli muja mubi, naguchiira olushinja gukulikirana n'ebinwa byaawe. Akaba waliyinji oku mba mudaarhi, oku ntoola ebi ntabiikaga n'oku nshaluula ebi ntahingaga,
LUK 19:23 bichi byarhumaga orhahira efuranga zaani omu banke? Omu kugaluka kwani, nakazirhoolere n'enyungu!›
LUK 19:24 Mwami aja abwira abantu baliiri ho ntya: ‹Mumunyage echo gicheri mugihe olaala ogwerhe bicheri ekumi.›
LUK 19:25 Babwira mwami ntya: ‹Waliha, oyoola akola agwerhe bicheri ekumi!›
LUK 19:26 Abashubiza ntya: ‹Mbabwirire oku ogwerhe akantu yi nji baheereza akandi, aliko orhagwerhe kantu nji bamunyaga n'ehintu hityuuli agwerhe.
LUK 19:27 N'bashombanyi baani boowe, barhalishondere oku mbe mwami waabo, mubaleerhe hano munabayirhire embere zaani.›»
LUK 19:28 Yeesu abeere amala kuderha ntyo, aja embere z'abantu eyi bali bayeerekera eYerusaleema.
LUK 19:29 Abeere agera hoofu n'egishagala ch'eBetefaage n'eche Betaniiya, hoofu n'omusozi gw'eMizeyituuni, arhuma bigirizwa baage babiri,
LUK 19:30 ababwira ntya: «Muje omu gishagala chiri embere zenyu. Hano muchigera mo, mwashimaana omwana gw'epunda gushwekerwe, nta muntu oshubiraga yikala oku go. Mugishwekuule munachileerhe.
LUK 19:31 Nka hali omuntu obabazize ntya: ‹Gichi girhumire muli mwagishwekuula?› Mumushubize oku Nnaweerhu achilagire ko.»
LUK 19:32 Abo bigirizwa barhumwaga bagenda, banabugaana byooshi nk'oku Yeesu ababwiraga.
LUK 19:33 Babeere bali bashwekuula omwana gw'epunda, banyina go bababaza ntya: «Gichi girhumire muli mwashwekuula ogu mwana gw'epunda?»
LUK 19:34 Baashubiza ntya: «Nnaweerhu agulagire ko.»
LUK 19:35 Baja baguleerhera Yeesu. Baava baasasa ko emyambalo n'okumuyikaza ko.
LUK 19:36 Okw'ali agenda, abantu baalema baasasa emyambalo yaabo omu njira.
LUK 19:37 Yeesu abeere ali ayegeera hoofu n'omwandagalo gw'omusozi gw'eMizeyituuni, echigusho chooshi ch'abigirizwa baage, babaaga bali kugenda baamoga. Babaaga bali bakuuza Nnamahanga n'omulenge munene, elugulu w'ebisomereene byooshi bali babwene ko.
LUK 19:38 Baliiri kuderha ntya: «Agishwe, oMwami wayinjire, oku ziino lya Nnaweerhu! Omurhuula gube omu mpingu n'obulangashane emwa Nnamahanga!»
LUK 19:39 aBafarisaayo baguma, baliiri omu lubaga lw'abantu, babwira Yeesu ntya: «Mwigiriza, okalihire abigirizwa baawe basire.»
LUK 19:40 Yeesu abashubiza ntya: «Mbabwirire byo, bagasira, amabaale mo mayaama!»
LUK 19:41 Amango Yeesu ageraga hoofu n'egishagala ch'eYerusaleema, abeere abona cho, alakira cho.
LUK 19:42 Aderha ntya: «Nka naawe wamenyaga zeene ebyagakuleerhera omurhuula! Aliko bunoola bibishirwe, orhakabibona.
LUK 19:43 Kwenge esiku zakuyinjira amango bashombanyi baawe bakuzirhira ko olugurhu, bakugorha n'okugufundeeza enyunda zooshi.
LUK 19:44 Baguhomboola looshi, wooyo n'abantu baawe. Barhagakulekera baale oku lindi, bulaala orhamenyaga egihe Nnamahanga ayinjaga gukulwira ko!»
LUK 19:45 Yeesu abeere aja omu Nju ya Nnamahanga, arhondera kulibisya abarhimbuuzi.
LUK 19:46 Ava ababwira ntya: «Biyandikirwe: ‹Enju yaani nji yaaba nju y'amasaala.› Aliko mwabo mwayijirire lukunda lw'abeezi!»
LUK 19:47 Yeesu agendaga ayigiriza esiku zooshi omu Nju ya Nnamahanga. Abakulu b'abadaahwa, abigiriza b'amarhegeko n'abashamuka b'aBayaahudi balemaga bashonda kumuyirha.
LUK 19:48 Aliko bafundwa, bulaala abantu booshi baliiri bamuyunviriza bwinja buzira kuluha.
LUK 20:1 Lusiku luguma, oku Yeesu ali ayigiriza abantu omu Nju ya Nnamahanga n'okubala oMwanzi Mwinja, ho n'aho abakulu b'abadaahwa n'abigiriza b'amarhegeko, haguma n'abashamuka b'aBayaahudi baahulukira.
LUK 20:2 Baava baamubaza ntya: «Orhubwire oku burhegesi bwa nde oli waajira ebi bintu. Nde ye waguhaaga obu burhegesi?»
LUK 20:3 Yeesu abashubiza ntya: «Naani, nababaza echibazo chiguma, munshubize:
LUK 20:4 ‹Obubatiizo bwa Yohaana ka bwarhengeraga empingu changwa emw'abantu?›»
LUK 20:5 Babwirana ntya bonyine oku bonyine: «Rhukaderha okw'empingu, arhubaza gichi charhumaga rhurhamuyemeera.
LUK 20:6 Kandi rhugashubiza oku emw'abantu, olubaga looshi lwarhuyirhiisa amabaale, kwenge lwali luyemereere oku Yohaana aliiri muleebi.»
LUK 20:7 Ntyo ku bamushubiize oku barhenji ngahe bwarhengeraga.
LUK 20:8 Yeesu aja ababwira ntya: «Ko n'oko naani, ntababwira oku burhegesi bwa nde njira ebi bintu.»
LUK 20:9 Kandi Yeesu ashuba kubachiira guno mugani: «Haliiri muntu muguma wahingaga eshwa ly'emizabiibu, aliyadiisa abahinzi n'okubalama siku zinene.
LUK 20:10 Egihe ch'ogushaluula chabeere chagera ho, arhuma omuja waage emwa bala bahinzi mpu bamuheerezage amaage malehe m'eshwa. Aliko abo bahinzi bashuurha oyo muja n'okumugalula maboko moomu.
LUK 20:11 Nyina eshwa ashuba gurhuma owindi muja. Naye bamushuurha, bamudukanga, banamugalula maboko moomu.
LUK 20:12 Ashuba gurhuma omuja wa gasharhu. Bamukoromesa, banamukabula embuga.
LUK 20:13 Nyina eshwa aderha ntya: ‹Gurhe naaja naajira? Naaja narhuma mugala waani muzigirwa, nkabaga yeewe bamukenga.›
LUK 20:14 Aliko balaala bahinzi babeere bamulangiira, babwirana ntya: ‹Tala, oyuula yi waaba nyina agashambala! Rhumuyirhe, y'agashambala kaba keerhu.›
LUK 20:15 Bamukuula omu shwa, banamuyirha.» Yeesu aja abaza abantu ntya: «Nyina eshwa gurhe nj'ajira aboola bahinzi?
LUK 20:16 Nj'agaluka, nj'anayirha aboola bahinzi, nj'anaheereza abandi eshwa.» Abantu babeere bayunva ntyo, baaderha ntya: «Ebiri ntya birhahira bikaba!»
LUK 20:17 Aliko Yeesu abaloleereza, aderha ntya: «Echi chinwa chiyandikirwe gurhe chiderhere? Ebaale ab'okuyumbaka balahiraga, lyo lyahindukire ly'engenzi, ly'okuyumbakira ko.
LUK 20:18 Ngasi muntu nji wakumbagala kw'eryo baale nj'avunagulika; n'eyi nji lyarhogera ko nji lyamuhomboola.»
LUK 20:19 Ho n'aho, abigiriza b'amarhegeko n'abakulu b'abadaahwa bashonda ogushweka Yeesu, bulaala bali bayinji oku bo baderherwe mw'ogu mugani. Aliko bayuubaha abantu.
LUK 20:20 Abo bakulu b'aBayaahudi barhondera guhenguuza Yeesu. Baamurhumira abantu b'okumuneeka, baliiri kubonekana nka bali b'okuli yi bamufarhira omu nderho, n'okulengera eyo njira bagale kumuhaana omu maboko m'omurhegesi w'egihugo.
LUK 20:21 Aba bantu baabaza Yeesu ntya: «Mwigiriza, rhuyinji oku oderha n'okuyigiriza bwinja; orhajira kaboolo, aliko oyigiriza enjira ya Nnamahanga gukulikirana n'okuli.
LUK 20:22 Orhubwirage leero, k'amarhegeko meerhu mayemereere changwa malahiire gufurha ekooli emwa Kayizaari?»
LUK 20:23 Aliko Yeesu amenya obulyaalya bwabo, ababaza ntya:
LUK 20:24 «Munyereke egicheri chiguma ch'edinaari. Giheekere eshusho n'eziino lya nde?» Baashubiza ntya: «Biri bya Kayizaari.»
LUK 20:25 Yeesu aja ababwira ntya: «Mugende mwaheereza Kayizaari ebiri byaage, na Nnamahanga naye ebiri byaage.»
LUK 20:26 Bafundwa kumufarhira oku chiguma omu binwa byaage embere z'olubaga. Basoomererwa egishubizo chaage, baava baasira.
LUK 20:27 Buzinda bw'aho, aBasadukaayo baguma baaja emwa Yeesu. aBasadukaayo bo barhayemeeraga obufuuke bw'abafu. Bayinja kubaza Yeesu ntya:
LUK 20:28 «Mwigiriza, tala oku Muusa arhuyandikiire ntya: ‹Nk'omulume aligwerhe omukazi, aliko agafa buzira mwana, mwene waabo anarhoola oyo mukazi n'okuburhira nyagufa abaana.›
LUK 20:29 Leero haliiri bazaana mushanvu ba nda nguma. Omwambere ashaba n'ogufa buzira mwana.
LUK 20:30 Owakabiri naye ayingira ola mukazi, naye afa buzira mwana.
LUK 20:31 N'owagasharhu naye ko n'oko. Byaaba ntyo oku booshi mushanvu, baafa buzira kuleka abaana.
LUK 20:32 Aha buzinda, ola mukazi naye afa.
LUK 20:33 Leero amango m'ogufuuka, oyo mukazi nj'aba wa nde? Bulaala aliiri mukaabo booshi oku bali mushanvu!»
LUK 20:34 Yeesu abashubiza ntya: «Mu lino gulu, abalume n'abakazi yi bashabana.
LUK 20:35 Aliko abaganjirwe kulama mw'elyo gulu lyayinja n'ogufuuka gurhenga omu bafu nji barhaashaba changwa gushabwa.
LUK 20:36 Barhaakanafa, bulaala bali kuguma na bamalahika, bali bagala ba Nnamahanga kwenge bafuukire.
LUK 20:37 Muusa ayerekeene bwinjabwinja oku abafu nji bafuuka. Omu mandiko maage aderhere elugulu w'egishaka chagulumiraga. Yeewe aderhere oku Nnaweerhu ali ‹Nnamahanga wa Abrahaamu, Nnamahanga wa Isaka na Nnamahanga wa Yakobo.›»
LUK 20:38 Yeesu ashuba kuderha ntya: «Nnamahanga arhali w'abafu, aliko w'abalamire; kwenge oku yeewe booshi balamire.»
LUK 20:39 Abigiriza baguma b'amarhegeko bashubiza ntya: «Mwigiriza, waderhere bwinja.»
LUK 20:40 Barhagishubiraga chiro kubaza liguma.
LUK 20:41 Yeesu abaza abantu baliiri ahoola ntya: «Gurhe abantu bakaderha mpu Krisitu ali mugala wa Daawudi?
LUK 20:42 Daawudi yenyine aderhere ntya omu gitaabu ch'eNanga: ‹Nnaweerhu Nnamahanga abwirire Nnaweerhu ntya: “Yikale ekulyo kwani,
LUK 20:43 guhika amango nji naajira bashombanyi baawe ndabarhiro yaawe.”›
LUK 20:44 Leero akonva Daawudi amuyirikire Nnaweerhu, gurhe akaja aba mugala waage?»
LUK 20:45 Abantu booshi babeere bali bayunviriza Yeesu, abwira abigirizwa baage ntya:
LUK 20:46 «Muchilange oku bigiriza b'amarhegeko. Basiima guchilambagiza n'efulema zileehere, n'okulamuswa n'obukenge ah'abantu banene bali, okuyikala oku ntebe z'embere omu masinagoogi n'omu madinye.
LUK 20:47 Bananyaga abashumbakazi ebintu byaabo byooshi. N'omu guchisiisa, banajira amasaala maleehere. Abo bantu, nji baahanwa bweneene.»
LUK 21:1 Yeesu ayinamula ameesho, abona abagale bali bahira entuulo zaabo omu gasanduku k'entuulo k'omu Nju ya Nnamahanga.
LUK 21:2 Abona omushumbakazi muguma w'omukene naye ahira mo rhucheri rhubiri rhw'efuranga.
LUK 21:3 Yeesu ava aderha ntya: «Okuli mbabwirire, oyu mushumbakazi w'omukene arhuulire kulusha abandi booshi;
LUK 21:4 kwenge abandi bantu booshi barhuulire nka ntuulo efuranga barhaalichilagire ko. Aliko yeewe, omu bukene bwage, arhuulire byooshi aligwerhe by'okulama nabyo.»
LUK 21:5 Bantu baguma babeere bali baderha okw'eNju ya Nnamahanga eyumbakirwe n'amabaale menja, na kandi epambirwe n'ebintu abantu barhuuliraga Nnamahanga, Yeesu aderha ntya:
LUK 21:6 «Hayinja esiku, ebiila muli kubona ko, harhagasigala baale oku lindi lirhagahiningulwa.»
LUK 21:7 Abo bantu baabaza Yeesu ntya: «Mwigiriza, lyaali ebyoola nji byaahika? Kimenyeeso gichi nji chayeerekana oku byashonda kujirika?»
LUK 21:8 Yeesu ashubiza ntya: «Muchilange, mumenye mwagahera. Bantu banene nji bayinja omu gukoleesa eziino lyaani n'okuderha ntya: ‹Nye Masiiya!›, na kandi: ‹Egihe chayeneere!› Aliko murhabakulikiraga.
LUK 21:9 Amango nji mwayunva badeerha emyaazi y'ebiirha na ey'okulwisa abarhegesi, murhayuubahaga. Kwenge ebyoola bikwaneene gurhanga kujirika. Aliko eyi burhaza kuba b'obuzinda bwa lino gulu.»
LUK 21:10 Yeesu aja alema ababwira ntya: «Egihugo nji chalwisa echindi gihugo, n'obwami nji bwalwisa obwindi bwami.
LUK 21:11 Nji haaba emisisi mineneenene, n'omu hantu hanene, nji haaba enzara n'endwala zinene z'okuyaahukira. Nji haaba kandi ebigiriginjo biyuubahize n'ebimenyeeso by'arhengera omu nkuba.»
LUK 21:12 «Aliko, embere z'ebi byooshi, abantu nji babagwarha n'okubalibuza. Nji babahaana omu masinagoogi, nji banabahira omu munyororo. Ko n'oko, nji babasidaakira embere z'abaami n'abakulu b'egihugo elugulu w'eziino lyaani.
LUK 21:13 Ebyoola nji byaarhuma mwahamiiriza ebi munyinji ko.
LUK 21:14 Mumenye bwinja omu mirhima yenyu oku murhakwaneene gurheganya gurhe mwabuurana.
LUK 21:15 Bulaala nyoono, nji naabaha nyenyine echinwa n'obwenge bunene, oku bulyo bashombanyi benyu barhakagala kubahima changwa kulahira ebi mwaderhere.
LUK 21:16 Nji mwalenganywa n'abazeere benyu, na beene benyu, na ab'omulala gwenyu, na beera benyu. Na baguma omu mwabo nji bayirhwa.
LUK 21:17 «Abantu booshi nji babashomba elugulu w'eziino lyaani.
LUK 21:18 Aliko nta luviiri luguma l'oku rhwe lyenyu nji lwahera.
LUK 21:19 Omu guchihangaana kwenyu, mwachungula akalamo kenyu.»
LUK 21:20 «Hano nji mubona egishagala ch'eYerusaleema chagorherwe n'ebigusho by'abasoda, mwanaja mwamenya oku ogushandaazwa kwacho kwagerere hoofu.
LUK 21:21 Leero, abantu nji baaba bali eYudeeya balibirhire omu misozi. N'aba nji baaba bali omu gishagala ch'eYerusaleema barhenge mo, n'aba nji baaba bali omu rhwango barhajaaga eYerusaleema.
LUK 21:22 Kwenge nji zaaba siku z'oguhanwa kw'abantu, yi byooshi biyandikirwe bijirika.
LUK 21:23 Buhanya buchi oku bakazi nji baaba bali bukule n'oku balaala nji baaba bali kuyonsa mw'ezoola siku! Nji haaba amalibuko manene omu gihugo, n'oburhe bwa Nnamahanga nji bwaba kw'olu lubaga.
LUK 21:24 Baguma nji bayirhwa n'engoorho, abandi nji baheekwa buja omu bihugo byooshi, na Yerusaleema nj'alabarhwa n'abapagaani, kugera amango egihe chaabo nji chayeenera.»
LUK 21:25 «Nji haaba ebimenyeeso omu zuuba, omu gahembi n'omu nyenyeezi. Na hano oku gulu nako, embaga nji zaaba omu malibuko n'ogufarhwa n'obuuba elugulu w'olwamo n'emilaba y'enyanja.
LUK 21:26 Abantu nji baalaba n'obuuba bunene omu kulinga ebi nji byayinjira egulu, kwenge byooshi bigwerhe obuhashe omu chaalege nji byashaganywa.
LUK 21:27 Nji baaja baabona Mwene oMuntu ayinjire omu bichu haguma n'obuhashe n'obukuuze bunene.
LUK 21:28 Hano ebyoola nji birhondera kuyinja, muyimange bwinjabwinja murhanayuubahaga, bulaala obuchunguke bwenyu bwayegereere.»
LUK 21:29 Buzinda bw'aho, Yeesu abachiira guno mugani: «Mulole omurhi gw'omutiini n'eyindi mirhi yooshi.
LUK 21:30 Eyi mubona yaashoga, munamenya mwenyine okw'echanda chiri hoofu.
LUK 21:31 Ko n'oko kandi, amango nji mwabona ebyoola byayinja, mumenye okw'obwime bwa Nnamahanga buli hoofu.
LUK 21:32 Okuli, mbabwirire, echi gisisi girhakagera ebyoola byooshi birhanaza kuyinja.
LUK 21:33 Empingu n'egulu nji byaahirima, aliko ebinwa byaani birhagahirima.»
LUK 21:34 Yeesu ashuba kuderha ntya: «Muchilange, emirhima yenyu yakayinja zikira omu budambi, omu bulalu, n'enyifinjo z'akalamo, y'olusiku luzinda lwakayinja kubagera ko buzira kumenya,
LUK 21:35 kula omurhego gushuuduka. Kwenge nji lwayinjira abantu booshi balamire oku gulu.
LUK 21:36 Mutarame, munasaliire ngasi gashanji, yi mugwarha emisi y'ogufuma byooshi byayinja, n'okugala kuyimanga embere za Mwene oMuntu.»
LUK 21:37 Mw'ezoola siku, Yeesu agendaga ayigiriza omu Nju ya Nnamahanga ezuuba. N'obudufu, agendaga aja kulyaama oku musozi gw'eMizeyituuni.
LUK 21:38 Olubaga looshi lwagendaga lwaja emunda ali omu Nju ya Nnamahanga eseeziseezi kumuyunviriza.
LUK 22:1 Olusiku lukulu lw'emigati nzira chachu, luyirikwa Paasaka, lwabaaga luli hoofu.
LUK 22:2 Abakulu b'abadaahwa n'abigiriza b'amarhegeko baliiri bashonda gurhe bakayirhiisa Yeesu. Aliko baliiri bayuubaha olubaga.
LUK 22:3 Shetaani aja aja mu Yuuda, ola bayirikaga Isikariyooti, waliiri muguma w'omu zila ntumwa ekumi n'ebiri.
LUK 22:4 Yuuda aja kuganiira haguma n'abakulu b'abadaahwa n'abakulu b'abalanzi b'eNju ya Nnamahanga gurhe akalenganya Yeesu emunda bali.
LUK 22:5 Basiima n'okulagaanana okumuha efuranga.
LUK 22:6 Yuuda ayemeera n'ogurhondera kulonza agashanji gakwiriire k'okumuha bo buzira abantu kumenya.
LUK 22:7 Olusiku lukulu lw'emigati nzira chachu lwahika. Olo lusiku, y'aBayaahudi balikwaneene kubaaga omwanabuzi gw'ePaasaka.
LUK 22:8 Yeesu arhuma Petero na Yohaana ntya: «Muje gurhurheganyiza ebiryo by'ePaasaka, rhuyinje kubisangira.»
LUK 22:9 Baamubaza ntya: «Ngahe osiimire rhubirheganyizage?»
LUK 22:10 Abashubiza ntya: «Muyunvirize, hanoola muhika omu gishagala, mwashimaana omulume oheekere endaha y'amenji. Mumukulikire omu nju ayinja kuja mo.
LUK 22:11 Mwakabwira nyina enju ntya: ‹Mwigiriza abazize mpu ngahe echumbi liri aliira mw'ebiryo by'ePaasaka haguma n'abigirizwa baage.›
LUK 22:12 Abayeereka echumbi linene lirheganyizwe omu gorofa, omoola mu mwarheganyiza ebiryo.»
LUK 22:13 Bagenda, bashimaana ebintu byooshi kulaala Yeesu ababwiraga. Baaja barheganya ebiryo by'ePaasaka.
LUK 22:14 Ebishanji by'okulya byabeere byaahika, Yeesu ayikala kulya haguma n'entumwa zaage.
LUK 22:15 Azibwira ntya: «Nachifiijaga bweneene kulya haguma nenyu eyi Paasaka embere ndibuke.
LUK 22:16 Kwenge, mbabwirire okuli, ntagachiyirya kugera amango nji yayeenera omu Bwami bwa Nnamahanga.»
LUK 22:17 Arhoola engumbu y'edivaayi, akuuza Nnamahanga n'okuderha ntya: «Murhoole eyi ngumbu, ngasi muguma anywe ko.
LUK 22:18 Kwenge mbabwirire okuli, ntagachinywa chiro oku divaayi y'omuzabiibu kugera amango Nnamahanga nji ayimanza obwime bwage.»
LUK 22:19 Ashuba gurhoola omugati. Abeere amala gukuuza Nnamahanga, agucha mo, abaheereza go n'okuderha ntya: «Oguula guli mubiri gwani, guhaanirwe elugulu wenyu. Mugende mwajira ntya omu kunyibuka.»
LUK 22:20 Ko n'oko enyuma z'okulya, arhoola engumbu, aderha ntya: «Eyi ngumbu eri gihango gihyaahya cha Nnamahanga haguma n'abantu baage kulengera eshagama yaani yasheeshekala elugulu wenyu.»
LUK 22:21 «Aliko tala k'owampaana ali kulya haguma naani.
LUK 22:22 Mwene oMuntu aja gufa nk'oku Nnamahanga arheganyaga. Aliko, buhanya buchi oku muntu wamuhaana!»
LUK 22:23 Abigirizwa baava barhondera kubazana nde omu boowe waajira echi chintu.
LUK 22:24 Buzinda, haahulukira entonganyi ahagarhi k'abigirizwa ba Yeesu, mpu nde wakaba mukulu ahagarhi kaabo.
LUK 22:25 Yeesu abwira bo ntya: «Abaami b'abapagaani banabarhegeka nka baja, n'abagwerhe obuhashe oku bantu bachiyirika ‹banyamenja.›
LUK 22:26 Aliko mwabo, birhabaaga ntyo. Ahuubwe, oli mukulu omu mwabo ahinduke nka ye mudoorho, n'orhambwire, abe nka ye mukozi.
LUK 22:27 Leero, nde y'eri mukulu oku windi: oyikeere n'okulya changwa oli kumuyuuhulira? K'arhali olaala oyikeere n'okulya? Ahuubwe, nyoono ndi ahagarhi kenyu nka mukozi.
LUK 22:28 «Mwewe mwachihangaanire kubeera haguma naani omu bigeregezo byaani.
LUK 22:29 Cho girhumire mbarheganyiize obwami nk'oku naani Daarha abunrheganyizaga,
LUK 22:30 yi mulya n'okunywa oku meeza maani, omu Bwami bwani. Kandi muyikale oku ntebe z'obwami yi muchiira olushinja emilala ekumi n'ebiri y'eIsraheeli.»
LUK 22:31 Yeesu ashuba kuderha ntya: «Simooni, Simooni, Shetaani abahemere oku mugere omu bigeregezo kuguma n'oku bayeera amahemba.
LUK 22:32 Aliko nagusaliriire wooyo Simooni, y'obwemeezi bwawe burhaheraga looshi. Na hanoola ongalukira, okomeze beene benyu.»
LUK 22:33 Petero amubwira ntya: «Nnaweerhu, nayemereere kugenda naawe nachiro akaba omu munyororo changwa omu lufu.»
LUK 22:34 Yeesu amushubiza ntya: «Petero, nkubwirire okuli, embere oluhazi lubike zeene, waaba eyi wamampakana gasharhu oku orhanyinji.»
LUK 22:35 Yeesu ashuba kubabaza ntya: «Amango nabarhumaga buzira shaho, buzira chigunira n'ebiraato, ka mwalibulire chintu?» Bamushubiza ntya: «Ntaacho.»
LUK 22:36 Yeesu ababwira ntya: «Ahuubwe leero, ogwerhe eshaho n'echigunira abirhoole. N'orhagwerhe engoorho aguze efulema yaage y'agula nguma.
LUK 22:37 Kwenge mbabwirire okuli, bihemere ebiyandikirwe binjirike ko: ‹Bamuganjire omu bajira amabi.› Leero, ebiyandikirwe elugulu waani bikola kujirika.»
LUK 22:38 Abigirizwa bamubwira ntya: «Nnaweerhu, tala ngoorho ebiri.» Naye ababwira ntya: «Mulekere ahoola!»
LUK 22:39 Yeesu arhenga mw'echo gishagala, aja oku musozi gw'eMizeyituuni nka okw'azigaanaga. Abigirizwa baage bamukulikira.
LUK 22:40 Agerere ahoola, ababwira ntya: «Musaliire, yi murhaja omu bigeregezo.»
LUK 22:41 Ava achikuula haguma nabo, aja oku bule nka ah'omuntu akagala kulekera ebaale, afukama, asaliira Nnamahanga ntya:
LUK 22:42 «Daarha, akaba ntya b'obulonza bwawe, ohire hale naani eyi ngumbu y'amalibuko. Aliko, burhabaaga bulonza bwani bo bujirikage, sy'obulonza bwawe.» [
LUK 22:43 Ho n'aho, malahika amubonekera gurhenga empingu gushuba kumuheereza emisi.
LUK 22:44 Yeesu abeere ababeere bweneene, ashuba gusaliira n'obushiru kulusha. Entuubano yaage yaba nka mirhonyi y'eshagama eri gurhoga oku budaka.]
LUK 22:45 Amalire gusaliira, ayimanga n'okuja emunda abigirizwa bali. Ashimaana balyaamire elugulu w'amaganya manene.
LUK 22:46 Abaza bo ntya: «Charhumire mwalyaama? Muzuuke munasaliire, yi murhaja omu bigeregezo.»
LUK 22:47 Yeesu abeere achiri aderha, ho n'aho abantu banene baahika. Yuuda, ola muguma w'omu zila ntumwa ekumi n'ebiri, aliiri kulambagira embere zaabo. Ashegera hoofu na Yeesu y'amuhoobera.
LUK 22:48 Yeesu amubaza ntya: «Yuuda, omu kumuhoobera mu wamalenganya Mwene oMuntu?»
LUK 22:49 Abigirizwa baliiri haguma na Yeesu babeere baabona ebyaja kuba, baamubaza ntya: «Nnaweerhu, ka rhubashogoorhe n'engoorho?»
LUK 22:50 Ho n'aho, mwigirizwa muguma ashinjibula ogurhwi kw'emalyo k'omuja w'omudaahwa mukulu.
LUK 22:51 Aliko Yeesu aderha ntya: «Lekera aho!» Ava ahuma oku gurhwi k'oyo mulume n'okugufumya.
LUK 22:52 Omu bayinjaga gufarha Yeesu mwaliiri abakulu b'abadaahwa, abimangizi b'abalanzi b'eNju ya Nnamahanga n'abashamuka b'aBayaahudi. Yeesu ababwira ntya: «Mwayinjire n'engoorho n'enkoni, owamenya mpu ndi gishumuusi!
LUK 22:53 Esiku zooshi, naliiri haguma nenyu omu Nju ya Nnamahanga, murhayinjaga kunfarha. Aliko chinoola gihe gikola chenyu na ech'obuhashe b'omwizimya.»
LUK 22:54 Abo bantu baafarha Yeesu, bamuheeka omu nju y'omudaahwa mukulu. Petero abakulikira buzira kubayegeera.
LUK 22:55 Bachaana omuliro ahagarhi k'embuga, bayikala. Petero naye ayikala ahagarhi kaabo.
LUK 22:56 Elugulu w'obumoleke b'omuliro, omuja muguma w'omukazi abona Petero ayikeere. Amuloleereza n'okuderha ntya: «Oyuula naye aliiri haguma n'ola muntu.»
LUK 22:57 Aliko Petero ahakana, aderha ntya: «Ego mukazi, nyoono ntamuyinji!»
LUK 22:58 Hagerere hishanji higeeke, owindi muntu amubona n'okuderha ntya: «Naawe, oli muguma wabo.» Petero naye aderha ntya: «Nangwa maani, ntali muguma wabo!»
LUK 22:59 Hagerere nka saa nguma, kandi owindi muntu ayemeereza ntya: «Okuli, oyu mulume aliiri haguma na Yeesu, kwenge naye ali Mugalilaaya.»
LUK 22:60 Petero ashubiza ntya: «Muza wee, ntamenyere ebi washonda kuderha!» Ho n'aho, oku achiri aderha, oluhazi lwabika.
LUK 22:61 Nnaweerhu ava ahindamuka n'okulola Petero. Petero ayibuka echinwa Nnaweerhu amubwiraga oku: «Embere oluhazi lubike zeene, waaba eyi wamampakana gasharhu.»
LUK 22:62 Petero ahuluka, alira bweneene.
LUK 22:63 Abantu bali bafarhire Yeesu, baalema bamushuuka n'okumushuurha.
LUK 22:64 Baamuhubya ameesho n'okulema bamubwira ntya: «Leeba! Orhubwire nde wamagushuurha!»
LUK 22:65 Baashuba kulema bamudukanga ebindi bidusi binene.
LUK 22:66 Bwabeere bwacha, abashamuka b'aBayaahudi, abakulu b'abadaahwa n'abigiriza b'amarhegeko bachiigusha haguma. Baheeka Yeesu omu kabuga kaabo.
LUK 22:67 Bamubwira ntya: «Akaba wooyo we Krisitu, orhubwirage.» Naye abashubiza ntya: «Nkababwira ko murhakayemeera!
LUK 22:68 Naani nkola nababaza, murhanshubiza.
LUK 22:69 Aliko gurhengera buno, Mwene oMuntu aba ayikeere emalyo ma Nnamahanga w'obuhashe.»
LUK 22:70 Booshi baabaza ntya: «Ka gasi wooyo we Mwene Nnamahanga?» Abashubiza ntya: «Mwewe mwe muderhere oku ndi ye.»
LUK 22:71 Baava baaderha ntya: «Bwindi buhamiiriza buchi rhulagire ko? Rhwayunviirhe rhwenyine eby'aderhere!»
LUK 23:1 Bala bantu booshi babaaga bali omu kabuga k'aBayaahudi bayimanga, baheeka Yeesu embere z'omwimangizi Pilaato.
LUK 23:2 Barhondera kumusidaaka, baderha ntya: «Rhwabugaanire oyu muntu ali ararusa olubaga lwerhu; ali abuza guhaana ekooli emwa mwami mukulu Kayizaari, anali achiiderha yenyine oku ali Krisitu, k'okuderha mwami.»
LUK 23:3 Pilaato amubaza ntya: «Ka wooyo oli mwami w'aBayaahudi?» Yeesu amushubiza ntya: «Wooyo, we waderhere ntyo.»
LUK 23:4 Pilaato abwira abakulu b'abadaahwa n'olubaga lw'abantu ntya: «Ntaacho nabwene emw'oyu muntu chagarhuma ahanwa.»
LUK 23:5 Aliko, baharhiiriza n'okuderha ntya: «Enyigirizo zaage yi zaarhuma abantu balwisa abakulu omu Yudeeya yooshi. Arhangiriraga eGalilaaya, leero ali kuno.»
LUK 23:6 Pilaato abeere ayunva ebyoola, abaza akaba oyu muntu aliiri Mugalilaaya.
LUK 23:7 Abeere amenya oku Yeesu arhengera omu gihugo girhegekerwe na Heroode, amurhuma emwa Heroode, kwenge naye aliiri eYerusaleema mw'ezoola siku.
LUK 23:8 Heroode abeere abona Yeesu, ashagaluka bweneene. Gurhengera miira, aliiri ashonda kumubona kwenge abaaga ayunviirhe emyaazi yaage. Na kandi, aliiri alangaalira okubona Yeesu ajira egisomereene.
LUK 23:9 Heroode amubaziiriza, aliko Yeesu ntaacho amushubize.
LUK 23:10 Abakulu b'abadaahwa n'abigiriza b'amarhegeko baliiri ahoola, bamusidaaka n'obukali bunene.
LUK 23:11 Heroode naye, haguma n'abasoda baage, bashekera Yeesu n'okumukena. Bamalire kumushekera n'okumuyambisa omwambalo gukwiriire bweneene, ashuba kugalula Yeesu emwa Pilaato.
LUK 23:12 Olo lusiku, Heroode na Pilaato baaba beera, n'obo embere baliiri banzi.
LUK 23:13 Pilaato ahamagaza abakulu b'abadaahwa, abimangizi b'aBayaahudi n'abandi bantu.
LUK 23:14 Ababwira ntya: «Mwandeerheraga oyu muntu bulaala mwaderhaga oku aliiri gurarusa olubaga. Namubazize embere zenyu aliko nyoono ntaacho namubwene ko chagarhuma ahanwa omu byooshi mwamusidakiire.
LUK 23:15 Heroode naye ntaacho amubwene ko, kwenge arhugaluliire ye. Ntaacho omu by'ajirire chagarhuma ayirhwa.
LUK 23:16 Boboola enyuma z'okumushuurha, namulikuula.» [
LUK 23:17 Ngasi lusiku lukulu lw'ePaasaka, Pilaato alikwaneene kubalikuulira omuntu muguma oli omu munyororo.]
LUK 23:18 Abantu booshi bayaamira chaligumira ntya: «Oyirhe oyu muntu! Orhulikuulire Baraaba!»
LUK 23:19 Baraaba abaaga ashwekerwe elugulu w'entambala yabaaga omu gishagala n'okuyirha omuntu.
LUK 23:20 Pilaato ashuba kuderha nabo, kwenge alishondere alikuule Yeesu.
LUK 23:21 Aliko boowe baalema bayaama ntya: «Omubambe oku musalaaba! Omubambe oku musalaaba!»
LUK 23:22 Pilaato ababwira ntya obwa gasharhu: «Bubi buchi ajirire? Ntaacho namubwene ko chagarhuma ayirhwa. Enyuma z'okumushuurha, namulikuula.»
LUK 23:23 Aliko bachihanda n'olwamo lunene, omu guhema abambwe oku musalaaba. Olwamo lwabo lunene lwahimana.
LUK 23:24 Buzinda, Pilaato arhegeka oku bibe nk'oku abantu baahemaga.
LUK 23:25 Alikuula ola bashondaga, wali wahirirwe omu munyororo elugulu w'obugome n'okuyirha omuntu; abaheereza Yeesu, bamujire nk'oku balonzaga.
LUK 23:26 Abasoda b'aBarooma babeere bali baheeka Yeesu emunda bamuyirhira, bashimaanana n'omuntu muguma oyirikwa Simooni, w'egishagala ch'eKureene, waliiri gurhenga omu shwa. Baava bamurhoola n'okumuheesa omusalaaba mpu aguheeke enyuma za Yeesu.
LUK 23:27 Olubaga lunene lw'abantu lwali kulikiire Yeesu. Ahagarhi kaabo haliiri abakazi baliiri balira n'oguchiniguula elugulu waage.
LUK 23:28 Yeesu abahindamukira n'okubabwira ntya: «Mwe bakazi b'eYerusaleema, murhandiriraga. Aliko muchiilirire n'abaana benyu.
LUK 23:29 Kwenge esiku zayinjire abantu nji baderha ntya: ‹Bagishirwe abakazi b'engumba, zigishirwe enda zirhashubiraga kuburha n'amabeere marhashubiraga kuyonsa!›
LUK 23:30 Amo mango, abantu nji barhondera okubwira emisozi ntya: ‹Murhurhogere ko!›, n'okubwira orhusozi ntya: ‹Murhuhambe!›
LUK 23:31 Bulaala eyi bankajira ebyoola oku murhi mubishi, bichi nji byajirirwa omurhi guyuumire?»
LUK 23:32 Kandi, abasoda bali baheekere ebishumuusi bibiri, byaali byaaja kuyirhwa haguma na Yeesu.
LUK 23:33 Babeere baagera ahantu hayirikwa Mpanga, bamubambira ahoola oku musalaaba, na bila bishumuusi bibiri, chiguma ekulyo n'echindi ekulembe.
LUK 23:34 [Yeesu aderha ntya: «Daarha, obababalire, kwenge barhamenyere echi bali baajira.»] Abasoda bagabaana emyambalo yaage omu kuyeesha esimbi.
LUK 23:35 Abantu baliyimangire ahoola, baanali baalola. Abarhegesi b'aBayaahudi boowe, bashinyagulira Yeesu, baderha ntya: «Achungwire abandi; agichungule yenyine, akaba ali Krisitu, ola Nnamahanga agishogere!»
LUK 23:36 Abasoda nabo baliiri bamushekera. Bayinja kumuha edivaayi y'enkala,
LUK 23:37 n'okumubwira ntya: «Akaba oli mwami w'aBayaahudi, ogifumye wenyine!»
LUK 23:38 Haliiri kandi elugulu waage ogu mwandiko: «Oyu ye Mwami w'aBayaahudi.»
LUK 23:39 Muguma omu bishumuusi bibambirwe oku musalaaba amudukanga ntya: «K'orhali we Krisitu? Ochifumye wenyine onarhufumye!»
LUK 23:40 Aliko echindi gishumuusi chakalihira echaabo ntya: «K'orhagwerhe chiro obuuba bwa Nnamahanga, wooyo weeri waahanwa kuguma naye?
LUK 23:41 Oku rhwewe, obuhane burhukwaneene, kwenge rhuli rhwayankirira egikwaneene ebijiro byeerhu. Aliko oyuula nta chibi n'echiguma ajirire.»
LUK 23:42 Ashuba kuderha ntya: «Yeesu, onyibuke hano nj'oja omu Bwami bwawe.»
LUK 23:43 Yeesu amushubiza ntya: «Okuli, nkubwirire, zeene waaba haguma naani omu Paradizo.»
LUK 23:44 Zaali zikola zashonda kuba saa ndarhu; haaba omwizimya oku gihugo chooshi kugera aha saa mwenda,
LUK 23:45 kwenge ezuuba lyalihirimire. N'omwenda gw'omu Nju ya Nnamahanga gwachisharhula ahagarhi.
LUK 23:46 Yeesu ayaama ntya: «Daarha, mpirire omurhima gwani omu fune zaawe.» Amalire kuderha ebyoola, asimuuka.
LUK 23:47 Omukulu w'abasoda abeere abona ebyabeere, akuuza Nnamahanga n'okuderha ntya: «Okuli, oyu muntu aliiri okwaneene!»
LUK 23:48 Abantu booshi balichigushire ahoola kulola kw'eyo myaazi, babwene ebyabeere, bagaluka emwabo n'amaganya manene.
LUK 23:49 Booshi baliyinji Yeesu, n'abakazi baliiri bamuherekeeze gurhengera eGalilaaya, bayimanga hale, baalola ebiri byaaba.
LUK 23:50 Haliiri mulume muguma oyirikwa Yozefu wahulukiraga eHarimateya, gishagala chiguma ch'aBayaahudi. Aliiri muntu mwinja onakwaneene, anagendaga alinga obwime bwa Nnamahanga. Aliiri muguma w'akabuga k'aBayaahudi, aliko arhaali yemereere omuhigo n'ebijiro byaabo by'okuyirha Yeesu.
LUK 23:52 Aja emwa Pilaato, ahema omubiri gwa Yeesu.
LUK 23:53 Aguyandagaza oku musalaaba, aguzingira kw'edaraape, aguhira omu shinda yajokolwaga omu baale. Mweyo shinda, mwabaaga murhashubiraga guhaabwa muntu.
LUK 23:54 Olo lusiku, lwaliiri lwagarhaano, lo lwanaliiri lusiku l'ogurheganya eSaabato, n'eSaabato yali kola gurhondera.
LUK 23:55 Balaala bakazi baliiri barhengeere eGalilaaya haguma na Yeesu, bakulikira Yozefu. Baabona eshinda n'obulyo bahiraga mo omubiri gwa Yeesu.
LUK 23:56 Bagaluka gurheganya amavurha n'amarashi. Olusiku lw'eSaabato, bahumuuka, gukulikirana n'eRhegeko lya Nnamahanga.
LUK 24:1 Olusiku lwakulikiraga eSaabato, bala bakazi baja ebwa shinda eseeziseezi, eyi baheekere amavurha m'amarashi bali barheganyize.
LUK 24:2 Bashimaana ebaale lyalichingire eshinda lyahirikirwe eburhambi.
LUK 24:3 Baja mo, aliko barhabonaga omubiri gwa Nnaweerhu Yeesu.
LUK 24:4 Babeere bali basoomerwa elugulu w'ebyabeere, ho n'aho balume babiri bayambeere emyambalo ebaraganyize babonekana embere zaabo.
LUK 24:5 Aboola bakazi bayuubaha bweneene, bayeerekeza amalanga maabo oku daho. Aliko aboola balume bababwira ntya: «Girhumire mwashondera ozeene omu bafu?
LUK 24:6 Arhali hano, afuukire! Muyibuke ebi ababwiraga amango alichiri eGalilaaya oku:
LUK 24:7 ‹Bihemere Mwene oMuntu ahaanwe oku banyabyaaha, abambwe oku musalaaba, anafuuke olusiku lwa gasharhu.›»
LUK 24:8 Abo bakazi baava bayibuka ebinwa byaage.
LUK 24:9 Bagaluka gurhenga ebwa shinda, n'ebyoola byooshi babibalira entumwa ekumi na nguma n'abandi bigirizwa.
LUK 24:10 Aboola bakazi babibaliraga entumwa baliiri: Mariya w'eMagadala, Jaani, Mariya nyina wa Yakobo n'abandi baliiri haguma nabo.
LUK 24:11 Aliko ebi binwa byabonekana oku meesho m'entumwa nka ntaacho bimalire, barhanabiyemeeraga.
LUK 24:12 Aliko Petero yeewe ayimanga, alibirhira ebwa shinda. Ayunamire, abona emyenda alizingirwe mo yonyine. Ava achigalukira emwage, eyi asomereerwe ebyabeere.
LUK 24:13 Olo lusiku lo n'olo, babiri omu bigirizwa ba Yeesu baliiri baaja omu gishagala chiyirikwa Emawu. Chaliiri oku bilomeetere byakagera kw'ekumi na chiguma n'eYerusaleema.
LUK 24:14 Baliiri baganiira oku byooshi byazindaga kugera.
LUK 24:15 Babeere bali baganiira n'okubazana, Yeesu yenyine abayegeera n'okugenda haguma nabo.
LUK 24:16 Aliko ameesho maabo maalihubizwe yi barhamumenya.
LUK 24:17 Yeesu ababaza ntya: «Binwa bichi muli mwaganiira muli kulambagira?» Bayimanga eyi bagwerhe amaganya manene.
LUK 24:18 Muguma omu bo, oyirikwa Keleopaasi, amubaza ntya: «Ka wooyo wenyine omu balama eYerusaleema werhamenyere ebyabeere mw'ezi siku?»
LUK 24:19 Yeesu naye abaza bo ntya: «Bichi ebyo?» Bamushubiza ntya: «Ebiyerekeere Yeesu w'eNazareeti, ola waliiri muleebi w'obuhashe omu bijiro n'enderho embere za Nnamahanga n'embere z'olubaga looshi.
LUK 24:20 Leero, abakulu b'abadaahwa n'abarhegesi beerhu nji bamuhaanire mpu ahanirwe olufu anabambwe oku musalaaba.
LUK 24:21 Rhwalinihiire oku yeewe ye wali wachungula Israheeli. Aliko leero haguma n'ebyo byooshi, zeene l'olusiku lwa gasharhu gurhenga ebyo bibeere.
LUK 24:22 Aliko kandi, abakazi baguma nabo b'echigusho cheerhu bali barhushalamize. Bali balamukiire zeene eseeziseezi oku shinda,
LUK 24:23 aliko barhaali babwene omubiri gwage. Bamaava bayinja kuderha oku babonekeerwe na bamalahika. Abo bamalahika bababwirire oku Yeesu ali mugumaguma.
LUK 24:24 Beerhu baguma balijiire oku shinda, banabugaanire ebintu nka okw'abakazi babiderhaga. Aliko yeewe, barhamubwene.»
LUK 24:25 Yeesu aja ababwira ntya: «Mwe bihwinja mwe! N'emirhima yenyu erhayemeerera ho byooshi abaleebi baderhaga!
LUK 24:26 Ka Krisitu arhaalikwaneene alibuke ntyo y'aja omu bukuuze bwage?»
LUK 24:27 Yeesu ava abahuguula oku biri omu Mandiko Matagatiifu mooshi elugulu waage, gurhonderera oku bitaabu bya Muusa n'ebyabaleebi booshi.
LUK 24:28 Babeere bayegeera egishagala baliiri baaja mo, Yeesu abonekana nk'owagendeerera n'olugenzi.
LUK 24:29 Aliko bamurhebeereza omu kuderha ntya: «Obeere haguma neerhu, kwenge bwayirire.» Ntyo ku Yeesu ajiire omu nju kubeera haguma nabo.
LUK 24:30 Abeere ayikala kulya haguma nabo, arhoola omugati n'okugugisha, aguchagulanga n'okuguheereza bo.
LUK 24:31 Ameesho maabo maaja mahumuulwa bwinja, baanaja bamumenya. Aliko ahirima embere zaabo.
LUK 24:32 Baabazana ntya: «K'emirhima yeerhu erhaliyunviirhe obushagaluke bunene amango aliiri aganiira neerhu omu njira n'ogurhuhuguulira eby'aMandiko Matagatiifu maderhere?»
LUK 24:33 Ho n'aho bayuumuka, bagaluka eYerusaleema. Babugaana zilaala ntumwa ekumi na nguma zichigushire haguma n'abandi bigirizwa.
LUK 24:34 Abo booshi, babwira bala bigirizwa babiri ntya: «Okuli Nnaweerhu afuukire, anabonekeere Simooni!»
LUK 24:35 Bala bigirizwa babiri baabala ebyaali bibahikiire omu njira, na gurhe barhegeeraga Yeesu amango achagulangaga omugati.
LUK 24:36 Bala bigirizwa babiri babeere bali baderha ebyoola, Yeesu yenyine achiyeerekana ahagarhi kaabo n'okubabwira ntya: «Omurhuula gube haguma nenyu!»
LUK 24:37 Abigirizwa baashalama n'okuyuubaha bweneene, eyi bakengereere mpu babwene omuzimu.
LUK 24:38 Aliko Yeesu ababwira ntya: «Bichi birhumire mwayuubaha? Bichi birhumire mwaganganwa omu mirhima yenyu?
LUK 24:39 Mulole amaboko maani n'amagulu maani, okuli nyoono! Munmamaarhe munaloleereze. Omuzimu arhajira munyofu changwa egufa, nka kunoola mubwene mbigwerhe.»
LUK 24:40 Omu kuderha ebyoola, abayeereka amaboko maage n'amagulu maage.
LUK 24:41 Abigirizwa basoomerwa n'ogushagaluka bweneene, n'obo babaaga barhaza kuyemeera echi babwene. Yeesu aja ababaza ntya: «Ka mugwerhe hano echintu ch'okulya?»
LUK 24:42 Baamuha egichiira ch'efi eyoosezwe.
LUK 24:43 Agirhoola n'oguchilya embere zaabo.
LUK 24:44 Aja ababwira ntya: «Ebiila binababwiraga amango nali nchiri haguma nenyu. Byaalihemere bijirike byooshi byaali biyandikirwe elugulu waani omu Rhegeko lya Muusa, omu bitaabu abaleebi bayandikaga n'omu gitaabu ch'eNanga.»
LUK 24:45 Ho n'aho, Yeesu abahunuula obwenge b'okuyunva aMandiko Matagatiifu.
LUK 24:46 Ava ababwira ntya: «Biyandikirwe oku Krisitu alibuka, n'oku afuuka omu bafu olusiku lwa gasharhu.
LUK 24:47 Kandi, omu ziino lyaage, abantu b'ebihugo byooshi gurhangirira eYerusaleema nji baabalirwa oku baleke ebyaaha byaabo yi bababalirwa.
LUK 24:48 Muli bahamiiriza b'ebyoola byooshi.
LUK 24:49 Nyoono, nabarhumira echi Daarha alaganyaga. Mwabo, mubeere hanoola Yerusaleema kugera amango mwayankirira obuhashe b'ogurhengera empingu.»
LUK 24:50 Yeesu aheeka abigirizwa baage kugera hoofu n'egishagala ch'eBetaniiya. Ayinamula amaboko elugulu, abagisha.
LUK 24:51 Abeere ali abagisha, achikuula haguma nabo, aheekwa empingu.
LUK 24:52 Abigirizwa boowe, bamalire kumuharamya, bagaluka eYerusaleema n'obushagaluke bunene.
LUK 24:53 Ngasi mango, baliiri omu Nju ya Nnamahanga eyi banali bamukuuza.
ACT 1:1 Muzigirwa Teofiile, Omu gitaabu girhanzi nayandikaga, naderhere elugulu wa byooshi Yeesu arhonderaga kujira n'okuyigiriza,
ACT 1:2 guhika olusiku aheekwaga empingu. Embere aheekwe yo, aheereza eNtumwa zaage abaaga agishogere amarhegeko kugerera Muuka-Mutagatiifu.
ACT 1:3 Enyuma z'ogufa kwage, ezo ntumwa z'achiyerekanaga ko kugerera ebimenyeeso binene yi zimenya okw'ali mugumaguma. Aliiri ababonekera omu gihe cha siku makumi mane, eyi ali abayigiriza emyaazi eyerekeere obwime bwa Nnamahanga.
ACT 1:4 Lusiku luguma mw'amo mango, Yeesu abeere ali haguma nabo, abarhegeka ntya: «Murharhengaga eYerusaleema, aliko mulingire yo echilagaane cha Daarha nababwiraga.
ACT 1:5 Yohaana abatiizaga omu menji, aliko mwabo omu siku zigeeke mwabatiizwa na Muuka-Mutagatiifu.»
ACT 1:6 Amango eNtumwa zalichigushire haguma na Yeesu zamubaza ntya: «Nnaweerhu, ka mu chino gihe y'okola kugalulira aBaisraheeli obwami bwabo?»
ACT 1:7 Abashubiza ntya: «Birhabalolere okumenya egihe n'ebishanji Daarha afundikire omu burhegesi bwage yenyine.
ACT 1:8 Aliko, mwayankiirira obuhashe hano Muuka-Mutagatiifu ayinja elugulu wenyu, mwanaba bahamiiriza baani eYerusaleema, eYudeeya yooshi n'eSamariya, n'omu gulu lyooshi.»
ACT 1:9 Yeesu abeere ayuusa kuderha ebyoola binwa, eyi bachiri bamulola, aheekwa empingu n'egichu chamubisha, barhanachimubonaga ko.
ACT 1:10 Babeere bachiri baheneera elugulu eyi ali agenda, ho n'aho balume babiri bayambeere emyambalo myeeru bayimanga embere zaabo.
ACT 1:11 Baabaza eNtumwa ntya: «Mwe bantu b'eGalilaaya, girhumire mwabeera ahoola eyi muli mwalola elugulu? Oyu Yeesu wamakuulwa ahagarhi kenyu guheekwa empingu, nj'agaluka nk'oku mwabwene aja yo.»
ACT 1:12 Enyuma z'aho, eNtumwa zagaluka eYerusaleema gurhengera oku musozi gw'eMizeyituuni. Ogo musozi guba hoofu n'eYerusaleema, lugenzi luyemereerwe kulambagirwa olusiku lw'eSaabato.
ACT 1:13 Babeere bagaluka omu gishagala, bazamuukira omu gorofa ebusiika. Omoola mu bagendaga babeera. Mwaliiri Petero, Yohaana, Yakobo na Ndereya, Firipo na Tomaasi, Baritolomaayo na Matayo, Yakobo mugala wa Lufaayo, Simooni w'omu chigusho ch'aBazelooti na Yuuda mugala wa Yakobo.
ACT 1:14 Abaala booshi bagendaga basaliira n'omurhima muguma, haguma na Mariya nyina wa Yeesu, n'abandi bakazi, na beene baabo Yeesu.
ACT 1:15 Lusiku luguma, oluganjo lw'abemeezi balichigushire lwaliiri hoofu egana na makumyaabiri. Petero ayimanga ahagarhi kaabo n'okuderha ntya:
ACT 1:16 «Beene beerhu, byaalihemere aMandiko mayeenere, mala Muuka-Mutagatiifu abaaga aderhere kugerera obuunu bwa Daawudi elugulu wa Yuuda. Oyuula Yuuda yi walongoolaga abafarhaga Yeesu.
ACT 1:17 Aliiri muguma omu rhwewe, analigwerhe echigabi oku kaasi keerhu.»
ACT 1:18 Enyuma z'okugula eshwa n'efuranga z'obuhemusi, arhoga buchuli, enda yaage yabereka n'amala maage masheeshekalira ahashi.
ACT 1:19 Abantu booshi b'eYerusaleema bamenya ogo mwazi, oku bulyo elyo shwa lyayirikwa omu lulimi lwaabo mpu lyo «Hakeledama», kw'okuderha «Eshwa ly'eshagama.»
ACT 1:20 «Kwenge biyandikirwe ntya omu gitaabu ch'eNanga: ‹Enju yaage ebe mushaka, na nta muntu oyilamage mo! N'owundi arhoole akaasi kaage!›»
ACT 1:21 «Bihemere leero, rhugishoge owindi muntu muguma w'ogurhoola akaasi kaage. Oyu muntu abe muguma w'omu bala bagendaga barhuherekeza ngasi bishanji byooshi Nnaweerhu Yeesu aliiri abalama haguma neerhu. Aba bantu baliiri haguma neerhu gurhengera amango Yohaana abatiizaga Nnaweerhu guhika olusiku aheekwaga gurhenga ahagarhi keerhu. Bihemere oyu muntu rhwachishoga abe haguma neerhu omu guhamiiriza obufuuke bwa Nnaweerhu.»
ACT 1:23 eNtumwa zaaja zamoleka bantu babiri: Yozefu oyirikwa Barisaba wanashembulwaga Yusto, na Matiyaasi.
ACT 1:24 Baaja basaliira ntya: «Nnaweerhu, weyinji emirhima y'abantu booshi, oyeerekane nde ochishogere mw'abaala babiri,
ACT 1:25 y'aja ahaali ha Yuuda mw'akaala kaasi k'eNtumwa alekaga omu kuja ahantu hamukwaneene.»
ACT 1:26 Bashaarha esimbi, nazo zarhoola Matiyaasi wayongeerwaga mu zila ntumwa ekumi na nguma.
ACT 2:1 Olusiku lw'ePendekosite lwabeere lwahika, abigirizwa booshi babaaga babuganeene hantu haguma.
ACT 2:2 Ho n'aho bayunva olwamo gurhengera empingu luli nka lw'empuusi ekalihire, enali yahuusahuusa. Olo lwamo lwayunviikana omu nju yooshi baliyikeere mo.
ACT 2:3 Haabonekana n'ebiri nka birimi by'omuliro, byachigaba; byanaja oku ngasi muguma wabo.
ACT 2:4 Abo bigirizwa booshi bayunjuzwa Muuka-Mutagatiifu, banarhondera kuderha omu zindi ndimi, gukulikirana n'oku Muuka-Mutagatiifu abahaaga obuhashe b'okuderha.
ACT 2:5 Mw'amo mango, eYerusaleema haliiri aBayaahudi baguma bakengaga Nnamahanga, bahulukiraga omu bihugo byooshi by'egulu.
ACT 2:6 Oloola lwamo lwabeere lwayunviikana, abantu banene bachiigusha, basoomerwa bweneene bulaala ngasi muguma aliiri abayunva baaderha omu lulimi lwage lw'akaburhano.
ACT 2:7 Booshi basoomerwa, banayuumirwa, baalema baabazana ntya: «Abaala bantu bali baderha, ka booshi barhali Bagalilaaya?
ACT 2:8 Gurhe ngasi muguma weerhu y'abayunva omu lulimi lwage lw'akaburhano?
ACT 2:9 Omu rhwewe hali abarhengeere omu gihugo ch'aBapariti, ech'aBameedi na ech'aBaelaamu. Hali abalama omu gihugo ch'eMezopotamiya, ech'eYudeeya na ech'eGapadokiya, ech'ePonto na ech'eAziya,
ACT 2:10 ech'eFurigiya na ech'ePamfiliya, ech'eMiisiri n'oluhande lwa ech'eLibiya luli hoofu n'egishagala ch'eKureene. Kandi omu rhwewe hali abahiisi b'ogurhengera eRooma,
ACT 2:11 hali aBayaahudi n'abandi bayemeeraga edini ly'ekiyaahudi, aBakereeti n'aBaharaabu. Aliko rhweshi rhuli rhwabayunva baaderha omu ndimi zeerhu ebijiro by'obuhashe Nnamahanga ajirire!»
ACT 2:12 Booshi baali basomeerwe bweneene n'okuyuumirwa, baabazana ntya: «Bichi ebiila biderhere?»
ACT 2:13 Aliko baguma omu bo bashekera abigirizwa n'okuderha ntya: «Barhamiriire edivaayi y'omuhyo!»
ACT 2:14 Petero aja ayimanga haguma na zila ntumwa ekumi na nguma, aderha ntya n'omulenge munene: «Mwe bantu b'eYudeeya nenyu mweshi mwe mulamire eYerusaleema, munyunvirize, munamenye bwinja ebi binwa nashonda kubabwira!
ACT 2:15 Abaala bantu barharhamiriire nk'oku mukengereere, kwenge zichiri saa esharhu z'eseezi.
ACT 2:16 Aliko ebiila bi Nnamahanga aderhaga kugerera omuleebi Yoweeri mpu:
ACT 2:17 ‹Omu siku zizinda, nji nayandaaza oMuuka gwani oku bantu booshi; bagala benyu n'abanyere benyu nji baleeba, emisole yenyu nji yabonekerwa, n'abashaaja benyu nji baloorha.
ACT 2:18 Neechi, mw'ezo siku, abaja baani, abalume n'abakazi, nji nabayandaaza k'oMuuka gwani, nji banaleeba.
ACT 2:19 Nji najira ebigiriginjo gurhengera elugulu omu mpingu n'ebimenyeeso eshiishi omu gulu, nji haaba eshagama, omuliro n'oluhomo l'omuusi.
