ACT 2:20 Ezuuba nji lyahindulwa mwizimya n'omwezi nji gwahindulwa shagama, embere olusiku lwa Nnaweerhu luyinje, olo lusiku lunene, kandi l'obukuuze.
ACT 2:21 Mw'amo mango, ngasi yeeshi nji wahema oburhabaale oku ziino lya Nnaweerhu nj'achungulwa.›
ACT 2:22 «Mwe bantu b'eIsraheeli, muyunve ebi binwa! Nnamahanga abayeerekere bwinjabwinja oku Yeesu w'eNazareeti ali muntu arhumaga embere zenyu kugerera ebijiro by'obuhashe, ebigiriginjo n'ebimenyeeso. Nnamahanga ajiraga ebyo booshi ahagarhi kenyu kugerera Yeesu, nk'oku mubiyinji mwenyine.
ACT 2:23 Oyu Yeesu ahirwaga omu maboko menyu, nk'oku Nnamahanga ashondaga, na nka okw'amenyaga yenyine gurhengera miira. Nenyu mwamuyirhire omu kumubamba oku musalaaba, kugerera abantu babi.
ACT 2:24 Aliko, Nnamahanga nj'amufuulire omu kumulikuula omu malumwa m'olufu, bulaala birhakagalikeene ashwekwe na lo.
ACT 2:25 Kwenge Daawudi aderhere ntya elugulu wa Yeesu: ‹Naliiri nabona Nnaweerhu embere zaani ngasi mango, bulaala ali ekulyo kwani yi ntashaganywa.
ACT 2:26 Cho girhumire omurhima gwani gusiimire n'olulimi lwani lushagalukire; kandi omubiri gwani nago nji gwahuumukira omu bulangaalire,
ACT 2:27 kwenge orhakandekeerera kubeera ekuzimu; orhakanaleka oMutagatiifu waawe abola.
ACT 2:28 Wanyeerekere enjira z'akalamo, nji wanyunjuza obushagaluke embere zaawe.›»
ACT 2:29 Petero ashuba kuderha ntya: «Beene beerhu, bihemere mbabwire bwinjabwinja ebilolere shookuluza weerhu Daawudi: afiire, ahambwa n'eshinda yaage echiba eno mwerhu kugera zeene.
ACT 2:30 N'obuula aliiri muleebi, aliyinji oku Nnamahanga amulahizizaga endahiro oku nj'ayikaza muguma omu baburhwa baage oku ntebe yaage y'obwami.
ACT 2:31 Daawudi alibwene embere obufuuke bwa Krisitu, anabuderha ko ntya: ‹Arhalekeererwaga kubeera ekuzimu, n'omubiri gwage gurhabolaga.›
ACT 2:32 Nnamahanga afuulire oyo Yeesu, rhweshi rhunali bahamiiriza boboola bufuuke.
ACT 2:33 Abeere azamuulwa ekulyo kwa Nnamahanga, Eshe amuha Muuka-Mutagatiifu walilaganyizwe. Naye arhuyandaazize ye, nk'okuula muli mwabona, munali mwayunva.
ACT 2:34 Kwenge arhali Daawudi wazamuukiraga empingu, aliko yeewe yenyine aderhere ntya: ‹Nnaweerhu Nnamahanga abwirire Nnaweerhu ntya: “Yikala ekulyo kwani,
ACT 2:35 guhika amango nji naajira abanzi baawe ndabarhiro yaawe.”›
ACT 2:36 Leero, bihemere olubaga looshi lw'eIsraheeli lumenye bwinja oku ola Yeesu mwabambaga oku musalaaba, Nnamahanga amujirire kuba Nnaweerhu na Krisitu!»
ACT 2:37 Enyuma z'okuyunva ebyoola binwa, abantu baababazwa bweneene omu mirhima yaabo n'okuva baabaza Petero n'ezindi ntumwa ntya: «Beene beerhu, gurhe rhujirage?»
ACT 2:38 Petero abashubiza ntya: «Muleke ebyaaha byenyu, na ngasi muguma omu mwabo abatiizwe oku ziino lya Yeesu Krisitu yi mubabalirwa ebyaaha byenyu. Na ntyo, mwanayankiirira Muuka-Mutagatiifu nka luhembo.
ACT 2:39 Kwenge echilagaane cha Nnamahanga chiri chenyu, ch'abaana benyu n'abantu booshi balamire hale; k'okuderha oku chiri ch'abantu booshi Nnaweerhu Nnamahanga nj'ahamagala.»
ACT 2:40 Petero ashuba kubabwira ebindi binwa binene by'okubayinginga n'okubayunviisa. Alema aderha ntya: «Mugichungule gurhenga mw'echi gisisi ch'ebyaaha!»
ACT 2:41 Abayankiiriraga ebinwa byaage babatiizwa. Oloola lusiku, hoofu bantu bihumbi bisharhu bayongeereka omu chigusho ch'abemeezi.
ACT 2:42 Abemeezi bagendekera gukulikira enyigirizo z'eNtumwa, kulama echinyabuguma, kugabaana omugati haguma n'ogusaliira.
ACT 2:43 Ebigiriginjo n'ebimenyeeso binene byaliiri kujirika n'eNtumwa oku bulyo ngasi muguma alema ayunva obuuba.
ACT 2:44 Abemeezi booshi baliiri haguma n'ogushangiira byooshi baligwerhe.
ACT 2:45 Baliiri baguza amashwa maabo n'ebintu byaabo, n'efuranga zarhengaga mo baliiri bazigabana gukulikirana n'obulagiirire bwa ngasi muguma.
ACT 2:46 Ngasi lusiku, omu bunviikane, baliiri baaja omu Nju ya Nnamahanga. Baliiri bagabaana omugati n'ogusangira ebiryo byaabo omu nju zaabo n'obushagaluke haguma n'omurhima mwinja.
ACT 2:47 Baliiri bakuuza Nnamahanga n'abantu booshi bali basiimire bo. Na ngasi lusiku, Nnaweerhu aliiri ayongeera abachungwirwe oku chigusho ch'abemeezi.
ACT 3:1 Lusiku luguma, Petero na Yohaana baliiri bazamuukira omu Nju ya Nnamahanga aha saa mwenda z'ezuuba, cho chaliiri gihe ch'ogusaliira.
ACT 3:2 Mw'ebyo bishanji, abantu baliiri baheeka omulume waburhwaga eyi chirema. Abo bantu bagendaga bamuhira ngasi lusiku hoofu n'omulyango gw'eNju ya Nnamahanga guyirikwa «Mulyango Gukwiriire» y'ahemuuze oburhabaale oku baliiri baaja mo.
ACT 3:3 Abwene Petero na Yohaana bakola baaja omu Nju ya Nnamahanga, arhondera kubahema oburhabaale.
ACT 3:4 Petero na Yohaana bamuloleereza, naye Petero amubwira ntya: «Orhulole!»
ACT 3:5 Naye abalola, kwenge alilangaliire oku hali echi bamuha.
ACT 3:6 Aliko Petero amubwira ntya: «Ntagwerhe furanga changwa oro, aliko echi ngwerhe, nguheere cho: omu ziino lya Yeesu Krisitu w'eNazareeti, yimanga onalambagire!»
ACT 3:7 Amufarhira oku kuboko kw'ekulyo, amuyimanza. Ho n'aho, ebishando byaage n'orhuzirabulongo rhwage byakomera.
ACT 3:8 Ayuumuka oku liguma, ayimanga n'ogurhondera kulambagira. Aja haguma nabo omu Nju ya Nnamahanga eyi ali alambagira, abalalabalala n'ogukuuza Nnamahanga.
ACT 3:9 Abantu booshi bamubona ali alambagira n'ogukuuza Nnamahanga.
ACT 3:10 Bamurhegeera oku y'olaala wagendaga ayikala halaala «Mulyango Gukwiriire» gw'eNju ya Nnamahanga guhema oburhabaale. Basoomerwa banahwerwa n'ebyamubereere.
ACT 3:11 Oyo muntu abeere arhagirhengere ku Petero na Yohaana, abantu basoomerwa, balibirhira emunda bali, hoofu n'embaraza y'eNju ya Nnamahanga eyirikwa «Mbaraza ya Solomoono.»
ACT 3:12 Petero abwene ebyoola, abaza olubaga ntya: «Mwe bantu b'eIsraheeli, girhumire mwasoomerera ogufuma kw'oyu muntu? Girhumire mwarhuloleereza nka rhwewe rhwe rhwalambagiriisaga ye oku buhashe bwerhu rhwenyine changwa elugulu w'ogukwanana kwerhu embere za Nnamahanga?
ACT 3:13 Nnamahanga w'Abrahaamu, Isaka na Yakobo, Nnamahanga wa bashookuluza beerhu, akuuzize omukozi waage Yeesu. Oyu Yeesu yi mwabo mwahaanaga mwanamulahira embere za Pilaato, n'obo yeewe abaaga amahiga kumulikuula.
ACT 3:14 Mwewe, mwalahira oMutagatiifu na Okwaneene, mwanahema babalikuulire omwisi w'abantu.
ACT 3:15 Mwayirha ohaana akalamo, aliko yeewe Nnamahanga amufuulire omu bafu; neerhu rhuli bahamiiriza bw'obo bufuuke.
ACT 3:16 Oyu muntu muli mwabona munamuyinji, eziino lya Yeesu n'obwemeezi kw'elyo ziino byo byamukomeeze. N'obwemeezi kugerera Yeesu bo bwaheere oyu muntu amagala makwiriire nk'oku mubwene.
ACT 3:17 «Na bunoola, beene beerhu, nyinji oku mwabo n'abakulu benyu mwajiriraga Yeesu ebyoola omu buhwinja.
ACT 3:18 Na Nnamahanga ayeneeze ntya eby'abalaganyaga embere kugerera ebinwa by'abaleebi booshi oku Krisitu waage alibuzwa.
ACT 3:19 Mujaage mwaleka ebyaaha byenyu, munagalukire Nnamahanga y'ebyaaha byenyu bibabalirwa.
ACT 3:20 Na ntyo, Nnaweerhu abahumuusa, n'okubarhumira Krisitu, ye Yeesu, olaala achishogaga embere elugulu wenyu.
ACT 3:21 Alikwaneene gurhanga kubeera empingu guhika amango ebintu byooshi byayeenera nk'oku Nnamahanga aderhaga miira kulengera abaleebi baage batagatiifu.
ACT 3:22 Muusa aliderhere ntya: ‹Nnaweerhu, Nnamahanga wenyu, nj'abaha omuleebi warhengera omu beene benyu oli nka nyoono. Nji mwamuyunva omu byooshi nj'ababwira.
ACT 3:23 Aliko ngasi yeeshi nj'orhayunva oyo muleebi nj'achiibwa looshi omu lubaga n'okuyirhwa.›
ACT 3:24 N'abaleebi booshi, gurhengera ku Samweri n'abamukulikiraga, nabo baderhere, banabala elugulu w'emyaazi y'eziila siku rhulamire zeene.
ACT 3:25 Mwabo, muli bagala b'abaleebi n'egihango Nnamahanga ajiraga na bashookuluza benyu chiri chenyu. Kwenge Nnamahanga ajiraga cho omu kubwira Abrahaamu ntya: ‹Emilala yooshi y'egulu nji yaagishwa omu gisisi chaawe.›
ACT 3:26 Amango Nnamahanga ahaanaga omukozi waage, arhanga kumurhuma emwenyu kubagisha, omu gukuula ngasi muguma wenyu omu mabi maage.»
ACT 4:1 Petero na Yohaana babeere bachiri bayigiriza olubaga, abadaahwa, omukulu w'abalanzi b'eNju ya Nnamahanga, n'aBasadukaayo baahulukira.
ACT 4:2 Abo bakulu bali bakalihire okubona Petero na Yohaana bali bayigiriza olubaga n'okubala oku obufuuke gurhenga omu bafu bubonekana kugerera Yeesu.
ACT 4:3 Babashweka n'okubahira omu munyororo kugera olusiku lwakulikiraga kwenge lyaliiri likola golo.
ACT 4:4 Aliko banene omu bayunvaga ezo nyigirizo bayemeera Yeesu. Oluganjo lw'abemeezi lwahikiira hoofu balume bihumbi birhaano.
ACT 4:5 Bwacheere eseezi, abakulu n'abashamuka b'aBayaahudi, n'abigiriza b'amarhegeko bachigusha eYerusaleema.
ACT 4:6 Baliiri haguma n'omudaahwa mukulu Hanaasi, Kayaafa, Yohaana, Alegizandere n'abandi bantu booshi baliiri b'omu mulala gw'omudaahwa mukulu.
ACT 4:7 Bamalire kuyimanza Petero na Yohaana ahagarhi kaabo, bababaza ntya: «Oku buhashe buchi changwa oku ziino lya nde mwajiraga ebyoola?»
ACT 4:8 Petero eyi ayunjwizwe Muuka-Mutagatiifu, ababwira ntya: «Ego mwe bakulu b'olubaga nenyu mwe bashamuka b'aBayaahudi,
ACT 4:9 rhubazizwe zeene elugulu w'amenja rhwajiriire echirema n'oku bulyo chafumyagwa.
ACT 4:10 Leero mwabo mweshi, n'olubaga looshi lw'eIsraheeli, mumenye bwinja: oyu muntu ayimangire embere zenyu n'amagala makwiriire oku ziino lya Yeesu Krisitu w'eNazareeti, olaala mwabambaga oku musalaaba, aliko Nnamahanga amufuula omu bafu.
ACT 4:11 Yeewe y'aMandiko Matagatiifu maderhere ko ntya: ‹Ebaale mwabo mwe muyumbaka mwalahiraga, lyo lyahindukire ly'engenzi, ly'okuyumbakira ko.›
ACT 4:12 Obuchunguke burhali omu windi muntu, kwenge nta lindi ziino omu gulu abantu bahaabirwe, lyagarhuchungwire.»
ACT 4:13 Abantu b'akabuga k'aBayaahudi babeere baabona Petero na Yohaana baderha n'oobushiru, basoomerwa, kwenge bali bayinji oku baliiri bantu konyine barhasomaga. Baanalimenyere oku boowe bo baliiri haguma na Yeesu.
ACT 4:14 Aliko, nk'okuula bali babwene olaala muntu bafumyaga ayimangire eburhambi bwabo, baabula echi bagashuba kuderha.
ACT 4:15 Baava babarhegeka oku barhange barhenge mw'ako kabuga. Bala bakulu boowe basigala omu mahwe.
ACT 4:16 Baabazana ntya: «Gurhe rhujirage abaala bantu? Bulaala abantu booshi b'eYerusaleema bayinji bwinja okw'echimenyeeso chabeere kugerera bo. Rhurhakanagala kugihakana.
ACT 4:17 Aliko y'omwazi gw'echoola chimenyeeso gurhayandaala bweneene omu lubaga, rhubakalihire oku barhachiderhaga n'omuntu n'omuguma elugulu w'eziino lya Yeesu.»
ACT 4:18 Baaja bahamagala Petero na Yohaana, banabarhegeka mpu barhachiderhaga changwa okuyigiriza chiro n'eliguma oku ziino lya Yeesu.
ACT 4:19 Aliko Petero na Yohaana babashubiza ntya: «Ka bikwaneene embere za Nnamahanga oku rhubakenge ahaali haage? Mugishogage,
ACT 4:20 kwenge rhwabo rhurhakagala kuleka kuderha ebintu rhwabwene ko rhwanayunva.»
ACT 4:21 Abantu b'akabuga k'aBayaahudi baashuba kubakalihira, banaja babalikuula. Barhaali babwene enjira y'okubahana, bulaala olubaga looshi lwaliiri lwakuuza Nnamahanga oku byooshi byabaaga.
ACT 4:22 Oyo muntu bajiriraga echoola kimenyeeso ch'ogufuma, aligwerhe myaaka minene ku makumi mane.
ACT 4:23 Babeere balikuulwa, Petero na Yohaana baaja kubalira abaabo byooshi abakulu b'abadaahwa n'abashamuka b'aBayaahudi bababwirire.
ACT 4:24 Bamalire kuyunva eyo myaazi, booshi basaliira Nnamahanga n'omurhima muguma. Baaderha ntya: «Nnaweerhu, wooyo we wajiraga echaalege, egulu n'enyanja, na byooshi biba omu byo.
ACT 4:25 Wooyo we waderhaga ntya kugerera Muuka-Mutagatiifu, omu buunu bwa shookuluza weerhu Daawudi, mukozi waawe: ‹Charhumire abarhali Bayaahudi baruukura n'embaga zagwarha emihigo erhagwerhe kamaro?
ACT 4:26 Abaami b'egulu bachikerekere n'abakulu bachigushire haguma yi balwisa Nnaweerhu Nnamahanga na Krisitu waage.›
ACT 4:27 Kwenge biri by'okuli oku Heroode na Ponsiyo Pilaato bayunvikeene muno gishagala haguma n'abarhali Bayaahudi n'olubaga lw'eIsraheeli kulahira Yeesu, omukozi waawe mutagatiifu, olaala wagishogaga.
ACT 4:28 Bajiraga ntyo, yi bayeeneza byooshi wabaaga warheganyize gurhenga miira oku buhashe bwawe n'emihigo yaawe.
ACT 4:29 Leero Nnaweerhu, olole bwinja obuhambaazi bwabo, ogaliise abaja baawe okubala eChinwa chaawe buzira buuba.
ACT 4:30 Ojaage walambuula okuboko kwawe y'abantu bafume, ebimenyeeso n'ebigiriginjo bibe kugerera eziino lya Yeesu, mukozi waawe mutagatiifu.»
ACT 4:31 Bamalire gusaliira, ahantu bali bachigushire hadirhimana bweneene, booshi bayunjula Muuka-Mutagatiifu. Barhondera kubala eChinwa cha Nnamahanga buzira buuba.
ACT 4:32 Abemeezi booshi baligwerhe omurhima muguma n'enkengeero nguma. Ntaaye waderhaga oku ebikulo byaage biri byaage yenyine, aliko bagendaga bashangiira byooshi bali bagwerhe.
ACT 4:33 Entumwa zaliiri zahamiiriza n'obuhashe bunene obufuuke bwa Nnaweerhu Yeesu, n'omugisho munene gwaliiri oku bo booshi.
ACT 4:34 Nta muguma omu bo walikeneere echintu, kwenge booshi bali bagwerhe amashwa changwa enju, bagendaga babiguza, banaleerha efuranga babiguzaga.
ACT 4:35 Bagendaga bahira zo embere z'eNtumwa, n'enyuma zanagabirwa ngasi muguma gukulikirana n'obulagiirire bwage.
ACT 4:36 Haliiri oMulaawi muguma oyirikwa Yozefu, aliiri muburhwa w'oku chizimba ch'eGipuro. Entumwa zamushembula eziino lya Baranaaba, kw'okuderha «Muntu okomeza abandi omurhima.»
ACT 4:37 Aguza eshwa aligwerhe, aleerha efuranga anazihira embere z'eNtumwa.
ACT 5:1 Haliiri mulume muguma oyirikwa Hananiya haguma na mukaage Safira. Baguza eshwa lyaabo.
ACT 5:2 Omu bunviikane, yeewe na mukaage baabisha muhango muguma oku furanga baliguzaga. Ezasigalaga, aziheeka anazihira embere z'eNtumwa.
ACT 5:3 Petero amubaza ntya: «Ego Hananiya, charhumire Shetaani aja omu murhima gwawe, guhika okubeehya Muuka-Mutagatiifu omu kubisha furanga ziguma waguzaga eshwa?
ACT 5:4 Egihe eliila shwa lyalichiri lyaawe, ka lirhaliiri bikulo byaawe? Na chiro egihe lyaguzwaga, k'efuranga orhakazikoleeseze okw'oshondere? Chajaaga charhuma wakengera omu murhima gwawe echijiro chiri ntya? Arhali bantu warhebekere, sy'aliko Nnamahanga!»
ACT 5:5 Hananiya abeere ayunva ebyoola binwa, ahena n'okuva afa. Booshi bayunvaga ogo mwazi bagwarhwa n'obuuba bunene.
ACT 5:6 Emisole yaliiri ahoola yayimanga, yarhuba omubiri gwage, yaguheeka embuga, yanaguhamba.
ACT 5:7 Hagerere hoofu saa esharhu, mukaage aja mw'eyo nju buzira kumenya ebyabeere.
ACT 5:8 Petero amubaza ntya: «Ombwirage bwinja, ka kw'eyi ngulo ku mwaguzaga eshwa?» Ashubiza ntya: «Neechi, kw'eyoola ngulo.»
ACT 5:9 Petero ashuba kumubaza ntya: «Gurhe mwagalaga kuyunviikana yi mugeregeza Muuka-Mutagatiifu wa Nnaweerhu? Ololage! Amagulu m'abahambaga balo mo mano oku mulyango. Naawe baguheeka!»
ACT 5:10 Ho n'aho ahena embere z'amagulu ma Petero n'ogufa. Elaala misole yajiire omu nju, y'abugaana afiire. Yaheeka omubiri gwage yanaguhamba eburhambi bw'eba.
ACT 5:11 Echigusho chooshi ch'abemeezi na booshi bayunvaga ogoola mwazi bagwarhwa n'obuuba bunene.
ACT 5:12 Ebimenyeeso n'ebigiriginjo binene byaliiri kujirika omu bantu kulengera eNtumwa. Abemeezi baliiri gushimaanana booshi omu Mbaraza ya Solomoono.
ACT 5:13 Nta muntu n'omuguma orhali mwemeezi wagendaga abayegeera, aliko olubaga lwabakenga bweneene.
ACT 5:14 Abantu banene, abalume n'abakazi, baliiri bayemeera Nnaweerhu. Bagendekera kuluga bweneene.
ACT 5:15 Baliiri baleerha abalwala oku njira zigalihire, banabalyaamiza oku bishanja n'oku bipoyi, yi hano Petero agera, chiro egichuuchu chaage chigale gushukulira baguma omu bo.
ACT 5:16 Abantu banene bagendaga barhenga n'omu bishagala bitureene n'eYerusaleema eyi baheekere abalwala n'abantu bafarhirwe n'abazimu. Booshi baliiri baafumywa.
ACT 5:17 Omudaahwa mukulu n'abantu baage booshi, k'okuderha abantu b'echigusho ch'aBasadukaayo, baaja bayunvira eNtumwa obongwa.
ACT 5:18 Bazifarha n'okuzihira omu munyororo gw'abantu booshi.
ACT 5:19 Aliko obudufu, malahika wa Nnaweerhu achinguula emilyango y'omunyororo. Akuula mo zila ntumwa n'okuzibwira ntya:
ACT 5:20 «Mugende, muje omu Nju ya Nnamahanga, munabalire olubaga byooshi biyerekeere kano kalamo gahyaahya.»
ACT 5:21 Ezo ntumwa zabeere zayunva ebyoola binwa, zalamukira eseeziseezi omu Nju ya Nnamahanga, zanarhondera kuyigiriza. Omudaahwa mukulu n'abantu baage baahika. Bahamagaza akabuga k'aBayaahudi n'enshimaanano yooshi y'abashamuka b'aBaisraheeli. Banarhuma abalanzi kuja omu munyororo kuleerha eNtumwa.
ACT 5:22 Aliko abalanzi bagerere omu munyororo, barhababugaana mo. Baaja bagaluka n'okuja kubwira abakulu ntya:
ACT 5:23 «Rhwabugaanire omunyororo guchingirwe bwinja n'abalanzi bayimangire embere z'emilyango. Aliko rhwabeere rhwachinguula, ntaaye rhwabugaanire mo!»
ACT 5:24 Egihe omukulu w'abalanzi b'eNju ya Nnamahanga n'abakulu b'abadaahwa bayunvaga ebyoola binwa, bayuumirwa, banachiibaza akaba bichi byahikiire eNtumwa.
ACT 5:25 Muntu muguma aja ayinja kubabalira ntya: «Tala okw'abantu mwahiraga omu munyororo bayimangire omu Nju ya Nnamahanga, banali bayigiriza olubaga!»
ACT 5:26 Omukulu w'abalanzi n'abantu baage baava baaja kubaleerha. Babaleerha buzira kubalibuza, kwenge baliyuubahire olubaga lwakababanda amabaale.
ACT 5:27 Bayuusize kubaleerha, babaheeka embere w'akabuga k'aBayaahudi. Omudaahwa mukulu ababaza ntya:
ACT 5:28 «Ka rhurhalibabuzize bweneene ogurhachiyigiriza mw'eryoola ziino? Tala oku mwayunjwize eYerusaleema n'enyigirizo zenyu! Munashondere gurhuheesa eshagama y'oyu muntu!»
ACT 5:29 Petero n'ezindi ntumwa bashubiza ntya: «Bihemere ogukenga Nnamahanga ahaali h'abantu.
ACT 5:30 Nnamahanga wa bashookuluza beerhu, afuulire Yeesu mwayirhaga omu kumubamba oku musalaaba.
ACT 5:31 Anamuzamwire ekulyo kwage nka Mukulu na Muchunguzi, y'aha aBaisraheeli obulyo b'okuleka ebyaaha na Nnamahanga ababalire ebyaaha byaabo.
ACT 5:32 Rhuli bahamiiriza b'ebyoola byooshi haguma na Muuka-Mutagatiifu Nnamahanga aheere abamukenga.»
ACT 5:33 Abantu b'akabuga k'aBayaahudi baaja bakaliha looshi omu kuyunva ebyoola binwa, banashonda kuyirha eNtumwa.
ACT 5:34 Aliko haliiri omu bo oMufarisaayo oyirikwa Gamaliyeeri. Aliiri mwigiriza w'amarhegeko okengerwe n'olubaga looshi. Ayimanga ahagarhi k'akabuga k'aBayaahudi n'ogurhegeka barhange bahuluse eNtumwa hityu.
ACT 5:35 Enyuma, aderha ntya: «Bantu b'eIsraheeli, muchilange oku bimukola kujirira abaala bantu.
ACT 5:36 Embere za bino bihe, hahulukiire muntu muguma oyirikwa Teuda. Aliiri achiderha oku ali muntu mukulu, n'abantu hoofu magana mane bamukulikira. Aliko ayirhwa, booshi bamukulikiraga balibirha n'echigusho chaage chaafa.
ACT 5:37 Enyuma zaage, omu gihe ch'oluganjo lw'abantu, haahulukira Mugalilaaya muguma oyirikwa Yuuda, arhuma abantu bamukulikira. Naye ayirhwa, na booshi bamukulikiraga bashandaazwa.
ACT 5:38 Leero bunoola mbabwirire oku murhakulikiraga abaala bantu, munabaleke bagende. Bulaala, akaba ebi bali kujira guli muhigo changwa kaasi k'abantu, byaafa.
ACT 5:39 Aliko akaba ebyoola birhengeere emwa Nnamahanga, murhakagala kubahanza. Muchilange mwangahengeera eyi muli mwalwisa Nnamahanga!» Abantu b'akabuga k'aBayaahudi bayunva amahano ma Gamaliyeeri.
ACT 5:40 Bahamagala eNtumwa, bazishurhiisa, banazirhegeka oku zirhachiyigirizaga oku ziino lya Yeesu. Buzinda, bazilikuula.
ACT 5:41 Entumwa zarhenga omu kabuga k'aBayaahudi eyi zishagalukire okubona zaganjirwe oku zikwaneene gukeneerezwa elugulu w'eziino lya Yeesu.
ACT 5:42 Bagendeerera ngasi lusiku kuyigiriza omu Nju ya Nnamahanga n'omu nju z'abantu, n'okubala oMwazi Mwinja gwa Yeesu, ye Krisitu.
ACT 6:1 Mw'ezoola siku, oluganjo lw'abemeezi lwaliiri lwayushuuka. aBayaahudi baliiri kuderha olulimi lw'eKigiriki barhondera kulundumira aBayaahudi baliiri kuderha olulimi lw'eGiheburaniya, bulaala abashumbakazi baabo baali babonereerwe egihe ch'okugaba ebiryo ngasi lusiku.
ACT 6:2 Zilaala ntumwa ekumi n'ebiri zagusha abemeezi booshi, zanababwira ntya: «Birhakwaneene rhulekeerere kuyigiriza eChinwa cha Nnamahanga mpu rhubeere rhuli rhwagaba ebiryo.
ACT 6:3 Cho girhumire, beene beerhu, mushonde ahagarhi kenyu bantu mushanvu bahamiriizwe bwinja n'abantu, bayunjwire Muuka-Mutagatiifu n'obwenge bunene. Boowe, barhwaheereza akoola kaasi.
ACT 6:4 Ntyo neerhu, rhwakomeza gusaliira n'okuyigiriza eChinwa cha Nnamahanga.»
ACT 6:5 Abemeezi booshi bali chigushire ahoola basiima eyoola myaazi. Bachishoga Sitefaano, muntu w'obwemeezi bunene onayunjwire Muuka-Mutagatiifu, Firipo, Porokoro, Nikanori, Timooni, Parimena na Nikola w'eAntiyokiya wayemeeraga edini ly'eKiyaahudi.
ACT 6:6 Bamoleka bo eNtumwa, nazo zabasaliirira eyi zibalambuliire kw'amaboko.
ACT 6:7 Echinwa cha Nnamahanga chaliiri kuyaalagala omu bantu, oluganjo lw'abemeezi lwaliiri kuyushuuka bweneene eYerusaleema, n'echigusho chinene ch'abadaahwa chayemeera Yeesu.
ACT 6:8 Sitefaano aliyunjwire emigisho n'obuhashe bunene. Byaarhuma agenda ajira ebigiriginjo n'ebimenyeeso binene omu lubaga.
ACT 6:9 Aliko bantu baguma, barhondera obuhaka na Sitefaano. Abo bantu bahulikiraga omu sinagoogi ederhwa y'«aBantu Barhengaga omu Buja», barhengaga omu gishagala ch'eKureene n'eche Alegizanduriya. Abandi bahulukiraga omu gihugo ch'eKilikiya n'eche Aziya.
ACT 6:10 Aliko barhagalaga guhima Sitefaano kwenge aligwerhe bwenge bunene, na Muuka-Mutagatiifu aliiri kumuha ebinwa by'okuderha.
ACT 6:11 Baaja baaha abantu efuranga yi baderha oku: «Rhwamuyunvaga ali aderha ebinwa by'okudukanga Muusa na Nnamahanga.»
ACT 6:12 Bararusa olubaga n'abashamuka b'aBayaahudi haguma n'abigiriza b'amarhegeko. Bayegeera Sitefaano, bamurhoola, banamuheeka omu kabuga k'aBayaahudi.
ACT 6:13 Baleerha abahamiiriza b'obubeeshi baliiri baderha ntya: «Oyu muntu arhali aleka kuderha ebinwa bibi elugulu w'eNju ntagatiifu ya Nnamahanga n'eRhegeko lya Muusa.
ACT 6:14 Kwenge rhwamuyunvaga aderha oku Yeesu w'eNazareeti ashanda eyi Nju ya Nnamahanga, anahindamula n'emicho Muusa arhulekeraga.»
ACT 6:15 Abantu booshi baliiri mw'akoola kabuga k'aBayaahudi babeere bali baheneereza Sitefaano, baava baabona amalanga maage makola mashushire nk'ama malahika.
ACT 7:1 Omudaahwa mukulu aja abaza Sitefaano ntya: «K'ebi bali bakuderha ko biri by'okuli?»
ACT 7:2 Sitefaano ashubiza ntya: «Ba daarha na beene beerhu, munyunvirize! Nnamahanga w'obukuuze abonekeraga Abrahaamu, shookuluza weerhu, egihe aliiri omu gihugo ch'eMezopotamiya, embere alame omu gishagala ch'eHaraani.
ACT 7:3 Anamubwira ntya: ‹Rhenga omu gihugo chaawe n'omu mulala gwawe, oje omu gihugo nji nakuyeereka.›
ACT 7:4 Abrahaamu aja arhenga omu gihugo ch'aBakalidayo aja kulama omu gishagala ch'eHaraani. Enyuma w'olufu lw'eshe, Nnamahanga amubungiisa kandi gurhenga eHaraani, ayinja kulama mu chinoola gihugo mulamire mo bunoola.
ACT 7:5 Nnamahanga arhamuhaaga agashambala mu chinoola gihugo, arhamuhaaga chiro ahantu agahira okugulu. Aliko amulaganya okumuheereza cho n'ababurhwa baage nachiro nta mwana abaga aza kugwarha.
ACT 7:6 Nnamahanga amubwira ntya: ‹Ababurhwa baawe nji baalama nka bahiisi omu gihugo chabeene, nji babajira baja, nji banabalibuza myaaka magana mane.
ACT 7:7 Aliko egihugo nji baaba babeere mo baja, nyoono nye nji nagihana. Buzinda bw'aho nji babunguluka n'okumparamya hanoola.›
ACT 7:8 Ntyo, Nnamahanga aja ajira endaganyo haguma n'Abrahaamu. Echimenyeso chaayo kwali gukembuulwa. Aja aburha Isaka anamukembuula olusiku lwa munaane enyuma z'okuburhwa. Isaka naye akembuula omugala Yakobo, na Yakobo akembuula bashookuluza beerhu, bo balaala bagala baage ekumi na babiri.
ACT 7:9 «Bashookuluza bagwarha obongwa ku Yozefu, bamuguza y'aheekwa omu gihugo ch' eMiisiri nka muja. Aliko Nnamahanga aliiri haguma naye,
ACT 7:10 anamukuula omu malibuko maage mooshi. Amuha obwenge bunene n'okuyemeerwa embere za Farao, mwami w'egihugo ch'eMiisiri. Farao naye amujira mwimangizi w'echo gihugo n'enju yaage yooshi.
ACT 7:11 Enyuma z'aho, enzara nene yaba omu gihugo chooshi ch'eMiisiri n'omu gihugo ch'eKanaana. Amalibuko maliiri manene bweneene. Bashookuluza beerhu barhaalichiri baabona echi baalya.
ACT 7:12 Yakobo abeere ayunva oku hali engano omu gihugo ch'eMiisiri, arhuma yo bashookuluza beerhu oku burhanzi.
ACT 7:13 Bajiire y'obwakabiri, Yozefu achimenyeesa oku beene baabo, na Farao aja amenya omulala gwa Yozefu.
ACT 7:14 Enyuma, Yozefu arhuma baje guhamagala eshe Yakobo n'omulala gwage gooshi. Abantu b'omulala gwage baliiri makumi gali mushanvu na barhaano.
ACT 7:15 Yakobo aja eMiisiri, afiira yo n'abandi bashookuluza beerhu.
ACT 7:16 Babaheeka eShekemu, banabahamba omu shinda Abrahaamu agulaga emwa beene Hamoori oku gichiiro ch'efuranga.
ACT 7:17 «Egihe chabeere chiri hoofu Nnamahanga alikwaneene kuyeeneza mo echilagaane ahaaga Abrahaamu, olubaga lwerhu lwaluga, lwanaba lunene omu gihugo ch'eMiisiri.
ACT 7:18 Omwami muhyaahya orhaliyinji Yozefu ava ayima oku gihugo ch'eMiisiri.
ACT 7:19 Oyoola mwami arhebeka olubaga lwerhu, alibuza bashookuluza beerhu, abalekeesa enjolyaana zaabo yi zifa.
ACT 7:20 «Mw'amo mango, Muusa aburhwa. Aliiri mwinja omu meesho ma Nnamahanga. Alilemberwe myeezi esharhu omu nju y'eshe.
ACT 7:21 Abeere abishwa embuga, mwali wa Farao amubugula, anamulemba nka mugala waage.
ACT 7:22 Muusa ayigirizwa omu bwenge bunene booshi bw'aBanyamiisiri, anaba muntu w'obuhashe omu binwa byaage n'omu bijiro byaage.
ACT 7:23 «Egihe ayeenezaga myaaka makumi mane, ahiga kuja kulambagirira beene baabo, b'aBaisraheeli.
ACT 7:24 Ava abona mwene waabo muguma oli alibuzwa n'oMunyamiisiri. Amulwira, anamuhoolera omu kuyirha oyoola Munyamiisiri.
ACT 7:25 Alikengereere oku beene baabo bakamenyere oku kugerera ye Nnamahanga abakuula omu buja. Aliko barhabimenyaga.
ACT 7:26 Olusiku lwakulikiraga, Muusa abugaana aBaisraheeli babiri bali baalwa. Omu gushonda abayunvisanye yi bagwarha omurhuula, ababwira ntya: ‹Ego baza wee, oku muli baguma! Chagarhuma mwalibuzanya?›
ACT 7:27 Aliko olaala waliiri alibuza owaabo ashunika Muusa n'okubaza ntya: ‹Nde wakujiraga mukulu na muzuuzi weerhu?
ACT 7:28 Ka wooyo oshondere kunyirha nk'oku nji wayirhaga olaala Munyamiisiri mulaagolo?›
ACT 7:29 Muusa ayunviirhe echoola chinwa, alibirha n'okuva abungira omu gihugo ch'eMidiyaani. Aburhira eyoola munda bagala babiri.
ACT 7:30 «Myaaka makumi mane yabeere yayeenera, malahika amubonekera omu mpinga y'omusozi gw'eSinaayi omu birimi by'omuliro byaliiri byagulumira omu gishaka.
ACT 7:31 Muusa abwene ebyoola, asoomererwa okoola kubonekerwa. Aliko egihe abaaga ali ayegeera y'achirhegeereza, ava ayunva omulenge gwa Nnaweerhu gwaderha ntya:
ACT 7:32 ‹Nyoono nye Nnamahanga wa bashookuluza baawe, Nnamahanga w'Abrahaamu, Isaka na Yakobo!› Muusa ahinda omusisi, arhanagishubiiraga kugendeerera kulola.
ACT 7:33 Nnaweerhu amubwira ntya: ‹Hogola ebiraato byaawe, kwenge hanoola oyimangire hali hantu hatagatiifu.
ACT 7:34 Nabwene bwinja amalibuko m'olubaga lwani luli omu gihugo ch'eMiisiri, nayunviirhe amalira maabo. Bo bunoola nayandageere kubalikuuza. Jaaga wayinja, nagurhuma eMiisiri.›
ACT 7:35 «Oyo Muusa y'aBaisraheeli balahiraga omu kuderha ntya: ‹Nde wakujiraga mukulu na muzuuzi weerhu?›, yeewe ye Nnamahanga arhumire nka mukulu na murhabaazi, kugerera oburhabaale bwa malahika wamubonekeraga omu gishaka.
ACT 7:36 Yeewe ye wakuulaga aBaisraheeli omu gihugo ch'eMiisiri omu kujira ebigiriginjo n'ebimenyeeso mw'echo gihugo, omu nyanja Ndukula n'omu mpinga mu myaaka makumi mane.
ACT 7:37 Kandi Muusa ye wabwiraga aBaisraheeli ntya: ‹Nnamahanga nj'abaha omuleebi oli nka nyoono gurhenga omu beene benyu.›
ACT 7:38 Egihe olubaga lw'eIsraheeli lwaliiri omu mpinga, oyo Muusa ye waliiri ahagarhi ka bashookuluza beerhu, na malahika waliiri amuganiiza oku musozi gw'eSinaayi. Yeewe ye wayankiiriraga ebinwa by'akalamo y'arhuha byo.
ACT 7:39 Aliko bashookuluza beerhu barhashondaga kumukenga, si bamulahira. Bachifiija omu mirhima yaabo mpu bagaluke eMiisiri.
ACT 7:40 Babwira Haruuni ntya: ‹Orhujirire emaana z'okulambagira embere zeerhu, kwenge rhurhamenyere ebyabereere oyo Muusa warhukuulaga omu gihugo ch'eMiisiri.›
ACT 7:41 Mw'ezoola siku, bachijirira egishushanyo ch'ekimasha. Barhuulira cho entuulo y'ogusireeza, banajirira edinye echintu enfune zaabo zajiraga.
ACT 7:42 Nnamahanga aja arhenga ahagarhi kaabo, anabaleka baharamye ezuuba, omwezi n'enyenyeezi nk'oku biyandikirwe ntya omu gitaabu ch'abaleebi: ‹Ego bantu b'eIsraheeli, ka nyoono nye mwarhuuliraga ebirhungano n'ezindi ntuulo z'ogusirezwa omu myaaka makumi mane omu mpinga?
ACT 7:43 Nangwa, aliko mwaliheekere ehema ly'emaana yenyu eyirikwa Moloki n'enyenyeezi y'emaana yenyu eyirikwa Refaani, ebyoola bishushanyo mwajiraga yi mubiharamya! Elugulu w'ebyoola nabarhuma buja gurhaluka eBabilooni.›
ACT 7:44 «Bashookuluza beerhu bali bagwerhe omu mpinga ehema ly'obuhamiriza. Bakwizaga elyoola hema nk'oku Nnamahanga arhegekaga Muusa gukulikirana n'eshusho abonaga.
ACT 7:45 Enyuma z'okuyankiirira elyo hema, bashookuluza beerhu haguma na Yoshuwa baliheeka omu gihugo barhoolaga eyi Nnamahanga amalibisya embaga zaacho embere zaabo. Lyabeera mw'echo gihugo kugera amango ma Daawudi.
ACT 7:46 Daawudi ayemeerwa na Nnamahanga, ava amuhema ntya: ‹Nnamahanga wa Yakobo, onyemeerere nkuyumbakire eNju.›
ACT 7:47 Aliko Solomoono ye wamuyumbakiire eNju.
ACT 7:48 Chiro akaba ntyo, Nnamahanga w'Elugulu Bweneene arhalama omu bintu byajirirwe n'efune z'abantu, nk'oku omuleebi aderhere:
ACT 7:49 ‹Nnaweerhu aderhere ntya: “Empingu yo ntebe yaani, n'egulu yo ndabarhiro yaani. Nju nchi nji mwanyumbakira, hayi nji haaba hantu haani h'oguhumuukira?
ACT 7:50 K'arhali fune yaani yajiraga ebyoola byooshi?”›
ACT 7:51 «Ego mwe bantu bazibu! Emirhima yenyu n'amarhwi menyu biri by'abantu barhayemereere Nnamahanga, muli kuguma na bashookuluza benyu. Ngasi mango munalahira kuyunva omulenge gwa Muuka-Mutagatiifu.
ACT 7:52 Nde omu baleebi orhalibuzwaga na bashookuluza benyu? Bayirhaga balaala babalaga embere okuyinja kw'Okwaneene. Y'olaala mwabo nji mwalenganyaga, mwanamuyirha.
ACT 7:53 Mwewe, mwe mwayankiriraga Erhegekobamalahika babalaga, aliko murhalikulikiraga!»
ACT 7:54 Abantu b'akabuga k'aBayaahudi bayunvire ebyoola binwa byooshi bakaliha bweneene, banarhondera kumugugurhira amenyo.
ACT 7:55 Aliko Sitefaano alola empingu eyi ayunjwire Muuka-Mutagatiifu, abona obukuuze bwa Nnamahanga na Yeesu eyi ayimangire ekulyo kwa Nnamahanga.
ACT 7:56 Aderha ntya: «Mbwene empingu zichinguukire na Mwene oMuntu ayimangire ekulyo kwa Nnamahanga!»
ACT 7:57 Baaja bayaama bweneene eyi bafukire amarhwi maabo. Booshi haguma bamubalalira ko.
ACT 7:58 Bamukuula omu gishagala, banamubanda amabaale. Abantu bamusidaakaga babikiisa omuzaana wayirikwaga Saawulo emyambalo yaabo.
ACT 7:59 Babeere bali bamubanda amabaale, Sitefaano asaliira ntya: «Nnaweerhu Yeesu, yankirira omuuka gwani!»
ACT 7:60 Afukama, n'okuva ayaama ntya n'omulenge munene: «Nnaweerhu, orhabahaniraga echiila chaaha!» Ayuusize kuderha ebyoola binwa, afa.
ACT 8:1 Saawulo aliyemereere olufu lwa Sitefaano. Oloola lusiku, echigusho ch'abemeezi ch'eYerusaleema charhondera kulibuzwa bweneene. Booshi, kuleka entumwa, bayandaala omu gihugo ch'eYudeeya n'omu ch'eSamariya.
ACT 8:2 Aliko abantu bakengaga Nnamahanga bahamba Sitefaano, banamulakira bweneene.
ACT 8:3 Saawulo yeewe, aliiri kulibuza echigusho ch'abemeezi. Aliiri kuja omu maju, anakuula mw'abalume n'abakazi, anabaheeka omu munyororo.
ACT 8:4 Aliko emunda balaala bashandaalaga baliiri balenga, baliiri babala oMwazi Mwinja.
ACT 8:5 Firipo ayandagalira omu gishagala chinene ch'egihugo ch'eSamariya, arhondera kubalira abantu elugulu wa Krisitu.
ACT 8:6 Abantu banene baliiri bayunviriza bwinjabwinja haguma enyigirizo za Firipo, n'okubona ebimenyeeso aliiri ajira.
ACT 8:7 Abazimu baliiri barhenga omu bantu banene eyi bali bayaama bweneene. Bantu banene bahunzize n'ebirema baafuma.
ACT 8:8 Habonekana obushagaluke bunene mw'echoola gishagala.
ACT 8:9 Muntu muguma oyirikwa Simooni abaaga arhuula mw'echoola gishagala. Aliiri ajirira m'obukurungu n'ogusoomeza aBasamariya. Aliiri guchiihala oku ye ntabalalwa.
ACT 8:10 Booshi, gurhengera oku mudoorho guhika oku mukulu, baliiri bamuyunviriza n'okuderha ntya: «Oyoola muntu ali buhashe bwa Nnamahanga, bulaala buderhwa ‹Buhashe Bunene.›»
ACT 8:11 Baliiri bamuyunviriza, bulaala haliiri hamaagera esiku zinene ey'abasomeeze n'obukurungu bwage.
ACT 8:12 Babeere bayemeera Firipo waliiri abalira bo oMwazi Mwinja gw'obwime bwa Nnamahanga n'eziino lya Yeesu Krisitu, abalume n'abakazi babatiizwa.
ACT 8:13 Simooni naye yenyine ayemeera Yeesu, anabatiizwa. Arhagirhengaga ku Firipo, anasoomererwa ebimenyeeso n'ebijiro by'obuhashe binene byaliiri byajirika.
ACT 8:14 Entumwa zaliiri eYerusaleema zabeere zayunva okw'abantu b'eSamariya bayankiriire eChinwa cha Nnamahanga, zabarhumira Petero na Yohaana.
ACT 8:15 Bombi babeere baagera eSamariya, basaliirira abemeezi yi bayankirira Muuka-Mutagatiifu,
ACT 8:16 kwenge abaga arhaza yandagalira chiro oku muguma wabo. Babaaga babatiizizwe konyine oku ziino lya Nnaweerhu Yeesu.
ACT 8:17 Petero na Yohaana baaja babalambuulira kw'amaboko, banayankirira Muuka-Mutagatiifu.
ACT 8:18 Egihe Simooni abonaga oku bayankiriire Muuka-Mutagatiifu kugerera eNtumwa omu kubalambuulira kw'amaboko, abaheekera efuranga, anababwira ntya:
ACT 8:19 «Mumpaage naani obuula buhashe yi ngasi muntu naani nalambuulira kw'amaboko ayankirire Muuka-Mutagatiifu.»
ACT 8:20 Aliko Petero amubwira ntya: «Efuranga zaawe zihere haguma naawe, bulaala waliganiizize kugula empaano ya Nnamahanga kugerera efuranga!
ACT 8:21 Orhagwerhe chigabi chiro n'egityu mw'aka kaasi, kwenge omurhima gwawe gurhakwaneene embere za Nnamahanga.
ACT 8:22 Jaaga waleka ebyaaha byaawe by'oguchifiija, onasaliire Nnaweerhu yi nkabaga ababalire enganiiza y'omurhima gwawe.
ACT 8:23 Kwenge mbwene oku oyunjwire obongwa nka kalulwe k'endulwe, onashwekerwe n'ebyaaha.»
ACT 8:24 Simooni ashubiza ntya: «Mwenyine munsaliirire Nnaweerhu, yi ntaacho chimbeerage omu bi mwaderhere.»
ACT 8:25 Petero na Yohaana bamalire guhaana obuhamiriza bwabo n'okuyigiriza eChinwa cha Nnaweerhu, bagaluka eYerusaleema. Bagenda bali baabala oMwazi Mwinja omu bishagala binene by'aBasamariya.
ACT 8:26 Malahika wa Nnaweerhu abwira Firipo ntya: «Yimanga, onagende omu njira ejiire egarhongo, elaala erhengeere eYerusaleema guhika eGaza.» Eyoola njira egerere omu mpinga.
ACT 8:27 Ava ayimanga, agenda. Na mw'eyoola njira, mwaliiri oMunyaetiyopiya muguma w'entazi. Aliiri mukozi mukulu wa Kandake mwamikazi w'Etiyopiya, na murhegesi w'ebikulo byaage byooshi. Alijiire eYerusaleema guharamya Nnamahanga.
ACT 8:28 Abeere ali arhenga yo ey'ayikeere omu mudugaari gwage, eyi anali asoma n'omulenge munene egitaabu ch'omuleebi Isaya.
ACT 8:29 Muuka-Mutagatiifu abwira Firipo ntya: «Gendeerera, oshimaane guliira mudugaari.»
ACT 8:30 Firipo alibirhira go, ayunva oMunyaetiyopiya ali asoma egitaabu ch'omuleebi Isaya. Firipo amubaza ntya: «K'oyunviirhe eby'oli wasoma?»
ACT 8:31 Ashubiza ntya: «Gurhe nakabiyunva, akonva ntaaye oli ampuguulira?» Ava ayinginga Firipo ashone, ayikale haguma naye omu mudugaari.
ACT 8:32 aMandiko Matagatiifu aliiri asoma maderhere ntya: «Aliheekerwe nka ntaama baaja kubaaga. Nka mwanabuzi osirire embere z'oli wamucha amooya, arhabumbuulaga obuunu bwage.
ACT 8:33 Omu guchirhonda kwage, barhamuchiiraga bwinja olushinja lwage. Nde nji waabala emyaazi y'egisisi chaage? Kwenge bakuulire akalamo kaage omu gulu.»
ACT 8:34 Oyoola Munyaetiyopiya abaza Firipo ntya: «Nkuyingingire, ombwire nde y'omuleebi aderhere ko ebyoola? Ali achiiderha oku byo changwa oku windi?»
ACT 8:35 Firipo aja arhonderera oku malaala Mandiko Matagatiifu oMunyaetiyopiya aliiri asoma, amubalira oMwazi Mwinja gwa Yeesu.
ACT 8:36 Babeere bachiri bagenda, baagera aha amenji mali. Oyoola Munyaetiyopiya abaza ntya: «Tala amenji! Bichi bimbuzize kubatiizwa?»
ACT 8:37 [Firipo amushubiza ntya: «Akonva oyemeerere Yeesu n'omurhima gwawe gooshi, wakabatiizwa.» Naye aderha ntya: «Neechi! Nayemereere oku Yeesu Krisitu ali Mwene Nnamahanga.»]
ACT 8:38 Oyoola Munyaetiyopiya ava ayimanza omudugaari. Bombi bayandagalira omu menji, Firipo n'olaala Munyaetiyopiya. Firipo ava amubatiiza.
ACT 8:39 Babeere barhenga omu menji, oMuuka gwa Nnaweerhu gwaheeka Firipo. Oyoola Munyaetiyopiya arhachimubonaga, aliko agendeerera olugenzi, eyi ashagalukire.
ACT 8:40 Firipo yeewe, ahengeera akola ali omu gishagala che Azoto. Alema abala yo oMwazi Mwinja omu bishagala byooshi aliiri agera mo, guhika okugera kwage omu gishagala ch'eKayizariya.
ACT 9:1 Mw'ezoola siku, Saawulo alichiri aderha okw'ayirha abemeezi ba Nnaweerhu. Aja emw'omudaahwa mukulu,
ACT 9:2 anamuhema amaruba m'okuja omu masinagoogi m'omu gishagala ch'eDamasiki, y'akabugaana yo abalume changwa abakazi bakulikiire eNjira ya Nnaweerhu, abashweke, anabaleerhe eYerusaleema.
ACT 9:3 Abeere ali omu njira hoofu ahike eDamasiki, ho n'aho, obumoleke bwarhenga empingu bwamugorha.
ACT 9:4 Ahenera ahashi, anava ayunva omulenge gwamubaza ntya: «Saawulo, Saawulo, girhumire wandibuza?»
ACT 9:5 Ashubiza ntya: «Nnaweerhu, wooyo oli nde?» Omulenge gwashubiza ntya: «Nyoono, ndi Yeesu, oli walibuza.
ACT 9:6 Aliko oyimange, oje omu gishagala. Omoola, bakubwira ech'okwaneene kujira.»
ACT 9:7 Abantu baliiri babalama haguma na Saawulo bayimanga buzira kuderha elugulu w'ogusoomerwa. Baliiri bayunva omulenge, aliko ntaaye baliiri baabona.
ACT 9:8 Saawulo ayimanga, azibuula ameesho, aliko ntaacho aliiri abona. Baava bamufarhira oku kuboko, bamuheeka eDamasiki.
ACT 9:9 Ajira siku esharhu buzira kubona, na buzira kulya changwa kunywa.
ACT 9:10 eDamasiki yaliiri omwemeezi oyirikwa Hananiya. Nnaweerhu amubonekera, amuhamagala: «Hananiya!» Naye ashubiza ntya: «Nyoono oyu, Nnaweerhu!»
ACT 9:11 Nnaweerhu amubwira ntya: «Yimanga, ogende omu njira eyirikwa ‹Elambuukire›, obaze omu nju ya Yuuda omuntu oyirikwa Saawulo w'eTariso. Ali asaliira mu kino gihe.
ACT 9:12 Omu kubonekerwa, abwene omuntu oyirikwa Hananiya aja omu nju, amanamulambuulira kw'amaboko y'ashube kubona.»
ACT 9:13 Hananiya ashubiza ntya: «Nnaweerhu, nayunvire bantu banene baderha obubi booshi oyoola muntu ajiriire abemeezi baawe eYerusaleema.
ACT 9:14 Chiro na hanoola, abakulu b'abadaahwa bamuheere obuhashe bw'ogushweka abantu booshi basaliira oku ziino lyaawe.»
ACT 9:15 Aliko Nnaweerhu abwira Hananiya ntya: «Genda, kwenge oyoola mulume ali gikoleeso nachishogere ch'okubala eziino lyaani embere z'abarhali Bayaahudi n'abaami baabo, n'embere z'aBaisraheeli.
ACT 9:16 Namuyeereka nyoono nyenyine amalibuko mooshi akwaneene kulibuka elugulu waani.»
ACT 9:17 Hananiya aja agenda. Abeere agera omu nju, alambuulira Saawulo kw'amaboko, anamubwira ntya: «Saawulo, mwene weerhu, Nnaweerhu Yeesu wakubonekeraga omu njira embere oyinje hano, antumire y'oshube kubona, onayunjule Muuka-Mutagatiifu.»
ACT 9:18 Ho n'aho, ameesho maage maarhoga kw'ebiri nk'amagamba, anashuba kubona. Ayimanga, anabatiizwa.
ACT 9:19 Aja alya ebiryo, anashuba kugwarha emisi. Saawulo abeera siku zigeeke haguma n'abemeezi baliiri eDamasiki.
ACT 9:20 Ava arhondera kubala omu masinagoogi oku Yeesu ali Mwene Nnamahanga.
ACT 9:21 Booshi baliiri bamuyunva, basoomerwa; banalema babazana ntya: «K'arhali oyuula ye waliiri alibuza bweneene abasaliira eYerusaleema oku ziino lya Yeesu? K'arhanayinjaga hanoola kubashweka n'okubaheeka embere z'abakulu b'abadaahwa?»
ACT 9:22 Aliko obuhashe bwa Saawulo bwaliiri bwayuushuka omu gusoomeza aBayaahudi balilamire eDamasiki, omu kuyeereka bwinjabwinja oku Yeesu ye Krisitu.
ACT 9:23 Enyuma w'esiku zinene, aBayaahudi bahiga kuyirha Saawulo.
ACT 9:24 Aliko naye amenya ogo muhigo. Baliiri balanga emilyango y'egishagala ezuuba n'obudufu yi bamuyirhe.
ACT 9:25 Aliko obudufu, abigirizwa ba Saawulo bamurhoola, banamuyandagaza omu garhanda embuga w'olugurhu lw'egishagala.
ACT 9:26 Saawulo agenda eYerusaleema. Abeere ahika yo, ashonda gurhe agachigusha haguma n'abemeezi, aliko booshi baliiri bamuyuubahire, kwenge barhaliyemereere oku abeere mwemeezi.
ACT 9:27 Baranaaba aja amurhoola, amuheekera eNtumwa. Abashambaalira gurhe Saawulo alibwene Nnaweerhu omu njira na gurhe Nnaweerhu ashambaalaga naye. Ashuba kubashambaalira gurhe Saawulo ayigirizaga buzira buuba eDamasiki oku ziino lya Yeesu.
ACT 9:28 Gurhengera echoola gihe, Saawulo alema alama haguma n'eNtumwa, alambagira haguma nabo omu Yerusaleema, analiiri ayigiriza buzira buuba oku ziino lya Nnaweerhu.
ACT 9:29 Aliiri ashambaala n'oguhatana n'aBayaahudi b'olulimi lw'eKigiriki. Aliko aboola bantu baliiri bashonda kumuyirha.
ACT 9:30 Abaabo babeere bamenya ogoola mwazi, baheeka Saawulo omu gishagala ch'eKayizariya, banamurhuma omu gishagala ch'eTariso.
ACT 9:31 Mw'echoola gihe, echigusho ch'abemeezi chaliiri omu murhuula omu Yudeeya yooshi, eGalilaaya n'eSamariya. Chaliiri chagwarha emisi, chalama omu kuyuubaha Nnaweerhu, n'okuyuushuka kugerera oburhabaale bwa Muuka-Mutagatiifu.
ACT 9:32 Petero abeere ali agera ngasi hantu, ayandagalira emwa abemeezi baliiri balamire omu gishagala ch'eLuuda.
ACT 9:33 Abugaana y'omuntu oyirikwa Ayineya walihunzize. Alilyaamire oku gishanja gurhenga myaaka munaane.
ACT 9:34 Petero ava amubwira ntya: «Ayineya, Yeesu Krisitu amagufumya. Yimanga onazinge egishanja chaawe!» Ho n'aho ayimanga.
ACT 9:35 Abantu booshi b'eLuuda na b'omu bulambo bw'eSaroni babeere baabona Ayineya, bayemeera Nnaweerhu.
ACT 9:36 Omu gishagala ch'eYopa mwaliiri omukazi muguma mwemeezi wayirikwaga Tabita. Omu lulimi lw'eKigiriki ye Dorika. Agendaga ajira ebijiro binene binja n'ebyo bubabale.
ACT 9:37 Mw'ezoola siku, alwala, anava afa. Bamuyooza, bamuheeka omu gorofa ebusiika.
ACT 9:38 Abemeezi babeere bayunva oku Petero ali eLuuda, hoofu n'eYopa, baarhuma balume babiri kumuyinginga ntya: «Rhuguhemere, yinja emwerhu buzira kulegama.»
ACT 9:39 Petero ayimanga, anava agenda haguma nabo. Bagerere yo, bamuheeka omu gorofa ebusiika. Abashumbakazi booshi baliiri ahoola bayegeera Petero eyi bali baalira. Baliiri bamuyeereka amalopo n'eyindi myambalo Dorika abahangiraga egihe aliiri mugumaguma.
ACT 9:40 Petero ahulusa abantu booshi, aja afukama, asaliira. Enyuma ahindamukira emunda omubiri gwaliiri, aderha ntya: «Tabita, yimanga!» Tabita aja azibuula ameesho. Abwene Petero, ayikala.
ACT 9:41 Petero amufarhira oku kuboko, amurhabaala kuyimanga. Aja ahamagala abashumbakazi n'abandi bemeezi, anabamoleka ye, eyi ali mugumaguma.
ACT 9:42 Eyoola myaazi yamenyeekana omu gishagala chooshi ch'eYopa n'abantu banene bayemeera Nnaweerhu.
ACT 9:43 Petero abeera eYopa siku zinene emw'omulume oyirikwa Simooni waliiri muhanga omu gukwiza empu.
ACT 10:1 Omu gishagala ch'eKayizariya haliiri muntu muguma wayirikwaga Korineliyo. Aliiri mukulu w'echigusho ch'abasoda chayirikwaga «Chigusho ch'aBaitaliyana.»
ACT 10:2 Yeewe n'abantu booshi b'omu mwage, bakengaga Nnamahanga n'okumuyuubaha. Agendaga arhabaala abakene bweneene, anazigaanaga gusaliira Nnamahanga ngasi mango.
ACT 10:3 Hoofu n'esaa mwenda z'ezuuba, abonekerwa, abona malahika wa Nnamahanga aja omu mwage n'okumuhamagala ntya: «Ego Korineliyo!»
ACT 10:4 Abeere amuloleereza, ayuubaha, anamubaza ntya: «Nnaweerhu, bichi byabeere?» Malahika amushubiza ntya: «Nnamahanga ayunviirhe amasaala maawe n'oburhabaale bwawe oku bakene anabuyibukire.
ACT 10:5 Ojaage warhuma abantu eYopa baleerhe Simooni washembulwaga Petero.
ACT 10:6 Ahandire emw'owundi Simooni w'omulenga omu gukwiza empu, n'enju yaage eri eburhambi bw'enyanja.»
ACT 10:7 Malahika wamuganiizaga abeere agenda, Korineliyo ahamagala abakozi baage babiri b'akaasi k'omu nju, n'omusoda muguma omu balaala balemaga bamulanga, okenga Nnamahanga.
ACT 10:8 Amalire kubalira bo byooshi byabeere, abarhuma eYopa.
ACT 10:9 Olusiku lwakulikiraga, aboola bantu basharhu babeere bachiri omu njira banakola bali bayegeera egishagala, Petero azamuukira elugulu oku nju gusaliira ey'emidi eri hoofu.
ACT 10:10 Ayunva enzara, anagifiija kulya. Babeere bali bamuvuyira ebiryo, abonekerwa.
ACT 10:11 Abona empingu echingwirwe n'echintu gishushire n'omwenda munene gifarhiriirwe oku bishimbiri bine chiri charhenga omu chanya n'okuyandagazwa oku daho.
ACT 10:12 Kw'echoola chintu kwaliiri ngasi buuko bw'enyama z'amagulu mane, enyama zibululuka oku daho, n'enyunyi zibalala omu chaalege.
ACT 10:13 Omulenge muguma gwava gwamubwira ntya: «Petero, yimanga, baaga onalye.»
ACT 10:14 Petero ashubiza ntya: «Nangwa Nnaweerhu! Ntashubiraga kulya echintu girhakwaneene kuliibwa, girhanacheesezwe!»
ACT 10:15 Obwakabiri omulenge gwamubwira ntya: «Echi Nnamahanga acheeseze, wooyo orhagirhoolaga oku girhakwaneene kuliibwa!»
ACT 10:16 Ebyoola byaaba gasharhu, n'enyuma echoola chintu chaava chazamuulirwa empingu.
ACT 10:17 Petero abeere achiri achibaza bichi okola kubonekerwa abonaga kuderhere, abantu Korineliyo arhumaga baaja baahika oku mulyango g'okuja omu nju. Babaaga babaziriize embere bamenye enju ya Simooni.
ACT 10:18 Balegereza, banabaza akonva ahoola ha Simooni washembulwaga Petero ahandire.
ACT 10:19 Petero abeere ali aganiiza kw'okola kubonekerwa, Muuka-Mutagatiifu amubwira ntya: «Haliira hali balume basharhu bali bagushonda.
ACT 10:20 Yandagala, onagende haguma nabo buzira kuganganwa, kwenge nyoono nye nabarhumaga.»
ACT 10:21 Petero ava ayandagala n'okubwira aboola balume ntya: «Nyoono nye muli mwashonda. Bichi birhumire muli hanoola?»
ACT 10:22 Baashubiza ntya: «Omukulu w'abasoda oyirikwa Korineliyo ye rhurhumire. Ali muntu okwaneene, oyuubaha Nnamahanga, n'aBayaahudi booshi bamuhamiiriza bwinja. Malahika Mutagatiifu amurhegekere oku rhukuleerhe emwage akuyunvirize.»
ACT 10:23 Petero aja abayankirira omu nju, anabaha aha balaala. Bwacheere eseezi, Petero azuuka, anagenda haguma nabo. Abemeezi baguma b'eYopa bamuherekeza.
ACT 10:24 Olusiku lwakulikiraga, baagera eKayizariya. Korineliyo aliiri abalinga eyi analaalikire emwage abantu b'omulala gwage, n'abeera baage b'oku murhima.
ACT 10:25 Petero abeere ahika emwa Korineliyo, Korineliyo aja kumuyankirira, afukama, anayuunama embere zaage omu kumukuuza.
ACT 10:26 Aliko Petero amuyimanza, anamubwira ntya: «Yimanga, kwenge naani ndi muntu kuguma naawe.»
ACT 10:27 Petero aja omu nju haguma naye eyi bali baganiira, anabugaana mo abantu banene bachigushire.
ACT 10:28 Ababwira ntya: «Muyinji mwenyine okw'oMuyaahudi alahiizwe kugwarha obwira n'orhali Muyaahudi changwa okuja omu mwage. Aliko Nnamahanga anyerekere oku birhahemere ogurhoola omuntu nk'orhacheere changwa nk'arhakwaneene kuyegeerwa.
ACT 10:29 Cho girhumire, egihe mwantumiraga abantu kunshonda, namayinja buzira kuganganwa. Mbahemere muje mwambwira bichi byarhumaga mwampamagala.»
ACT 10:30 Korineliyo ashubiza ntya: «Hamaagera bunoola siku esharhu, naliiri nasaliira omu mwani, oku gihe nka kinoola ch'esaa mwenda. Ho n'aho omuntu oyambeere emyambalo eri yabaraganya ayimanga embere zaani.
ACT 10:31 Aderha ntya: ‹Korineliyo, Nnamahanga ayunviirhe amasaala maawe, anayibukire oburhabaale bwawe oku bakene.
ACT 10:32 Jaaga warhuma abantu eYopa, baje guhamagala Simooni washembulwaga Petero. Ahandire ahaburhambi bw'enyanja, omu nju ya Simooni muhanga w'ogukwiza empu.›
ACT 10:33 Ho n'aho nava nagurhumira abantu kugushonda, naawe wajirire bwinja okuyinja. Leero rhweshi rhuli hanoola mw'eno saa embere za Nnamahanga yi rhuyunva byooshi Nnaweerhu agurhegekere gurhubwira.»
ACT 10:34 Petero aj'aderha ntya: «Okuli bunoola namaamenya oku Nnamahanga arhajira kalondoole.
ACT 10:35 Aliko omu ngasi lubaga, ngasi yeeshi omuyuubaha n'okujira ebikwaneene, Nnamahanga anamuyankirira.
ACT 10:36 Arhumaga echinwa oku Baisraheeli omu kubabalira oMwazi Mwinja gw'omurhuula kugerera Yeesu Krisitu. Yeewe ye Nnaweerhu w'abantu booshi.
ACT 10:37 Mwewe, muyinji echizinda kuba omu Yudeeya yooshi gurhonderera eGalilaaya, enyuma za Yohaana kubala okw'abantu babatiizwe.
ACT 10:38 Muyinji gurhe Nnamahanga agishogaga Yeesu w'eNazareeti gukola akaasi kaage, anamuha Muuka-Mutagatiifu n'obuhashe. Hooshi aliiri agera, aliiri ajira amenja n'ogufumya abantu booshi baliiri omu buja bwa Shetaani. Kwenge Nnamahanga aliiri haguma naye.
ACT 10:39 Rhuli bahamiiriza ba byooshi ajiraga omu gihugo ch'aBayaahudi n'eYerusaleema. Olaala bayirhaga omu kumubamba oku musalaaba,
ACT 10:40 aliko Nnamahanga amufuulire olusiku lwa gasharhu. Amuyeerekana oku bantu,
ACT 10:41 arhali oku lubaga looshi, aliko oku bahamiiriza Nnamahanga abaaga agishogere, oku rhwewe rhwe rhwalyaaga, rhwananywa haguma naye enyuma w'ogufuuka kwage omu bafu.
ACT 10:42 Arhurhegekere okubalira olubaga n'okuyeerekena oku yeewe ye Nnamahanga ajirire muzuuzi w'abazeene n'abafiire.
ACT 10:43 Abaleebi booshi bamuha obuula buhamiiriza: ngasi yeeshi omuyemeera, ebyaaha byaage binababalirwa kugerera eziino lyaage.»
ACT 10:44 Petero abeere achiri aderha ebyo binwa, Muuka-Mutagatiifu ayandagalira oku booshi baliiri babiyunviriza.
ACT 10:45 Abemeezi booshi b'aBayaahudi bayinjaga haguma na Petero basoomerwa okubona abarhali Bayaahudi nabo bayandaazwa kw'empaano ya Muuka-Mutagatiifu.
ACT 10:46 Kwenge baliiri babayunva baderha omu ndimi n'ogukuuza Nnamahanga. Petero aja aderha ntya:
ACT 10:47 «Abaala bantu bayankirire Muuka-Mutagatiifu kuguma neerhu. Ka hali omuntu wakabalahirira kubatiizibwa omu menji?»
ACT 10:48 Ava arhegeka oku babatiizwe oku ziino lya Yeesu Krisitu. Baaja bahema Petero abeere haguma nabo siku zigeeke.
ACT 11:1 Entumwa n'abemeezi baliiri eYudeeya bayunva okw'abarhali Bayaahudi nabo bayankiriire eChinwa cha Nnamahanga.
ACT 11:2 Amango Petero azamuukiraga eYerusaleema, abemeezi b'aBayaahudi bamurhonganya,
ACT 11:3 bamubwira ntya: «Ego muza we! Gurhe wajiire omu nju z'abarhali Bayaahudi wamanalya nabo!»
ACT 11:4 Petero aja arhondera kubalira bo byooshi gurhe byalibeere. Ababwira ntya mwazi oku gwindi:
ACT 11:5 «Nyoono naliiri omu gishagala ch'eYopa. Oku ndi nasaliira, nabonekerwa: chintu chiguma chiri nka mwenda munene gifarhirwe hantu hane, chachima gurhengera omu chaalege, chayandagazwa emunda ndi.
ACT 11:6 Nabeere nasuuzuma cho, nabona chiri mo enyama z'amagulu mane, enyama z'elubala, ezibululuka n'enyunyi zibalala omu chaalege.
ACT 11:7 Nayunva omulenge gwambwira ntya: ‹Yimanga Petero, baaga, onalye.›
ACT 11:8 Aliko nashubiza ntya: ‹Nangwa Nnaweerhu! Echintu girhacheesezwe girhanakwaneene kuliibwa girhashubiraga kuja omu buunu bwani!›
ACT 11:9 Oku bwakabiri, omulenge gwashubiza ntya gurhengera empingu: ‹Echi Nnamahanga acheeseze, wooyo orhagirhoolaga oku girhakwaneene kuliibwa!›
ACT 11:10 Ebyoola byabeere byamajirika gasharhu, byooshi byaava byazamuulwa omu mpingu.
ACT 11:11 Ho n'aho, bantu basharhu balintumiirwe gurhengera eKayizariya baahika omu nju rhwaliiri mo.
ACT 11:12 Muuka-Mutagatiifu ambwira mpu ngende nabo buzira kuganganwa. Aba beerhu ndarhu mubwene, bali mperekeeze, rhwanaja omu nju y'omuntu oyirikwa Korineliyo.
ACT 11:13 Oyoola Korineliyo arhubalira gurhe alibwene malahika ayimanga omu nju yaage n'okumubwira ntya: ‹Rhuma abantu eYopa baje gushonda Simooni washembulwaga Petero.
ACT 11:14 Yeewe ye wakubwira ebinwa byakuleerhera obuchunguke, wooyo n'abantu b'omu nju yaawe booshi.›
ACT 11:15 Nabeere narhondera kuderha, Muuka-Mutagatiifu ayandagalira oku bo nk'oku arhuyandagaliraga ko neerhu oku murhondero.
ACT 11:16 Nava nayibuka echiila chinwa Nnaweerhu aderhaga ntya: ‹Yohaana abatiizaga omu menji, aliko mwabo nji mwabatiizwa na Muuka-Mutagatiifu.›
ACT 11:17 Akaba leero Nnamahanga abaheere empaano nguma n'elaala arhuhaaga neerhu amango rhwayemeeraga Nnaweerhu Yeesu-Krisitu, naliiri nde, nyoono, mpu ngale kulwisa Nnamahanga?»
ACT 11:18 Abemeezi b'aBayaahudi bamalire kuyunva ebyoola, barhuleera, banakuuza Nnamahanga n'oku derha ntya: «Gasi Nnamahanga aheere abarhali Bayaahudi nabo enjira y'okuleka ebyaaha byaabo yi baabona akalamo k'esiku n'amango!»
ACT 11:19 Balaala bemeezi bashandaazwaga elugulu w'okuyirhwa kwa Sitefaano, baguma omu bo bagenda guhika omu gihugo ch'eFoyinikiya. Abandi baaja oku chizimba ch'eGipuro, n'abandi baahika omu gishagala ch'eAntiyokiya. Ntaaye bayigiriize eChinwa cha Nnamahanga arhali aBayaahudi bonyine.
ACT 11:20 Aliko ahagarhi kaabo haaba bantu baguma b'eGipuro na ab'omu gishagala ch'eKureene bayinjaga eAntiyokiya, nabo baganiira n'abarhali Bayaahudi n'okubalira bo oMwazi Mwinja gwa Nnaweerhu Yeesu.
ACT 11:21 Obuhashe bwa Nnaweerhu bwaliiri haguma nabo, n'abantu banene bahindamukira Nnaweerhu, baanaba bemeezi.
ACT 11:22 Echigusho ch'abemeezi b'eYerusaleema babeere bayunva ogo mwazi, baarhuma Baranaaba agende eAntiyokiya.
ACT 11:23 Abeere ahika yo, agishwa na Nnamahanga, asiima, n'okuyinginga abemeezi bagendekere guseera ku Nnaweerhu omu mirhima yaabo yooshi.
ACT 11:24 Baranaaba aliiri muntu mwinja, oyunjwizwe Muuka-Mutagatiifu n'obwemeezi. Abantu banene bakulikira Nnaweerhu.
ACT 11:25 Buzinda, Baranaaba aja eTariso gushonda Saawulo.
ACT 11:26 Abeere amubona, amuheeka eAntiyokiya. Baranaaba na Saawulo bamala omwaka gooshi eyi bali bachigusha haguma n'echigusho ch'abemeezi. Banayigiriza abantu banene. Mw'echi gishagala ch'eAntiyokiya mw'abemeezi bahamagalwaga «Bakrisitu» oku burhanzi.
ACT 11:27 Mwamo mango, baleebi baguma bachima gurhenga eYerusaleema kuja eAntiyokiya.
ACT 11:28 Muguma omu bo, oyirikwa Hagabo, ayimanga n'ogurhondera kuleeba n'obuhashe bwa Muuka-Mutagatiifu okw'enzara nene yaaba omu gulu lyooshi. Eyo nzara yava yaaba amango mw'omwami mukulu Kuloode w'eRooma.
ACT 11:29 Abemeezi b'eAntiyokiya baava bahiga gurhumira abemeezi bali balamire eYudeeya oburhabaale, ngasi muguma gukulikirana na okw'agalire.
ACT 11:30 Baagusha esholoolo haguma, bayirhumira abashamuka b'echigusho ch'abemeezi b'eYerusaleema kulengera Baranaaba na Saawulo.
ACT 12:1 Mw'amo mango, mwami Heroode arhondera kulibuza bantu baguma b'echigusho ch'abemeezi.
ACT 12:2 Anayirha Yakobo mwene waabo Yohaana n'engoorho.
ACT 12:3 Abeere abona okw'ebyo byasimiisize aBayaahudi, aderha oku bafarhe Petero naye. Ebyoola byajirikaga amango m'edinye y'emigati nzira chachu.
ACT 12:4 Abeere amafarha Petero n'okumuhira omu munyororo, amuhira omu bulanzi bw'ebigusho bine by'abasoda baneebane eyi bali guhinguulirana. Ajira ntyo ey'ali gukengeera okw'amuburaniisa embere w'olubaga enyuma w'ePaasaka.
ACT 12:5 Oku Petero alangirwe omu munyororo, echigusho ch'abemeezi boowe baliiri bakomeza kumusaliirira bweneene emwa Nnamahanga.
ACT 12:6 Obudufu b'olo lusiku Heroode akaburanyize Petero, Petero alilyaamire ahagarhi k'abasoda babiri ey'anashwekerwe n'amalegule mabiri. N'abalanzi baliiri embere z'omulyango eyi bali balanga omunyororo.
ACT 12:7 Ho n'aho malahika wa Nnaweerhu ahulukira n'obumoleke bwayunjula omu busiika b'ogo munyororo. Malahika abanda ku Petero omu mbavu, amuchula n'okumubwira ntya: «Yimanga juba!» Amalegule malishwekere amaboko maage machishwekuula, marhogera ahashi.
ACT 12:8 Malahika ava amubwira ntya: «Yambala omukaba gwawe n'ebiraato byaawe.» Naye ajira ntyo. Kandi, malahika amubwira ntya: «Yambala egorhe lyawe, onankulikire.»
ACT 12:9 Petero ahuluka eyi anamukulikiire, aliko arhamenyaga kw'echijiro cha malahika chiri ch'okuli: alikengereere okw'abonekeerwe.
ACT 12:10 Babeere bamarhaluka echigusho girhanzi ch'abalanzi n'echakabiri, baahika oku mulyango gw'echuuma guyerekeere omu gishagala. Ogo mulyango gwachichinguula gonyine embere zaabo. Nabo bahuluka n'ogukomeza kugenda omu njira. Ho n'aho oyo malahika amuleka.
ACT 12:11 Petero abeere arhegeera okw'ebyabeere biri by'okuli, ava aderha ntya: «Bunoola namaaja naamenya oku Nnaweerhu arhumaga malahika waage, anankuulire omu maboko ma Heroode n'omu mabi mooshi aBayaahudi balilangaliire okw'ankolera.»
ACT 12:12 Petero abeere amenya bwinja ebyabeere, agenda emwa Mariya, nyina wa Yohaana. Oyo Yohaana ye washembulwaga Mariko. Omu mwage mu bantu banene balichigushire n'ogusaliira Nnamahanga.
ACT 12:13 Petero abeere akongoorha oku lunvi lw'embuga, omukozi muguma w'omunyere oyirikwa Rooda ayegeera omulyango kubaza nde oli akongoorha.
ACT 12:14 Arhegeera omulenge gwa Petero, aliko ahaali h'okumuchinguulira, alibirha n'obushaguluke kuja kubwira abaabo oku Petero ali oku mulyango gw'embuga.
ACT 12:15 Nabo bamubwira ntya: «Ego munyere! Wasirehere!» Aliko Rooda agendekera kuderha ntya: «Neechi, yeewe maani!» Boowe baliiri bakomeza kuderha ntya: «Oyoola, ali malahika waage.»
ACT 12:16 Aliko Petero agendekera gukongoorha oku lunvi. Baava bachinguula, banasoomerwa bweneene kumubona.
ACT 12:17 Abasimira n'okuboko mpu basire. Ababalira gurhe Nnaweerhu amukuulire omu munyororo n'okubabwira ntya: «Mubibalire Yakobo na beene beerhu.» Petero ava ahuluka n'okuja ahandi hantu.
ACT 12:18 Bwacheere eseezi, abasoda bagwarha obuuba bunene n'okubazana ntya: «Bichi byahikiire Petero?»
ACT 12:19 Heroode arhuma abantu mpu bamushonde, aliko barhamubonaga. Asambiisa abalanzi, anarhegeka oku bayirhwe. Oku buzinda, Heroode arhenga eYudeeya ayandagalira omu gishagala ch'eKayizariya gurhanga kubeera yo.
ACT 12:20 Amo mango, haliiri obushombanyi ahagarhi ka Heroode n'abantu b'egishagala ch'eTiiro n'abe ch'eSidoona. Aliko, abo bantu bachihira haguma, baaja kumulola. Barhanga kuyunviikana na Balasito waliyimangiire enju ya mwami, baaja bahema omurhuula emwa mwami Heroode. Bulaala ebiryo bagendaga balya omu gihugo chaabo, byabaaga birhenga omu gihugo ch'oyo mwami.
ACT 12:21 Olusiku bayunvikanaga lwabeere lwahika, Heroode ayambala emyambalo y'echaami, ayikala oku ntebe yaage y'obwami ekarubanda, arhondera kuderha embere z'abantu.
ACT 12:22 N'abantu nabo baalema baderha ntya n'omulenge munene: «Gurhali mulenge g'omuntu ogu, sy'aliko guli gw'emaana!»
ACT 12:23 Ho n'aho, malahika wa Nnaweerhu ahaana Heroode, bulaala arhakuuzaga Nnamahanga, sy'achikuuza yenyine. Enzoka z'omu nda zamuluma bweneene, ava afa.
ACT 12:24 Aliko, eChinwa cha Nnamahanga chagendeerera kuja embere n'okuyandaala ahantu hanene.
ACT 12:25 Baranaaba na Saawulo babeere bamaamala akaasi kaabo eYerusaleema, bagaluka eAntiyokiya eyi bali haguma na Yohaana washembulwaga Mariko.
ACT 13:1 Omu chigusho ch'abemeezi b'eAntiyokiya, mwaliiri abaleebi n'abigiriza: Baranaaba, Simeooni oyirikwa Mwiragula, Lukiyo w'eKureene, Manaheni walembwaga haguma na mwami Heroode, na Saawulo.
ACT 13:2 Lusiku luguma, oku bali baharamya Nnaweerhu n'oguchiibuza kulya, Muuka-Mutagatiifu aderha ntya: «Mumpirire eburhambi Baranaaba na Saawulo gukulikirana n'akaasi nabahamagaliire.»
ACT 13:3 Bayuusize guchiibuza kulya, basaliira, babalambuulira kw'amaboko, banabarhuma bagende gukolera Nnamahanga.
ACT 13:4 Muuka-Mutagatiifu abeere arhuma Baranaaba na Saawulo, bayandagalira omu gishagala ch'eSelukiya. Mw'echo gishagala, barhoola echombo, babalamira oku chizimba ch'eGipuro.
ACT 13:5 Babeere baahika omu gishagala ch'eSalami, baabala omwazi gwa Nnamahanga omu masinagoogi m'aBayaahudi. Baliiri haguma na Yohaana oyirikwa Mariko nka murhabaazi waabo.
ACT 13:6 Babeere bamazungula omu chizimba chooshi guhika omu gishagala ch'ePafo, babugaana mo mukurungu muguma w'oMuyaahudi. Oyoola mukurungu aliiri muleebi w'obubeeshi oyirikwa Bara-Yeesu.
ACT 13:7 Aliiri murhabaazi wa Serugiyo Paawulo, munyabwenge na murhegesi w'eGipuro. Oyu murhegesi ahamagala Baranaaba na Saawulo baje emwage bulaala alishondere kuyunva eChinwa cha Nnamahanga.
ACT 13:8 Aliko olaala mukurungu Bara-Yeesu, oyirikwa Elima omu Kigiriki, arhonganya Baranaaba na Saawulo, n'ogushonda kubuza oyo murhegesi arhayemeeraga Yeesu.
ACT 13:9 Aliko Saawulo, oyirikwa kandi Paawulo, eyi ayunjwizwe Muuka-Mutagatiifu, ava amulola n'ameesho makalihire.
ACT 13:10 Amubwira ntya: «Ego mugala wa Shetaani, mwanzi wa byooshi bikwaneene! Wooyo oyunjwire na ngasi buuko b'obulyaalya n'obubeeshi. K'orhaluha kulema walenganya oMwazi g'okuli gwa Nnaweerhu?
ACT 13:11 Leero Nnaweerhu akola aguhana. Waaba mpumi, wanamala siku zilebe buzira kulola obumoleke bw'ezuuba.» Ho n'aho oluhomo n'omwizimya byaaja omu meesho maage. Arhondera kumamaarha omu gushonda omuntu w'okumufarha okuboko y'amuyeereka enjira.
ACT 13:12 Ola murhegesi abeere abona ebyamajirika, asoomererwa enyigirizo za Nnaweerhu, anamuyemeera.
ACT 13:13 Paawulo n'abaliiri nabo baaja omu chombo, barhenga ePafo, baaja omu gishagala ch'ePeriga omu gihugo ch'ePamfiliya. Babeere baagera yo, Yohaana oyirikwa Mariko abaleka, anagaluka eYerusaleema.
ACT 13:14 Aliko boowe, Gurhengera ePeriga bakomeza olugenzi lwabo, banahika omu gishagala ch'eAntiyokiya omu gihugo ch'ePisidiya. Olusiku lw'eSaabato baaja omu sinagoogi, banayikala mo.
ACT 13:15 Enyuma w'ogusomwa kw'ebitaabu by'eRhegeko na eby'abaleebi, abakulu b'esinagoogi babarhumira omuntu ababwire ntya: «Beene beerhu, akonva mugwerhe echinwa ch'ogukomeza abantu omurhima, mujage mwaderha.»
ACT 13:16 Paawulo aja ayumanga, abasimira n'okuboko mpu basire, n'okubabwira ntya: «Munyunvirize, bantu b'eIsraheeli nenyu mwe bandi muyuubaha Nnamahanga!
ACT 13:17 Nnamahanga w'olu lubaga lw'eIsraheeli, agishogere bashookuluza beerhu. Abajira kuba lubaga lunene amango balibungiire omu gihugo ch'eMiisiri. Buzinda abakuula yo omu buhashe bwage bunene.
ACT 13:18 Aliiri kulembera engeso zaabo zibi amango baliiri omu mpinga hoofu myaaka makumi mane.
ACT 13:19 Abeere amahima embaga mushanvu z'egihugo ch'eKanaana, abaheereza echo gihugo kuba gashambala kaabo.
ACT 13:20 Ebyoola byooshi byamala hoofu myaaka magana mane na makumi marhaano. «Buzinda bw'aho, abaha abazuuzi, guhika oku muleebi Samweri.
ACT 13:21 Oku buzinda bahema omwami. Nnamahanga abaha Saawulo, mugala wa Kiisi, w'omu buuko bwa Benjamina, abarhegeke myaaka makumi mane.
ACT 13:22 Nnamahanga abeere amakuula Saawulo oku bwami, ayimika Daawudi. Oyu Daawudi ye Nnamahanga ahamiirizaga ko ntya: ‹Nabwene Daawudi, mugala wa Yeese, ali muntu omurhima gwani gusiimire; nj'ajira byooshi nshondere ajire.›
ACT 13:23 Gurhengera omu mulala gw'oyo Daawudi mu Nnamahanga akuulaga Yeesu kuba Muchunguzi wa Israheeli, gukulikirana n'echilagaane chaage.
ACT 13:24 Embere z'oguhika kwage, Yohaana abwira abantu b'olubaga looshi lw'eIsraheeli baleke ebyaaha, banabatiizwe.
ACT 13:25 Amango Yohaana abeere akola hoofu kuyuusa omulimo gwage, aliiri aderha ntya: ‹Mukengereere oku nyoono ndi nde? Nyoono ntali oyo muli mwalinga! Aliko ayinjire enyuma zaani, eyi nyoono ntakwaneene chiro gushwekuula emigozi y'ebiraato byaage.›
ACT 13:26 «Beene beerhu, bantu b'omu mulala gwa Abrahaamu nenyu mweshi b'ezindi mbaga muyuubaha Nnamahanga, echi Chinwa ch'obuchunguke girhumirwe emwerhu.
ACT 13:27 Kwenge aBanyayerusaleema n'abarhegesi baabo barharhegeeraga Yeesu ali nde. Barhamenyaga ebinwa by'abaleebi bisomwa ngasi lusiku lw'eSaabato. Aliko omu kumuhana baajira nka kulaala aMandiko mali maderhere.
ACT 13:28 Buzira kubona echagarhumire ahanirwa ogufa, bahema Pilaato amuyirhe.
ACT 13:29 Babeere baamala kujira byooshi byaliyandikirwe elugulu waage, bamuyandagaza oku musalaaba, banamuhira omu shinda.
ACT 13:30 Aliko Nnamahanga amufuulire omu bafu.
ACT 13:31 Abonekeene siku zinene oku bantu bazamuukaga naye gurhenga eGalilaaya kuja eYerusaleema, na bunoola, bo bali bahamiiriza baage oku lubaga lw'eIsraheeli.
ACT 13:32 Neerhu, rhubabaliire ogu Mwazi Mwinja, oku echilagaane Nnamahanga ahaaga bashookuluza beerhu,
ACT 13:33 arhujiriire cho rhwe baana baabo, omu gufuula Yeesu. Ogu mwazi guyandikirwe ntya omu chigabi cha kabiri ch'eNanga: ‹Wooyo oli Mugala waani, Nyoono nye nkuburhire zeene.›
ACT 13:34 N'elugulu w'ogufuuka kwa Yeesu, y'arhabola, Nnamahanga aderha ntya: ‹Naguha emigisho ntagatiifu nalaganyaga Daawudi, emigisho y'okuli.›
ACT 13:35 Cho girhumire aderhere ntya omu chindi chigabi ch'aMandiko Matagatiifu: ‹Orhaaleka oMutagatiifu waawe abole.›
ACT 13:36 Daawudi yeewe, abeere amamala gukola gukulikirana n'oku Nnamahanga alirheganyize omu kalamo kaage, afa. Ahambwa ahaburhambi bw'eshinda za b'esheekuluza, anabola.
ACT 13:37 Aliko olaala Nnamahanga afuulaga, yeewe arhabolaga.
ACT 13:38 «Beene beerhu, mukwaneene kumenya oku kugerera yeewe, omwazi g'obubabale bw'ebyaaha gwabalirwe emwenyu. Kugerera oyu Yeesu, ngaasi yeeshi omuyemeerere ababalirwa ebyaaha, aliko murhakababalirwe kugerera amarhegeko ma Muusa.
ACT 13:40 Boboola muchilange y'ebiyandikirwe ntya omu bitaabu by'abaleebi birhabahikira:
ACT 13:41 ‹Mulole, mwe mugwerhe agakeno, musoomerwe munahirime, kwenge nyoono, najira ekijiro omu gihe chenyu, ekijiro murhakayemereere nachiro akaba bakababwirire cho.›»
ACT 13:42 Paawulo na Baranaaba babeere bahuluka omu sinagoogi, abantu babayinginga bashube kuyinja kubabalira eyo myaazi olusiku lw'eSaabato yakulikira.
ACT 13:43 Enyuma z'enshimaanano, aBayaahudi banene n'abandi bantu b'ezindi mbaga bayemeeraga edini ly'ekiyaahudi n'ogukuuza Nnamahanga, bakulikira Paawulo na Baranaaba. Abo bombi baganiira haguma n'abo bantu, banagendekera gukomeza bo, yi barhaleka guseera omu lukogo lwa Nnamahanga.
ACT 13:44 Olusiku lw'eSaabato yakulikiraga, hoofu abantu booshi b'egishagala bachigusha haguma kuyunva eChinwa cha Nnaweerhu.
ACT 13:45 aBayaahudi babeere baabona echo chigusho ch'abantu, bafarhwa n'obongwa bunene. Balahira ebinwa bya Paawulo, banamuhamiiriza obubeeshi.
ACT 13:46 Paawulo na Baranaaba baaja bababwira ntya buzira buuba: «Byaliiri bya bulagiirire mwabo mwe murhangage mubalirwe eChinwa cha Nnamahanga. Aliko oboola yi mwalahira cho, munali mwachiganja nka mwabo murhakwaneene akalamo k'esiku n'amango, rhwabo rhwayerekera emwa b'abarhali Bayaahudi.
ACT 13:47 Kwenge Nnaweerhu arhurhegekere ntya: ‹Nakujirire bumoleke bw'abarhali Bayaahudi, y'oheeka obuchunguke omu gulu lyooshi.›»
ACT 13:48 Abarhali Bayaahudi babeere bayunva eyo myaazi, bamoga. Bakuuza eChinwa cha Nnaweerhu. Na booshi balirheganyizwe akalamo k'esiku n'amango bayemeera Yeesu.
ACT 13:49 Echinwa cha Nnaweerhu chagenda chayandaala omu gihugo chooshi.
ACT 13:50 Aliko aBayaahudi bayoohya abakazi bakengerwe, banasiima guharamya Nnamahanga, haguma n'abashamuka b'egishagala. Barhondera kulibuza Paawulo na Baranaaba, banabalibisya omu gihugo chaabo.
ACT 13:51 Paawulo na Baranaaba babakungurhira k'olujuchu lw'oku magulu maabo, banachijiira omu gishagala ch'eIkoniyo.
ACT 13:52 Aliko abemeezi boowe baliyunjwire obushagaluke n'oMuuka-Mutagatiifu.
ACT 14:1 Babeere bali eIkoniyo, Paawulo na Baranaaba, baja omu sinagoogi y'aBayaahudi nk'oku bazigaanaga. Bayigiriza, oku bulyo aBayaahudi n'aBagiriki banene bahinduka bemeezi.
ACT 14:2 Aliko aBayaahudi barhayemeeraga Krisitu, bayoohya abarhali Bayaahudi mpu bashombe abemeezi.
ACT 14:3 Aliko, Paawulo na Baranaaba bajira siku zinene eIkoniyo. Baliiri bayigiriza elugulu wa Nnaweerhu buzira buuba. Na Nnaweerhu naye aliiri abagaliisa kujira ebimenyeeso n'ebigiriginjo, omu guhamiiriza okw'omwazi gwage g'olukogo guli g'okuli.
ACT 14:4 Omu gishagala che Ikoniyo, abantu bachigaba kabiri. Baguma baaja oku lunda lw'aBayaahudi, n'abandi oku lunda lw'eNtumwa.
ACT 14:5 Aliko, aBayaahudi n'abarhali Bayaahudi haguma n'abarhegesi baabo, baaja kaligi kw'okulibuza n'okuyirha Paawulo na Baranaaba omu kubabanda amabaale.
ACT 14:6 Nabo babeere babimenya, balibirhira omu bishagala by'eLisitira n'eDerebe, by'omu gihugo ch'eLikaoniya; n'omu hantu hatureene byo.
ACT 14:7 Eyoola munda, bagendekera kubala oMwazi Mwinja.
ACT 14:8 Omu gishagala ch'eLisitira, haliiri muntu muguma w'echirema. Arhalambagiraga chiro n'olusiku luguma, bulaala aburhwaga eyi ali chirema ch'amagulu.
ACT 14:9 Lusiku luguma, ey'ayikeere, ayunviriza enyigirizo za Paawulo. Paawulo amulolereza n'okubona okw'agwerhe obwemeezi bwagarhuma afumiiswa.
ACT 14:10 Ava amubwira ntya n'omulenge munene: «Yuumuka, yimangira oku magulu maawe!» Oyo muntu ayimanga ho n'aho, anarhondera kulambagira.
ACT 14:11 Abantu banene balichigushire, babeere baabona ebi Paawulo ajirire, baliika omulenge n'okuderha ntya omu lulimi lw'eKilikaoniya: «Emaana zachihindwire nk'abantu, zanayandagaliire eno mwerhu!»
ACT 14:12 Baliiri bayirika Baranaaba eziino ly'emaana Zeusi, Paawulo naye bamuyirika eziino ly'emaana Herime, kwenge ye waliiri w'okuderha.
ACT 14:13 Omudaahwa w'omu kajumiro k'emaana Zeusi kaliiri embere z'egishagala, aleerha oku milyango y'egishagala empanzi n'emikalaba elukiirwe k'obwaso. Abileerhaga bulaala yeewe haguma n'echo chigusho ch'abantu balishondere gurhuula entuulo.
ACT 14:14 Aliko Baranaaba na Paawulo babeere bayunva ogo mwazi, babera emishangi yaabo omu kuyeerekana oku bagayire, n'okuva balibirha omu bantu eyi bali baderha ntya n'omulenge munene:
ACT 14:15 «Beera baani, gichi girhumire mwajira ntyo? Neerhu, rhuli bantu kuguma nenyu! Akaba yi rhwababalira oMwazi Mwinja, kuli gushonda muleke ebi bintu bya bushaabusha, munahindamukire Nnamahanga olamire. Yeewe ye walemaga echaalege, egulu n'enyanja, na byooshi biri omu byo.
ACT 14:16 Omu siku zageraga, Nnamahaanga alilekere abarhali Bayaahudi booshi bakulikiire enjira zaabo.
ACT 14:17 Nachiro ntyo, arhalekaga guchihamiiriza kugerera ebijiro binja. Abaha mwabo gurhengera omu chaalege envula n'ebihe biyeeza, anabayuugusya ebiryo n'okuyunjuza emirhima yenyu n'obushagaluke bunene.»
ACT 14:18 Nachiro mpu Paawulo na Baranaaba baliderhere ebiila byooshi, birhali biyoolohere kubuza abantu barharhuuliraga bo entuulo.
ACT 14:19 Enyuma w'ebyoola, aBayaahudi baguma baahika gurhengera omu gishagala ch'eAntiyokiya n'eche Ikoniyo. Bayoohya abantu, babanda Paawulo amabaale, banamukululira embuga w'egishagala eyi bakengereere okw'afiire.
ACT 14:20 Aliko abemeezi babeere bamugorha, ayuumuka, agaluka mw'echo gishagala ch'eLisitira. Olusiku lwakulikiraga, aja omu gishagala ch'eDerebe haguma na Baranaaba.
ACT 14:21 Oku bali eDerebe, baalema baabala oMwazi Mwinja, abantu banene bayemeera Yeesu. Buzinda, bagaluka, baaja eLisitira, eIkoniyo n'eAntiyokiya y'ePisidiya.
ACT 14:22 Eyo munda, baliiri bakomeza abemeezi omurhima n'okubahanuula baseere omu bwemeezi. Baliiri bababwira ntya: «Rhukwaneene kugera omu malibuko manene yi rhuja omu Bwami bwa Nnamahanga.»
ACT 14:23 N'omu ngasi chigusho ch'abemeezi, Paawulo na Baranaaba bachishoga mo abashamuka b'okubiyimangira. Babeere bamasaliira n'oguchiibuza kulya, babahira omu maboko ma Nnaweerhu, ye bali bayemereere.
ACT 14:24 Enyuma z'aho, bagerera omu gihugo ch'ePisidiya, banahika omu ch'ePamfiliya.
ACT 14:25 Bamalire kuyigiriza eChinwa cha Nnamahanga oku bantu b'omu gishagala ch'ePeriga, bachimira omu siiko y'eAtaliya.
ACT 14:26 Gurhengera eyoola, basuuka n'echombo kuja eAntiyokiya y'eSuriya. Eyoola yi bahemeraga bo omugisho gwa Nnamahanga kw'aka kaasi bamakola.
ACT 14:27 Babeere baahika, bagusha echigusho ch'abemeezi, banashambaalira bo byooshi Nnamahanga ali ajirire haguma nabo, na gurhe achinguuliraga abarhali Bayaahudi omulyango g'obwemeezi.
ACT 14:28 Paawulo na Baranaaba babeera eyoola siku zinene haguma n'abemeezi.
ACT 15:1 Mw'ezoola siku, bantu baguma bachimira eAntiyokiya gurhengera eYudeeya. Barhondera kuyigiriza abemeezi ntya: «Akaba murhakembwirwe gukulikirana n'emigenzo ya Muusa, murhagachungulwa.»
ACT 15:2 Paawulo na Baranaaba babalahirira, banajira obuhaka bunene haguma nabo elugulu w'oguula mwazi. Abemeezi baahiga oku Paawulo na Baranaaba haguma n'abandi baguma omu bo bazamukire eYerusaleema kuganiira kw'echo chibazo embere z'eNtumwa n'abashamuka b'echigusho ch'abemeezi.
ACT 15:3 Echigusho ch'abemeezi chabaheereza ebintu byooshi by'olugenzi balilagire ko. Baagera omu gihugo ch'eFoyinikiya na ech'eSamariya, baliiri baabala gurhe abarhali Bayaahudi bayemereere kuba bemeezi. Ogu mwazi gwaliiri gwasimiisa bweneene abemeezi booshi.
ACT 15:4 Bahikire eYerusaleema, bayankirirwa n'eNtumwa, n'echigusho ch'abemeezi haguma n'abashamuka baacho. Babala byooshi Nnamahanga ajirire kugerera bo.
ACT 15:5 Aliko, bantu baguma b'omu chigusho ch'aBafarisaayo bahindukaga bemeezi, bayimanga n'okuderha ntya: «Bihemere gukembuula abarhali Bayaahudi n'okubarhegeka ogukenga eRhegeko lya Muusa.»
ACT 15:6 Entumwa n'abashamuka b'echigusho ch'abemeezi bajira enaama elugulu w'echo chibazo.
ACT 15:7 Enyuma z'obuhaka bunene, Petero ayimanga n'okubabwira ntya: «Beene beerhu, muyinji bwinja oku gurhengera miira Nnamahanga andondwere ahagarhi kenyu yi kugerera obuunu bwani, abarhali Bayaahudi bayunve oMwazi Mwinja, banayemeere Yeesu.
ACT 15:8 Na Nnamahanga oyinji emirhima y'abantu, aliyerekeene oku ayemereere abarhali Bayaahudi nabo omu guha bo Muuka-Mutagatiifu kuguma neerhu.
ACT 15:9 Nta kalondoole ajirire ahagarhi keerhu nabo, bulaala acheeseze emirhima yaabo kugerera obwemeezi.
ACT 15:10 Chagarhuma bunoola mwageregeza Nnamahanga omu guheesa abemeezi ogu muzigo, abe bashookuluza beerhu, abe neerhu rhwenyine rhurhagalaga guheeka?
ACT 15:11 Maani neerhu, rhuyinji oku rhwachungwirwe elugulu w'olukogo lwa Nnaweerhu Yeesu, nk'oku nabo bachungwirwe.»
ACT 15:12 Abantu booshi balichigushire baasira. Bayunviriza oku Paawulo na Baranaaba baabala emyaazi elugulu w'ebimenyeeso n'ebigiriginjo byooshi Nnamahanga ajirire kugerera bo ahagarhi k'abarhali Bayaahudi.
ACT 15:13 Babeere baasira, Yakobo naye aderha ntya: «Beene beerhu, munyunvirize!
ACT 15:14 Simooni Petero arhubaliire gurhe Nnamahanga achiyerekeene oku barhali Bayaahudi oku burhanzi y'achishoga baguma omu bo babe bantu baage.
ACT 15:15 Eyi myaazi eri kuguma n'ebinwa by'abaleebi nk'okubiyandikirwe ntya:
ACT 15:16 ‹Buzinda bw'aho, nji naagaluka n'ogushuba kuyumbaka enju ya Daawudi yashandeere. Nji nashuba kuyumbaka ebiguuka byaayo n'okuyiyumanza,
ACT 15:17 y'abandi bantu booshi bashonde Nnaweerhu, neechi, abantu b'embaga zooshi nahamageere babe baani. Ntyo ku Nnaweerhu aderhere, yi wajiraga ebyo bintu
ACT 15:18 biyinjikeene gurhengera miira.›
ACT 15:19 Cho girhumire, nyoono, mbwene oku rhurhalibuzaga abarhali Bayaahudi bali bayemeera Nnamahanga.
ACT 15:20 Aliko, rhubayandikire oku barhalyaaga ebiryo byarhuulirwaga emaana, banachilange n'obuhushi. Barhanalemaga baalya enyama zakanulwaga changwa omulegano.
ACT 15:21 Bulaala gurhengera miira, eRhegeko lya Muusa linayigirizwa omu ngasi gishagala, linasomwa omu masinagoogi m'aBayaahudi ngasi lusiku lw'eSaabato.»
ACT 15:22 Enyuma z'aho, eNtumwa, abashamuka n'echigusho chooshi ch'abemeezi ch'eYerusaleema, babona oku bakwaneene bachishoge ahagarhi kaabo bantu baguma, banabarhume eAntiyokiya haguma na Paawulo na Baranaaba. Baava bagishoga Yuuda oyirikwa kandi Barisaba na Siila. Abo bantu oku bali babiri balikengerwe bweneene embere z'abaabo bemeezi.
ACT 15:23 Babarhuma n'amaruba maliyandikirwe mo ntya: «Rhwabo, eNtumwa n'abashamuka b'echigusho ch'abemeezi, rhwabo benyu bemeezi, rhwabalamwise mwabo bemeezi murhali Bayaahudi muli omu gishagala ch'eAntiyokiya, n'omu gihugo ch'eSuriya na ech'eKilikiya.
ACT 15:24 Rhwayunviirhe oku bantu baguma barhengeraga eno mwerhu, bababwirire emyaazi y'okubalibuza n'okubahahaaza emirhima. Aliko rhurhabarhumaga.
ACT 15:25 Boboola, oku rhuli rhweshi haguma, rhwayunvikeene gugishoga bantu baguma, rhwamabarhuma emwenyu, bayinje haguma n'abazigirwa beerhu Baranaaba na Paawulo.
ACT 15:26 Abo bombi, bayemereere guhaana akalamo kaabo omu gukolera Nnaweerhu Yeesu Krisitu.
ACT 15:27 Ntyo ku rhwamabarhumira Yuuda na Siila. Nabo, bababwira buunu oku bwindi ebinwa rhubayandikiire.
ACT 15:28 Kandi, kuli kwinja emwa Muuka-Mutagatiifu n'emwerhu ogurhabahekesa ogwindi muzigo kuleka ebiri by'akamaro:
ACT 15:29 murhalyaaga enyama barhuuliraga emaana n'omulegano changwa enyama zakanulwaga, munachilange n'obuhushi. Mugachilanga kw'ebi, mwaba mwajirire bwinja. Buchaage!»
ACT 15:30 Bamalire guseezerana, abo barhumagwa bagenda n'okuyandagalira eAntiyokiya. Bagerere eyo, bagusha abemeezi booshi, banabahereza amo maruba.
ACT 15:31 Nabo, babeere bamamasoma, basiima elugulu w'ebinwa by'okubaseeza omurhima byabaaga biyandikirwe mo.
ACT 15:32 Gukulikirana n'oku Yuuda na Siila baliiri baleebi, babwira abaabo bemeezi binwa binene by'okubaseeza omurhima n'okubakomeza.
ACT 15:33 Babeere bamamala yo siku, abemeezi babaseezera, banababwira bagaluke n'obuholo yi bashigaane ababarhumaga.
ACT 15:34 [Aliko Siila yeewe abona bwinja ayoorhe eyo munda.]
ACT 15:35 Paawulo na Baranaaba nabo bayoorha eyo Antiyokiya. Boowe haguma n'abandi bantu banene, baalema bayigiriza n'okuyamagaza oMwazi Mwinja guyerekeere Nnaweerhu.
ACT 15:36 Enyuma w'esiku zigeeke, Paawulo abwira Baranaaba ntya: «Rhugaluke rhuje kulola beene beerhu bemeezi omu bishagala byooshi rhwayigirizaga m'oMwazi gwa Nnaweerhu, rhumenye gurhe yi baalama.»
ACT 15:37 Baranaaba alishondere Yohaana oyirikwa Mariko agende haguma nabo.
ACT 15:38 Aliko Paawulo abona oku birhakwiriire, kwenge Mariko abaaga abalekere omu gihugo ch'ePamfiliya, analilahiire kugendekeza gukola haguma nabo.
ACT 15:39 Haja haahulukira obuhaka bunene bwarhuma balekana. Baranaaba agenda aherekezwe na Mariko, baja omu chombo, bayambukira oku chizimba ch'eGipuro.
ACT 15:40 Paawulo achishoga Siila. Abemeezi bamalire kumuhemera olukogo lwa Nnaweerhu, agenda.
ACT 15:41 Agerera omu gihugo ch'eSuriya n'eche Kilikiya ey'ali akomeza ebigusho by'abemeezi.
ACT 16:1 Paawulo ahika omu gishagala ch'eDerebe n'eche Lisitira. Eyo munda yaliiri omwemeezi muguma oyirikwa Timoteyo. Nyina aliiri Muyaahudi-kazi oyemeerere Yeesu, n'eshe aliiri Mugiriki.
ACT 16:2 Abemeezi b'egishala ch'eLisitira n'eche Ikoniyo baliiri bahamiiriza bwinja oyo Timoteyo.
ACT 16:3 Paawulo alishondere Timoteyo amuherekeze. Aliko, aBayaahudi balilamire eyo munda, booshi baliyinji okw'eshe aliiri Mugiriki. Charhuma Paawulo amukembuula yi bamuyemeera.
ACT 16:4 Omu bishagala baliiri balenga mo, baalema baabalira abemeezi amarhegeko eNtumwa n'abashamuka b'echigusho ch'abemeezi b'eYerusaleema bahaaga bo n'okubahema bamakulikire.
ACT 16:5 Na ntyo, ebigusho by'abemeezi byakomera omu bwemeezi n'oluganjo lw'abemeezi lwagendekera kuyuushuka ngasi lusiku.
ACT 16:6 Paawulo n'abalimuherekeeze baagera omu gihugo ch'eFurigiya na ech'eGalatiya bulaala Muuka-Mutagatiifu alibabuzize kubala eChinwa cha Nnamahanga omu gihugo ch'eAziya.
ACT 16:7 Babeere baahika hoofu n'egihugo ch'eMisiya bahiga kuja omu gihugo ch'eBitiniya, aliko Muuka gwa Yeesu arhabayemeereraga.
ACT 16:8 Baaja baagera eburhambi bw'eMisiya, bayandagalira omu gishagala ch'eTorowa.
ACT 16:9 Omu budufu, Paawulo abonekerwa. Abona mulume muguma w'eMakedoniya waliyimangire embere zage, amuyinginga ntya: «Oyambukire eMakedoniya, oyinje orhurhabaale.»
ACT 16:10 Ho n'aho, enyuma z'okoola kubonekerwa, rhwachirheganya kuja eMakedoniya, bulaala rhwalibwene oku Nnamahanga arhuhamageere kubala eyoola munda oMwazi Mwinja.
ACT 16:11 Gurhenga eTorowa rhwabalama n'echombo, rhwabera omuhengere kuja eSamotirake. Olusiku lwakulikiraga, rhwahika eNeyapoli.
ACT 16:12 Rhwarhenga eNeyapoli, rhwahika eFiripi, gishagala gikulu ch'egihugo ch'eMakedoniya. Echo gishagala chaliiri omu buja bw'aBarooma. Rhwabeera mo siku zigeeke.
ACT 16:13 Olusiku lw'eSaabato, rhwarhenga mw'echo gishagala, rhwaja hoofu n'olwinji, bulaala rhwalikengerere oku ho hantu hajirirwa amasaala. Rhwabere rhwahika, rhwayikala n'ogushambala n'abakazi baliiri bachigushire ho.
ACT 16:14 Muguma mubo, oyirikwa Ludiya, aliiri murhimbuuzi w'ebiraka bidukula by'agachiiro. Aliiri w'egishagala ch'eTuwatera, analemaga aharamya Nnamahanga. Aliiri ayunviriza, na Nnaweerhu amuheereza omurhima g'ogukulikira oMwazi Mwinja Paawulo aliiri aderha.
ACT 16:15 Ludiya abeere amabatiizwa haguma n'abantu bw'omu mwage, arhulaalika omu kuderha ntya: «Akaba mubwene oku nyemereere Nnaweerhu, muyinje emwani munahande yo.» Arhuseeza rhuyemeere.
ACT 16:16 Lusiku luguma, rhwabeere rhulirhwaja ahantu ha masaala, rhwabugaanana n'omukozi w'omunyere. Oyo mukozi aligwerhe omuzimu w'obulaguzi. N'elugulu w'oboola bulaguzi alemaga achiza bannahamwabo.
ACT 16:17 Arhukulikira, rhwabo na Paawulo. Aliiri ayamuuza ntya: «Aba bantu bali baja ba Nnamahanga w'Elugulu Bweneene. Bali babashambaalira enjira y'obuchunguke.»
ACT 16:18 Alema ajira ntyo siku zinene. Paawulo agwarha oburhe elugulu waage, ahindamuka n'okubwira oyo muzimu ntya: «Ngurhegekere oku ziino lya Yeesu Krisitu, orhenge mw'oyu munyere!» Ho n'aho oyo muzimu amurhenga mo.
ACT 16:19 Bannahamwabo oyo mukozi w'omunyere babeere baabona okw'obulangaalire b'obuchire bwamahwa oku ye, bafarha Paawulo na Siila, babakululira omu kabuga embere z'abarhegesi b'egishagala.
ACT 16:20 Babeere bahisa bo embere z'abo barhegesi, baderha ntya: «Aba bantu bali Bayaahudi, yi bararusa abantu omu gishagala cheerhu.
ACT 16:21 Yi bayigiriza emicho rhwe Barooma rhulahiizwe kuyemeera changwa gukulikira.»
ACT 16:22 Echigusho ch'abantu nacho chagwira oku bo. Abazuuzi b'egishagala barhegeka oku babakuule emyambalo n'okubashurha enkoni.
ACT 16:23 Enyuma z'okubashuurha bweneene, babahira omu munyororo n'ogurhegeka okw'omulanzi abalange bwinja.
ACT 16:24 Babeere bamamurhegeka ntyo, oyo mulanzi abahira omu busiika b'omunyororo n'ogushwekera amagulu maabo oku bihirho by'emirhi.
ACT 16:25 Ahagarhi kw'obudufu, Paawulo na Siila baliiri basaliira n'okuyimpa enyimpo z'obukuuze emwa Nnamahanga. N'abandi balishwekerwe baliiri babayunva.
ACT 16:26 Ho n'aho haaba omusisi gunene, gwadirhimanya enkingi z'omunyororo. Emilyango yooshi yava yagichinguula n'amalegule mooshi maliiri mabashwekere magishwekuula.
